### [1] [Spectral theory for population density dynamics of spiking neurons with refractoriness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20699)
*Luca Falorsi,Gianni Valerio Vinci.,Maurizio Mattia*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文通过构建包含绝对不应期（absolute refractory period）的算子理论框架，严格求解了脉冲神经元群体密度方法中的福克-普朗克算子（Fokker-Planck operator）谱问题，导出了精确传递函数（transfer function），并证明不应期可促进交互神经元群体中极限环（limit cycles）的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知绝对不应期对非线性传递函数和网络稳定性有显著影响，但将其纳入脉冲神经元（spiking neurons）群体密度方法（population density approach）仍是一个未解决的理论问题。

Method: 通过扩展状态空间以包含不应期历史，将问题表述为福克-普朗克算子的非自伴边界特征值问题（non-self-adjoint boundary eigenvalue problem）；在此基础上得到生成元的完整谱刻画（spectral characterization），证明耗散性（dissipativity）和压缩半群（contraction semigroup）的存在性，并识别出缺陷特征值（defective eigenvalues）作为例外点（exceptional points）。

Result: 在微扰理论框架下推导出考虑边界条件调制的精确传递函数，修正了先前的启发式推导并揭示了额外的阈值-噪声贡献（threshold-noise contributions）。在平均场近似（mean-field approximation）下，进一步证明不应期可以促进耦合神经元群体中极限环的产生，即发放率（firing rate）的稳定振荡。

Conclusion: 这些结果为计算神经科学（computational neuroscience）中的谱分解方法（spectral decomposition methods）提供了严格的数学基础，并为进一步的严谨数学分析开辟了路径。

Abstract: Incorporating an absolute refractory period into the population density approach for spiking neurons remains an open problem, despite evidence that refractoriness can strongly affect nonlinear transfer functions and network stability. We develop a rigorous operator-theoretic framework for neuronal population dynamics with a finite refractory time by augmenting the state space to include refractory history and formulating the problem as a non-self-adjoint boundary eigenvalue problem for the Fokker-Planck operator. This yields a complete spectral characterization of the generator, proves dissipativity and the existence of a contraction semigroup, and identifies defective eigenvalues as exceptional points where oscillatory modes emerge from coalescing relaxational modes. Within the framework of linear response theory, we also derive an exact transfer function that accounts for boundary conditions modulated by external input, correcting previous heuristic derivations and revealing additional threshold-noise contributions. Using this transfer function under a mean-field approximation, we further show that refractoriness in populations of interacting neurons can facilitate the onset of limit cycles, that is, stable oscillations in the firing rate. These results provide a rigorous foundation for spectral decomposition methods in computational neuroscience, opening the way to their further rigorous mathematical analysis.

</details>


<div id='cond-mat.mes-hall'></div>

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Ideal Bands in Tight-Binding Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20624)
*Lexu Zhao,Yang Ge,Shinsei Ryu,Jiabin Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了有限能带紧束缚模型中理想能带（ideal band）的存在性条件，指出当Dirichlet泛函达到拓扑下界时能带即为理想能带。作者首先给出了陈数为1的孤立Chern-ideal带在指数衰减跳迁模型中的解析构造；随后证明在有限范围跳迁（finite-range hopping）模型中，不存在非零陈数的孤立Chern-ideal带；最后将这些结论推广到总陈数为零的Wilson-loop-ideal带（如Kane-Mele Z₂-ideal带）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理想能带在拓扑物质理论中具有重要意义，之前的研究主要针对陈数绝对值大于1的情形，而对陈数绝对值为1以及有限范围跳迁下的存在性问题尚不清楚。本文旨在填补这一空白，并系统考察有限能带模型中理想能带的存在性条件及其与跳迁范围、轨道位置的关系。

Method: 采用解析构造方法，基于紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）和二维晶格平移对称性（two-dimensional lattice translation symmetries），在Brillouin区（Brillouin zone）中分析Berry曲率（Berry curvature）的行为。通过区分轨道嵌入位置（embedded orbital positions）是否模晶格矢量不同，分别处理指数衰减跳迁和有限范围跳迁的情形，并将结论推广至Wilson-loop-ideal带。

Result: 1. 在指数衰减跳迁的有限能带模型中，当至少两个轨道具有不同的嵌入位置（模晶格矢量）时，可以构造出陈数绝对值为1的孤立Chern-ideal带。2. 在有限范围跳迁的有限能带模型中，无论轨道嵌入位置如何，均不存在非零陈数的孤立Chern-ideal带；即使存在孤立能带接触点（band touching points），只要Berry曲率在Brillouin区中不发散，该结论仍然成立。3. 上述结论可推广至总陈数为零的Wilson-loop-ideal带，包括Kane-Mele Z₂-ideal带。

Conclusion: 理想能带的存在性强烈依赖于跳迁范围（hopping range）和轨道嵌入位置：指数衰减跳迁允许陈数为1的孤立Chern-ideal带存在，但有限范围跳迁完全禁止非零陈数的孤立Chern-ideal带。这些结论还统一了Chern-ideal带与Wilson-loop-ideal带（如Z₂-ideal带）的行为，为拓扑能带理论（topological band theory）中理想能带的分类提供了重要约束。

Abstract: A band is called ideal when its Dirichlet functional saturates the topological lower bound. We study ideal bands in finite-band tight-binding models with conventional two-dimensional lattice translation symmetries, allowing the bands to have non-flat dispersion. We first provide an analytic construction of isolated Chern-ideal bands with Chern number $|\mathrm{Ch}|=1$ in finite-band models with exponentially decaying hopping. This construction applies only when at least two orbitals have different embedded positions (modulo lattice vectors), complementing the previously known construction for $|\mathrm{Ch}|>1$. We then show that isolated Chern-ideal bands with any nonzero Chern number cannot exist in finite-band models with finite-range hopping, regardless of the embedded orbital positions. The conclusion holds even if there are isolated band touching points, as long as the Berry curvature does not diverge anywhere in the Brillouin zone. We finally generalize the conclusions to Wilson-loop-ideal bands with zero total Chern number, such as Kane-Mele $\mathbb{Z}_2$-ideal bands.

</details>


### [3] [High Order Geometric Channels for Nonlinear Transport in Bloch Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20702)
*Sami Farrag,Eugene Mele,Tony Low*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种基于带间贝里联络（interband Berry connection）的布洛赫态（Bloch states）几何微扰理论，以规范不变的Bargmann迹（gauge-invariant Bargmann trace）构建了从量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）开始的逐级 dressing 色散与联络层级 \(Q^{(N)}\)，并揭示了高阶多带几何效应与响应中的纯几何扇区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论对布洛赫态的几何效应（如量子度规与贝里曲率）已有认识，但缺乏一套系统框架来处理通过带间贝里联络耦合的微扰，特别是如何将多带几何（multiband geometry）的高阶修正纳入统一的规范不变微扰论中。

Method: 引入规范不变的Bargmann迹作为核心构造，逐阶构建dressed色散与dressed联络，形成层级 \(Q^{(N)}\)，其中首项为量子几何张量；通过 connected amplitudes 控制顶点阶修正，strict-order 修正则约化为 disconnected 乘积。

Result: 在均匀电场情形下，推导出三阶响应（third-order response）中完全相干的纯几何扇区（purely geometric sector）。高阶层级 \(Q^{(N)}\) 编码了超出量子度规（quantum metric）和贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的多带几何信息。

Conclusion: 该几何微扰理论为系统研究布洛赫态中由带间贝里联络引发的各级几何效应提供了统一框架，并揭示了高阶非线性响应中纯几何贡献的存在与结构。

Abstract: We develop a geometric perturbation theory of Bloch states for perturbations coupling via the interband Berry connection. The gauge-invariant Bargmann trace builds the dressed dispersion and connection order by order as a hierarchy \(Q^{(N)}\), starting with the quantum geometric tensor. Higher members encode multiband geometry beyond the quantum metric and Berry curvature. Connected amplitudes control vertex-order corrections, while strict-order corrections reduce to disconnected products. For a uniform electric field we find the fully coherent, purely geometric sector of the third-order response.

</details>


### [4] [Exceptional Points in a Parallel Double-Quantum-Dot Josephson Junction Coupled to a Ferromagnetic Reservoir](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20856)
*Yiyan Wang,Ruixin Zhou,Bing Dong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究平行双量子点约瑟夫森结（parallel double-quantum-dot Josephson junction）与耗散库耦合系统中的奇异点（exceptional points, EPs），发现自旋相关耗散与磁通调控可产生并操控稳定的高阶奇异点，且约瑟夫森电流在奇异点处保持连续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索耗散超导纳米结构中奇异点的存在条件与调控机制，特别是有限超导能隙（superconducting gap）对奇异点的影响，以及如何通过自旋选择耗散和磁通干涉实现稳健的非厄米奇异性（non-Hermitian singularities）。

Method: 通过积分掉电极（leads）获得非厄米博戈留波夫-德热纳（non-Hermitian Bogoliubov-de Gennes）描述，其中超导相位差与轨道通量（orbital flux）共同决定复数安德烈夫谱（complex Andreev spectrum）。采用多体宇称分析（many-body parity analysis）建立有限能隙行为与奇偶宇称能谱之间的联系。利用自由能导数与替代模型密度矩阵（surrogate-model density matrix）计算约瑟夫森电流。

Result: 自旋无关耗散下，无限超导能隙极限中存在的二阶奇异点在计入有限超导能隙后被消除；而来自铁磁库的自旋相关耗散结合磁通可产生在有限能隙超导电极中存在的二阶奇异点；磁通调控可使两个二阶奇异点融合为一个三阶奇异点（third-order EP），其特征值分裂呈现立方根标度行为；在奇异点处，约瑟夫森电流保持连续。

Conclusion: 自旋选择耗散与干涉磁通可作为超导纳米结构中稳健非厄米奇异点的有效控制参数，为利用耗散调控超导量子器件中的非厄米物理提供新途径。

Abstract: We investigate exceptional points (EPs) in a parallel double-quantum-dot Josephson junction coupled to a dissipative reservoir. By integrating out the leads, we obtain a non-Hermitian Bogoliubov-de Gennes description wherein the superconducting phase difference and orbital flux govern the complex Andreev spectrum. For spin-independent dissipation, the second-order EPs identified within the infinite superconducting gap limit are eliminated when the finite superconducting gap is properly incorporated. In contrast, spin-dependent dissipation originating from a ferromagnetic reservoir, in conjunction with magnetic flux, gives rise to second-order EPs that persist in superconducting leads with finite gap. Moreover, flux tuning enables the coalescence of two second-order EPs into a third-order EP, whose eigenvalue splitting exhibits cubic-root scaling behavior. A many-body parity analysis establishes the connection between the contrasting finite-gap behavior and the spectral relationship between the even- and odd-parity sectors. Finally, Josephson currents calculated from both the free-energy derivative and the surrogate-model density matrix demonstrate consistency and remain continuous across the EPs. These findings establish spin-selective dissipation and interferometric flux as effective control parameters for robust non-Hermitian singularities in superconducting nanostructures.

</details>


### [5] [Machine Learning for Charge State Characterization of Isolated Double Quantum Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20871)
*Hyma Vallabhapurapu,Marco Candido,Krishna Choudhary,Paul Steinacker,Ensar Vahapoglu,Chris Escott,Wee Han Lim,Andre Saraiva,Nard Dumoulin Stuyck,MengKe Feng*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出两个轻量级卷积神经网络（CNN），总参数量低于100万，用于自动分析半导体量子点阵列的电荷稳定性图谱（CSM），在隔离模式（isolated-mode）下实现了电荷不稳定性检测（94%宏观平均准确率）和电荷转变线定位与电子占据数确定（95.3%精确线计数准确率），模型总占用6.5 MB，推理时间低于60 ms，为量子点器件的自动化调优提供了实用路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体量子点阵列向容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computing）扩展需要高效的自旋量子比特（spin qubit）调优，而这一过程依赖对电荷稳定性图谱（charge stability maps, CSMs）的分析，且目前仍主要依赖人工操作。尽管机器学习已广泛应用于储层耦合器件的CSM分析，但在日益重要的隔离模式（isolated-mode）器件中，自动化调优研究仍然有限。

Method: 提出了两个参数少于100万的卷积神经网络（convolutional neural networks, CNNs）：CSMClassifier用于识别电荷不稳定性和传感器伪影，ChargeLineNet用于定位电荷转变线并确定电子占据数。模型在从32个硅金属-氧化物-半导体（SiMOS）双量子点器件收集的CSM数据上训练，其中16个器件用于训练，16个用于跨器件泛化测试，并辅以合成图像预训练提升标签效率。

Result: CSMClassifier在2,407张保留图像上实现了94%的宏观平均准确率（三类质量分类）；ChargeLineNet在1,131张保留图像上达到95.3%的精确线计数准确率。组合管线对干净保留图像的电子占据数判断准确率为93.8%。两个模型总占用6.5 MB，在标准实验室硬件上推理时间低于60 ms。使用合成图像预训练后，在有限实验数据上微调仍能保持90%以上准确率，而从头训练则显著下降。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了在隔离模式量子点器件中，通过轻量级CNN模型实现自动化CSM分析的有效性和实用性。模型兼具高准确率、小内存占用和快速推理能力，为可扩展的量子点器件自动化表征与调优提供了一条可行的实践路径。

Abstract: Scaling semiconductor quantum dot arrays toward fault-tolerant quantum computing requires efficient tuneup of spin qubits, a process that depends on the analysis of charge stability maps (CSMs) and remains largely manual. While machine learning has been widely applied to CSM analysis in reservoir-coupled devices, automated tuning in the increasingly important isolated-mode regime has received limited attention. In isolated-mode CSMs, charge transitions appear as near-vertical lines, making them well suited to compact, task-specific models. We present two convolutional neural networks with fewer than one million parameters, trained on CSMs collected from 32 silicon metal-oxide-semiconductor (SiMOS) double-quantum-dot devices measured at approximately 1 K using an automated cryogenic probing system. Sixteen devices were used for training and sixteen were held out to evaluate cross-device generalization against hand-labeled ground truth. CSMClassifier identifies charge instability and sensor artifacts, achieving 94% macro-averaged accuracy across three quality classes on 2,407 held-out images. ChargeLineNet localizes charge-transition lines and determines electron occupancy, achieving 95.3% exact line-count accuracy on 1,131 held-out images. Combined into a single pipeline, the models correctly determine electron occupancy for 93.8% of clean held-out images. Pre-training on synthetic images substantially improves label efficiency. Fine-tuning the pre-trained model on limited experimental data maintains over 90% accuracy, whereas training from scratch degrades significantly under the same conditions. Together, the two models occupy only 6.5 MB and process images in less than 60 ms on standard laboratory hardware, demonstrating a practical path toward scalable, automated characterization and tuneup of quantum-dot devices.

</details>


### [6] [End-State-Controlled Quantum Transport in Armchair Graphene Nanoribbon Artificial Quantum Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21141)
*David M T Kuo*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个实空间理论框架，阐明三角烯（triangulene）与扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带（AGNR）构成的三叉接口中局域态的形成机制，推导出节点轨道数量与手性的普适关系，并展示这些轨道可用于构造具有可调平带的人工石墨烯纳米带。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于原子级精确石墨烯纳米结构的人工量子材料为探索局域电子态引发的量子现象提供了理想平台，但接口态（interface states）的微观起源尚不清晰。

Method: 发展了一个实空间（real-space）理论框架，通过连续调节石墨烯构筑单元之间的耦合，追踪三角烯的零能模（zero-energy modes）和AGNR端态（end states）如何演化为三叉接口处的紧致局域节点轨道（compact localized node orbitals）。并引入扩展安德森模型（extended Anderson model）定量复现隧道谱。

Result: 推导出节点轨道数量和手性满足普适关系$N_{node,\delta}=|N_{es,t,A(B)}-N_{tri,0,B(A)}|$；当AGNR端态数量占优时节点轨道继承其子格手性（sublattice chirality），反之则继承三角烯零能模的手性。这些节点轨道可作为基本构筑单元，构造在费米能附近具有高度可调平带（flat subbands）的人造石墨烯纳米带。

Conclusion: 该实空间图像超越了传统的体拓扑描述，提供了对紧致局域态（CLS）形成的透明理解。所得平带具有可控简并度和强各向异性量子输运特性，为设计新型人工量子材料奠定了基础。

Abstract: Artificial quantum materials based on atomically precise graphene nanostructures provide an ideal platform for exploring quantum phenomena arising from localized electronic states. Here, we develop a real-space theoretical framework to elucidate the microscopic origin of interface states in graphene architectures composed of $n$-triangulenes and armchair graphene nanoribbons (AGNRs). By continuously tuning the coupling between graphene building blocks, we reveal the evolution of triangulene zero-energy modes and AGNR end states into compact localized node orbitals at three-arm junctions. The number and chirality of these node orbitals obey a universal relation, $N_{node,δ}=|N_{es,t,A(B)}-N_{tri,0,B(A)}|$, where $N_{es,t}$ denotes the total number of AGNR end states contributed by the three AGNR arms at the junction, and $N_{tri,0}$ is the number of zero-energy modes of the attached triangulene. The chirality of the node orbitals is determined by the dominant constituent: when $N_{es,t}>N_{tri,0}$, they inherit the sublattice chirality of the AGNR end states ($δ=A(B)$), whereas for $N_{tri,0}>N_{es,t}$ they inherit that of the triangulene zero-energy modes ($δ=B(A)$). This real-space picture provides a transparent understanding of compact localized state (CLS) formation beyond conventional bulk topological descriptions. Using experimentally synthesized triangulene nanographenes as representative examples, we further explain the emergence of their zero-energy modes and quantitatively reproduce their tunneling spectra within an extended Anderson model. Finally, we demonstrate that these node orbitals can serve as elementary building blocks for constructing artificial graphene nanoribbons with highly tunable flat subbands near the Fermi energy. The resulting CLSs exhibit controllable degeneracy and strongly anisotropic quantum transport.

</details>


### [7] [Exceptional-Point Geometry of Weak Topological Boundary States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21148)
*Rafael A. Molina,Kevin González,Pedro A. Orellana*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个复动量空间几何框架，将弱拓扑（weak topology）的体—边对应关系统一描述为解析延拓布洛赫哈密顿量（Bloch Hamiltonian）中的例外奇异性（exceptional singularities），并以此统一解释了边缘态、角态和紧致局域态（compact localized states）的起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弱拓扑相（weak topological phases）的几何图像尚不清晰，缺乏一个统一的理论框架来同时描述其边缘态、角态和紧致局域态的几何起源。

Method: 通过将布洛赫哈密顿量解析延拓到复动量空间，识别其中的例外奇异性（包括例外点例外曲线），并利用二维plaquette手征模型作为最小实现，分析弱拓扑不变量与奇异性拓扑结构之间的对应关系。

Result: 弱拓扑边缘态对应复动量空间中的例外点（exceptional points），角零模对应双动量复化后的例外曲线（exceptional curves），而紧致局域态在例外根塌缩至原点时出现。

Conclusion: 该框架为边缘态、角态和紧致局域态提供了一种统一的复动量描述，揭示了弱拓扑的几何本质在于解析延拓哈密顿量的例外奇异性结构。

Abstract: In this article, we demonstrate that weak topology can be formulated geometrically in terms of exceptional singularities of an analytically continued Bloch Hamiltonian. A general plaquette chiral model in two dimensions serves as a minimal realization of dual weak topology, possessing two independent families of weak topological invariants, one for each spatial direction. The weak-topological edge states correspond to exceptional points in complex momentum space, while corner zero modes emerge from exceptional curves obtained by complexifying both momenta. Compact localized states arise when the exceptional roots collapse to the origin. This framework provides a unified complex-momentum description of edge, corner, and compact localization.

</details>


### [8] [Emergent ferromagnetism in the NiI$_2$-NbSe$_2$ van der Waals heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21218)
*Büşra Gamze Arslan,Mohammad Amini,Ziying Wang,Alessandro Orsini,Jose L. Lado,Adolfo O. Fumega,Robert Drost,Peter Liljeroth*

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明，单层多铁性材料NiI₂在邻近超导衬底NbSe₂时，其磁基态从非共线自旋结构转变为铁磁态，并利用超导能隙内的Yu-Shiba-Rusinov（YSR）态作为原位探针来表征这一磁性转变，展示了衬底工程对原子级薄层材料磁有序的调控能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管理论预测单层多铁性材料（monolayer multiferroics）的性质可通过应变、门电压或邻近效应进行调控，但实验上对这类调控的直接展示仍然非常匮乏。因此，本研究旨在通过实验手段验证衬底邻近效应对单层多铁性材料磁基态的影响。

Method: 作者选择单层NiI₂（一种典型的二维多铁性材料）并将其置于超导NbSe₂衬底上，利用低温扫描隧道显微镜（STM）和扫描隧道谱（STS）探测NiI₂的磁基态变化，同时通过观测超导能隙内的Yu-Shiba-Rusinov（YSR）态来表征磁性转变。

Result: 实验表明，金属性衬底NbSe₂通过重新归一化（renormalize）NiI₂内部的交换相互作用（exchange interactions），将其驱动至铁磁（ferromagnetic）基态。这一转变可通过超导能隙内的YSR态进行可视化观测。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了YSR态作为二维磁性原位探针（in situ probe）的有效性，并证明衬底工程（substrate engineering）可作为一种控制原子级薄层材料中磁有序的手段。

Abstract: Multiferroicity arising from non-collinear spin textures and strong spin-orbit interactions offers a route to magnetoelectric functionality in the monolayer limit. Although theory predicts that the properties of monolayer multiferroics can be tuned by strain, gating, or proximity effects, experimental demonstrations of such control remain scarce. Here we show that the magnetic ground state of monolayer NiI$_2$, a prototypical two-dimensional multiferroic, is altered by proximity to a superconducting NbSe$_2$ substrate. Using low-temperature scanning tunnelling microscopy (STM) and spectroscopy (STS), we show that the metallic substrate renormalizes the exchange interactions within NiI$_2$ and drives it into a ferromagnetic ground state. This can be visualized by probing the Yu-Shiba-Rusinov (YSR) states within the superconducting gap of the NbSe$_2$ substrate. Our results establish YSR states as an in situ probe of two-dimensional magnetism and demonstrate substrate engineering as a means of controlling magnetic order in atomically thin materials.

### [9] [Circular phonon dichroism in $d$-wave altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21221)
*Ding Li,Tao Qin,Jianhui Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出有限动量圆声子二色性（finite-momentum circular phonon dichroism）作为直接探测二维 d 波交变磁体（d-wave altermagnet）内奈尔矢量（Néel vector）的实验手段，通过 Onsager 互易关系与 C₂z 晶格对称性分析发现该二色信号在翻转奈尔矢量时符号反转，且典型动量截面下二色不对称比率可达 37.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁体（altermagnet）作为一种新型共线反铁磁体，具有动量依赖的自旋分裂，在反铁磁自旋电子学（antiferromagnetic spintronics）中有显著优势，但其磁序本质上难以读出，阻碍了实际应用。本文旨在解决这一读出示踪难题。

Method: 作者将 Onsager 互易关系（Onsager reciprocity）与 C₂z 晶格对称性（C₂z lattice symmetry）相结合，推导出有限动量圆声子二色性信号在面内声子波矢（in-plane phonon wave vector）下随奈尔矢量翻转而符号反转的规律；并通过通道分辨分解（channel-resolved decomposition）揭示该二色性源于带间相干跃迁（interband coherent transitions）。

Result: 典型有限动量截面下，圆声子二色性不对称比率可达 |η_CPD| = 37.3%，表明信号强度显著且可观测。

Conclusion: 该工作表明圆超声吸收（circular-ultrasound absorption）可作为直接探测 d 波交变磁体中奈尔矢量的有效探针。

Abstract: Altermagnets, a new class of collinear antiferromagnets, exhibit momentum-dependent spin splitting and offer compelling advantages for antiferromagnetic spintronics. However, the magnetic order is intrinsically difficult to read out, which hinders practical applications. We propose finite-momentum circular phonon dichroism as a direct probe of Néel vector in two-dimensional $d$-wave altermagnets. Combining Onsager reciprocity with $C_{2z}$ lattice symmetry, we find that the dichroic signal reverses sign when the Néel vector is flipped for the in-plane phonon wave vectors. Moreover, a channel-resolved decomposition identifies the circular phonon dichroism originates from the interband coherent transitions. Representative finite-momentum cuts show pronounced dichroic asymmetric ratio, with $|η_{\mathrm{CPD}}|=37.3\%$. Our work reveals that the circular-ultrasound absorption acts as a direct probe of the Néel vector of $d$-wave altermagnets.

### [10] [Direct Measurement of Exciton Dispersion in the Long-Wavelength Limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21234)
*Peiyi He,Jiade Li,Jiakai Wang,Jiangxu Li,Jiahao Wang,Weiyu Sun,Yiwen Song,Xiaoyue Gao,Quanlin Guo,Bo Han,Ruochen Shi,Niklas Dellby,Tracy Lovejoy,Xing-Qiu Chen,Kaihui Liu,Yu Ye,Hailin Peng,Peng Gao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究利用离焦工程动量分辨电子能量损失谱（defocus-engineered momentum-resolved EELS）在扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM）中实现了超高动量分辨率（0.0002 Å⁻¹），以自由悬挂的六方氮化硼（hBN）为原型体系，系统表征了层数依赖的激子色散（exciton dispersion）及其从单层到体材料的维度演化，揭示了非解析线性色散区的压缩和群速度的增长，并进一步探索了单层hBN激子能带结构对环境因素的响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在二维体系中，弱介电屏蔽和长程电子-空穴交换相互作用被预测会在长波长极限下诱导非解析激子色散，但尤其是在超低波数（q < 0.02 Å⁻¹）区间，对其维度演化的直接定量表征仍然缺乏。

Method: 采用离焦工程动量分辨电子能量损失谱（defocus-engineered momentum-resolved EELS）结合扫描透射电子显微镜（STEM），实现了0.0002 Å⁻¹的超高动量分辨率，以自由悬挂的hBN薄膜为原型样品进行测量。

Result: 随着层数从单层增加到25层，特征交叉动量（crossover momentum）q_c从1.82×10⁻¹ Å⁻¹增加到3.0×10⁻¹ Å⁻¹，非解析线性色散区被逐步压缩；低波数群速度（group velocity）从2.0×10⁻³ c增加到2.9×10⁻² c，最终色散趋近于体材料类抛物线极限。此外，还考察了温度、邻近石墨烯层及BN/石墨烯异质结中层间转角对单层hBN激子能带结构的影响。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了低维激子的基本物理机制，为调控层状量子材料中的激子输运、扩散和准粒子耦合提供了有价值的指导，并建立了一种探索低维激子物理学的强大实验途径。

Abstract: Exciton dispersion, which governs the propagation, scattering and radiative decay of electron-hole pairs, is essential to optoelectronics and quantum materials. In two-dimensional systems, weakened dielectric screening and long-range electron-hole exchange are predicted to induce nonanalytic exciton dispersion in the long-wavelength limit. However, direct quantitative characterization of its dimensional evolution remains lacking, especially in the ultralow-q regime (q < 0.02 $Å^{-1}$). Here we employ defocus-engineered momentum-resolved electron energy-loss spectroscopy in scanning transmission electron microscopy, achieving an ultrahigh momentum resolution of 0.0002 $Å^{-1}$. Using freestanding hBN as a prototypical platform, we resolve layer-dependent exciton dispersion and quantify its characteristic crossover momentum and group velocity in the long-wavelength limit. With increasing thickness, the nonanalytic linear-dispersion regime is progressively compressed, manifested by a reduction in characteristic crossover momentum q_c from $1.82 \times 10^{-1} Å^{-1}$ in the monolayer to $3.0 \times 10^{-1} Å^{-1}$ in 25 layers. Meanwhile, the low-q group velocity increases from $2.0 \times 10^{-3} c$ to $2.9 \times 10^{-2} c$, before the dispersion ultimately approaches the bulk-like parabolic limit. We further examine how the exciton band structure of monolayer hBN responds to its surrounding environment, including temperature, adjacent graphene layers, and interlayer twist in BN/graphene heterostructures. These findings uncover the fundamental physics of low-dimensional excitons, deliver valuable guidance for modulating exciton transport, diffusion and quasiparticle coupling in layered quantum materials, and establish a powerful experimental route to explore low-dimensional exciton physics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用扫描隧道显微镜/扫描隧道谱（STM/STS）实验探测CrSBr体材料中两种显著缺陷的结构与电子特征；并将实验数据与基于第一性原理（ab initio）模拟的STM图像进行对比分析。

Abstract: Chromium sulfur bromide (CrSBr) is a layered magnetic semiconducting material combining a rich magnetic phase diagram with axis-dependent electronic and optical properties. While defects in CrSBr have been shown to affect magnetic order and excitonic responses, their microscopic nature, atomic structure, and electronic properties are not yet fully understood. In this work, we use scanning tunneling microscopy/spectroscopy (STM/STS) to explore the structure and electronic signatures of two prominent defects in bulk CrSBr. Their structure reflects the symmetries of the underlying lattice, with electronic features near the valence band edge. By comparing experimental data with ab initio simulated STM images, we infer that a common defect corresponds to a b-axis-aligned double sulfur vacancy, in line with findings from a recent growth analysis study. This result advances our understanding of the role of intrinsic defects in shaping the electronic structure of CrSBr.

### [12] [An on-chip programmable mechano-quantum transducer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21487)
*Xinrui Zhang,Wei Liu,Duanyu Ma,Lin-Ke Xie,Nai-Jie Guo,Zhongtao Gou,Yifan Wang,Jianxin Xu,Xiaoguang Luo,Zhao Mu,Honglong Chang,Weizheng Yuan,Jian-Shun Tang,Chuan-Feng Li,Guangcan Guo,Tao Ye*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了一种片上可编程机械-量子换能器（OCPMQT），该器件在二维范德华量子缺陷宿主中集成了电压定义的微机械驱动与原位自旋频率读出，通过光探测磁共振（ODMR）谱学将机械编程的晶格态编码为零场分裂参数的频移，实现了紧凑芯片内机械-量子界面的定量映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有固态自旋缺陷技术中，机械驱动与量子读出在物理上相互分离，导致测量构型离散化；需要一种片上集成的机械-量子界面来编程缺陷宿主的晶格状态并将其定量映射到自旋哈密顿量上，以弥合这一功能鸿沟。

Method: 该研究通过将电压定义的微机械驱动与原位自旋频率读出集成在二维范德华量子缺陷宿主中，构建了片上可编程机械-量子换能器（OCPMQT）。机械编程的晶格状态通过轴向零场分裂参数的位移来编码，并由光探测磁共振（ODMR）谱学分辨。同时建立了一个微机械-自旋哈密顿量框架，关联片上机电学、界面应变传递与应变-自旋耦合。

Result: 在仅为2.05×10⁻² cm³的芯片体积内，该换能器可探测到低至0.0080%的ODMR推断应变，并产生约2.6×10⁴ N/m⁻³的体积力密度。通过微机械-自旋哈密顿量框架，电控微机械输入可直接作为自旋频率响应被测量。

Conclusion: 该工作实现了机械驱动与量子读出的片上集成，提供了一种紧凑、可编程的机械-量子界面，为固态自旋缺陷在量子传感领域的进一步实用化奠定了基础。

Abstract: Solid-state spin defects encode local perturbations as measurable shifts in spin-transition frequencies, but mechanical actuation and quantum readout remain physically separated, resulting in a discrete measurement setup. Integrating these functions requires an on-site mechano-quantum interface that programs the lattice state of a defect host and quantitatively maps it onto the spin Hamiltonian. Here we first report an on-chip programmable mechano-quantum transducer (OCPMQT) that integrates voltage-defined micromechanical actuation with in situ spin-frequency readout in a two-dimensional van der Waals quantum-defect host. Mechanically programmed lattice states are encoded as shifts in the axial zero-field splitting parameter and resolved by optically detected magnetic resonance (ODMR) spectroscopy. Within a chip volume of 2.05*10^-2 cm^3, the transducer accesses ODMR-inferred strains as low as 0.0080% and delivers a volumetric force density of approximately 2.6*104 N/m^-3. A micromechanical-to-spin-Hamiltonian framework links on-chip electromechanics, interfacial strain transfer, and strain-spin coupling, enabling the electrical control micromechanical input to be measured directly as spin-frequency response.

### [13] [Probing the nonlocality of Landau levels in GaAs quantum wells through modified Purcell factors, Lamb shifts and dipole emitted spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21528)
*Lara Greten,Sabrina Meyer,Christina Schröder,Andreas Knorr,Stephen Hughes*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文从微观非局域磁化率理论出发，推导了二维电子气中朗道能级系统的格林函数，并评估了超越马尔可夫和旋转波近似的近场电磁效应，发现了空间色散导致的长程非局域效应，包括局域偶极禁戒跃迁的增强，其尺度与太赫兹纳米结构实验相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维电子气在强垂直磁场中形成朗道能级（Landau levels），其最小轨道半径（磁长度）在几特斯拉下可达数十纳米，导致电磁激发具有固有的非局域响应。现有理论常采用局域近似，无法准确描述这种空间色散效应，因此需要建立微观非局域理论来揭示长程电磁相互作用机制。

Method: 基于非局域磁化率（nonlocal susceptibility）的微观理论，推导了描述所有电磁相互作用的中心量——格林函数（Green's function），并在超越马尔可夫近似（Markov approximation）和旋转波近似（rotating-wave approximation）的条件下，计算了近场偶极发射体的珀塞尔因子（Purcell factor）、兰姆移位（Lamb shift）和发射光谱。

Result: 朗道能级响应的空间色散（spatial dispersion）在数百纳米距离内产生显著的非局域效应，改变了电磁响应；特别地，近场梯度在回旋频率（cyclotron frequency）的倍数处增强了局域偶极禁戒跃迁（dipole-forbidden transitions）。这些非局域特征与近期朗道能级极化激元（Landau level polaritons）实验结果一致。

Conclusion: 非局域效应在实验相关的距离尺度上不可忽略，且所涉及的长度尺度与现代纳米结构太赫兹（terahertz）器件特征尺寸相匹配，表明该理论对于理解和设计太赫兹频段的近场光与物质相互作用具有重要意义。

Abstract: In a two-dimensional electron gas, a strong perpendicular magnetic field confines electrons to quantized cyclotron orbits, giving rise to Landau levels with discrete orbit radii. Even the smallest Landau orbit, set by the magnetic length, spans tens of nanometers for fields of a few Tesla, imposing an intrinsic nonlocal response to electromagnetic excitations. From a microscopic theory of the nonlocal susceptibility, we derive the Green's function, the central quantity governing all electromagnetic interactions, and evaluate Purcell factors, Lamb shifts, and emission spectra from a proximal dipole emitter beyond the Markov and rotating-wave approximations. Significant nonlocal effects resulting from spatial dispersion of the Landau level response modify the response for experimentally relevant situations up to distances of hundreds of nanometers and, in particular, brighten locally dipole-forbidden transitions due to near-field gradients at multiples of the cyclotron frequency. The relevant length scales are typical of state-of-the-art nanostructured terahertz architectures, and some of our nonlocal features are consistent with recent experiments using Landau level polaritons.

</details>

### [14] [Spin and momentum fraction carried by partons in the nucleon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21230)
*Constantia Alexandrou,Simone Bacchio,Jacob Finkenrath,Christos Iona,Giannis Koutsou,Christian Kummer,Yan Li,Bhavna Prasad,Gregoris Spanoudes*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本研究利用物理质量点附近的四组晶格量子色动力学（lattice QCD）系综，在连续极限下直接提取了质子的夸克和胶子动量分数与总角动量，验证了动量求和规则与自旋求和规则，并将结果与唯象学分析进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定质子的动量分数（momentum fraction）和角动量（angular momentum）在夸克与胶子之间的分配，是理解质子内部结构的关键问题。该研究旨在通过第一性原理的晶格QCD（lattice QCD）计算，直接验证动量求和规则与自旋求和规则（spin sum rule）的满足情况。

Method: 采用四组不同格点间距的晶格QCD系综（ensemble），均包含u、d、s、c四种夸克且质量调至物理值，系综具有相近的物理体积。通过外推至连续极限（continuum limit），在物理π介子质量点直接提取夸克和胶子的动量分数与总角动量，并分离内禀夸克自旋（intrinsic quark spin）和轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）对质子自旋的贡献。

Result: 质子总动量分数为⟨x_N⟩ = 0.995(60)(29），总自旋J_N = 0.507(43)(65)，表明动量求和规则与自旋求和规则均得到满足。结果与唯象学分析（phenomenological analyses）进行了比较。

Conclusion: 晶格QCD计算在物理质量点和连续极限下确认了质子动量与自旋求和规则的有效性，为理解质子内部结构提供了第一性原理的定量支持。

Abstract: We determine the momentum fraction and angular momentum carried by quarks and gluons in the proton in lattice QCD. We use four ensembles simulated with up, down, strange and charm quarks with their masses tuned to their physical values. These ensembles have similar physical volume and different lattice spacings allowing us to take the continuum limit directly at the physical pion mass point. We extract the quark and gluon momentum fractions and total angular momentum in the continuum limit as well as the intrinsic quark spin and orbital angular momentum contributions to the proton spin. We find the total momentum fraction $\langle x_N \rangle= 0.995(60)(29)$ and the total spin $J_N = 0.507(43)(65)$, showing that both the momentum and spin sum rules are satisfied. We compare our results to those extracted from phenomenological analyses.

### [15] [Stochastic Quantization as Optimal Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21436)
*Lingxiao Wang*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本文提出最优随机量子化（optimal stochastic quantization, OSQ），将随机量子化重新表述为一个有限时间随机最优控制问题，通过神经网络学习残余控制力，以控制而非平衡的方式实现量子场论的量化，并在二维标量φ⁴理论中验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统随机量子化（stochastic quantization）将Euclidean量子场论视为虚构时间Langevin动力学的平衡态，依赖长时间演化达到Gibbs测度。本文旨在将其重新表述为一个有限时间随机最优控制问题，从而避免漫长的平衡过程，并以控制力直接驱动系统到达目标测度。

Method: 方法上，将随机量子化转化为有限时间随机最优控制问题。以自由理论提供的Ornstein–Uhlenbeck过程作为可处理的参考过程（reference process），将完整的相互作用转化为参考校正的终端成本（reference-corrected terminal cost）。最优控制对应一个Doob变换（Doob transform）力，用于在指定时间和给定噪声振幅下将路径重加权（path-reweighted）终端系综导向目标分布。神经网络用于学习残余控制力，实现最优随机量子化。

Result: 在多峰势（multimodal potentials）中，有限时间内恢复了所有模式，并发现噪声振幅设定了实际的扩散-视界窗口（diffusion-horizon window）。在二维格点标量φ⁴理论中，在临界点附近恢复的观测值与混合蒙特卡洛（hybrid Monte Carlo, HMC）模拟结果一致。由于路径权重是精确的，不完美的训练只会增加估计量的方差（variance），而不会引入模型偏差（model bias）。

Conclusion: 量子化可以被表述为控制问题而非平衡过程。该方法以有限时间控制替代无限时间平衡，提供了无偏估计，并通过神经网络实现可扩展的数值方案。

Abstract: Stochastic quantization defines a Euclidean quantum field theory as the equilibrium of a fictitious-time Langevin dynamics, which reaches the Gibbs measure asymptotically. We show that this quantization can be formulated as a finite-time stochastic optimal control problem. A tractable reference process, naturally supplied by the free theory when available, provides an Ornstein--Uhlenbeck dynamics, while the full interaction enters as a reference-corrected terminal cost. The optimal control is a Doob-transform force that steers the path-reweighted terminal ensemble to the target at a prescribed time and for a given noise amplitude. A neural network learns the residual control, realizing this optimal stochastic quantization (OSQ). Because the path weights are exact, imperfect training increases the variance of estimators but does not introduce model bias. On multimodal potentials we recover all modes at finite time and find that the noise amplitude sets a practical diffusion-horizon window. In two-dimensional lattice scalar $φ^4$ theory we recover observables from hybrid Monte Carlo simulations near the critical point. Quantization is thereby formulated as control rather than equilibration.

</details>

### [16] [Determination of fundamental properties of nitrogen from first principles. III. Temperature and frequency dependence of the molecular polarizability and magnetic susceptibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21261)
*Jakub Lang,Giovanni Garberoglio,Michał Przybytek,Michał Lesiuk*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理（first-principles）计算，系统研究了氮气分子（N₂）在计量学（metrology）相关温度与频率范围内的分子极化率（molecular polarizability）和磁化率（magnetic susceptibility），结合理论结果与实验数据给出半经验估计（semi-empirical estimates），并指出磁化率方面存在显著的理论-实验差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定氮气在计量学中相关性质的精确理论值，填补静态极化率及磁化率等量尚未被实验测量的空白，并解决磁化率数据中存在的理论与实验之间的显著分歧。

Method: 采用结合多种电子结构方法（electronic structure methods）的稳健复合方案（composite scheme），在多个核间距下计算静态极化率、柯西系数（Cauchy coefficients，最高至六阶）及各向同性磁化率的纯电子贡献；温度依赖性（50 K–2000 K）通过两种独立方法评估：振转平均（rovibrational averaging）和路径积分蒙特卡洛（path integral Monte Carlo, PIMC）。

Result: 理论极化率与现有高精度测温实验一致，但精度显著较低；通过理论与实验数据结合，给出了关键参考温度下的高精度半经验静态极化率估计值（303 K时为11.735962 a.u.，273.16 K时为11.735585 a.u.），并报告了磁化率的理论值，指出顺磁贡献（paramagnetic contribution）的重要性及与实验数据的差异。

Conclusion: 理论计算本身精度不及实验，但其主要价值在于与实验结果联合，生成迄今未被测量的多种量的半经验估计；磁化率方面，理论结果突显了顺磁贡献的关键作用，并揭示了与实验数据之间的显著分歧。

Abstract: This work is the third part of the series of papers that focus on the theoretical determination of the properties of nitrogen that are relevant in metrology. Here we present first-principles calculations of the temperature and frequency dependence of the molecular polarizability and magnetic susceptibility of the nitrogen molecule (N$_2$). The purely electronic contributions to the static polarizability, Cauchy coefficients (up to sixth order), and isotropic magnetic susceptibility are computed over a range of internuclear distances using a robust composite scheme combining several electronic structure methods. The temperature dependence, evaluated from $50$~K to $2000$~K, is determined using two independent methods: rovibrational averaging and path integral Monte Carlo (PIMC). The polarizabilities obtained from theory agree with the recent high-precision thermometry measurements, wherever the latter are available, but are significantly less accurate. However, the main usefulness of the theoretical data revolves around combining it with the available experimental results to generate semi-empirical estimates of various quantities that have never been measured thus far. As an example, we determine highly accurate semi-empirical estimates of the static polarizability at key reference temperatures, $α_0(T)=11.735\,962$~a.u.\ at $T=303$~K and $α_0(T)=11.735\,585$~a.u.\ at $T=273.16$~K. Furthermore, we report theoretical values for the magnetic susceptibility, highlighting the importance of the paramagnetic contribution, and address a significant discrepancy with the experimental data for this quantity.

</details>


### [17] [Graph Neural Network Force Fields (GPTFF-mol) for Organic Molecules from Optimization Trajectories (OpenGEM26)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21369)
*Yifan Huang,Fankai Xie,Jiangnan Zheng,Tenglong Lu,Sheng Meng,Miao Liu*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文发布了包含20万独特分子与440万构象的大规模数据集OpenGEM26，并训练了基于图神经网络（GNN）的机器学习势能面GPTFF-mol，在能量预测（MAE 16 meV/分子）和受力预测上优于ANI-2x，为含硫氯有机分子提供高质量资源与稳健势能模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT）是可靠的原子级分子模拟工具，机器学习势能面（machine learning potential）则成为平衡精度与效率的有力补充。本文旨在构建一个涵盖更广构象空间的大规模数据集，并训练相应的机器学习势能模型，以改善含硫、氯有机分子的模拟能力。

Method: 构建了OpenGEM26数据集，包含20万种独特分子和440万构象，由H、C、N、O、S、Cl元素组成，最多含10个重原子。所有计算在ωB97X-D/Def2-SVP与Def2-TZVP级别进行，并计入色散校正（dispersion correction），记录完整结构优化轨迹及大量非平衡结构。基于该数据集，训练了图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）势能模型GPTFF-mol。

Result: 统计表明，OpenGEM26在能量、键长和键角方面覆盖了比QM9更广的构象空间。GPTFF-mol的能量平均绝对误差（mean absolute error, MAE）为16 meV/分子（相当于0.82 meV/原子），力预测性能优于ANI-2x。丁烷旋转与酮-烯醇互变异构测试验证了模型在畸变几何构型下能准确描述分子动力学行为和反应能垒。

Conclusion: 该工作为含硫、氯有机分子的高效模拟提供了高质量数据资源与稳健的机器学习势能面模型（ML potential）。

Abstract: Density functional theory (DFT) serves as a reliable tool for atomistic molecular simulations, while machine learning potentials have become powerful complements to balance accuracy and efficiency. In this work, we release OpenGEM26 (Open Generated Ensemble of Molecules, 2026), a large-scale dataset comprising 200,000 unique molecules and 4.4 million conformations composed of H, C, N, O, S and Cl with up to ten heavy atoms. All calculations are carried out at the ωB97X-D/Def2-SVP and Def2-TZVP levels with dispersion corrections, and complete structural optimization trajectories and abundant non-equilibrium structures are recorded. Statistical analyses confirm that this dataset covers a broader conformational space than QM9 in terms of energy, bond lengths and bond angles. A graph neural network-based potential GPTFF-mol is trained using the new dataset, achieving an energy mean absolute error of 16 meV/molecule, which is equivalent to 0.82meV/atom, and superior force prediction performance compared with ANI-2x. Validated by butane rotation and keto-enol tautomerization tests, the model accurately describes molecular dynamical behaviors and reaction barriers at distorted geometries. This work provides a high-quality resource and robust ML potential for efficient simulations of sulfur- and chlorine-containing organic molecules.

</details>

### [18] [The Well-Tempered Likelihood: Honest Confidence Intervals for Misspecified Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20718)
*Benjamin Nachman,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: stat.ME

TL;DR: 本文提出“well-tempered likelihood”（温调似然）方法，通过将似然比检验统计量除以最佳拟合点处的拟合优度（GOF）统计量，在模型误设定（misspecification）下自动限制置信区间宽度，避免因数据量增大而产生过度自信的推断；该方法在正确设定时恢复标准推断，在误设定时通过比例缩放保持置信区间自限，本质上是降低有效样本量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在粒子物理学及更广泛的物理科学中，基于似然（likelihood）的推断依赖于模型准确描述数据的假设。当模型存在误设定（misspecification）时，标准置信区间会随着数据量增大而收缩至零宽度，产生过度自信且可能误导的约束。因此需要一种能够在模型误设定下自动防止置信区间过度收缩的推断方法。

Method: 提出well-tempered likelihood方法，将似然比检验统计量（likelihood-ratio test statistic）除以在最佳拟合点处计算的拟合优度（goodness-of-fit, GOF）统计量。在正确设定（correct specification）下，GOF为$\mathcal{O}(1)$，恢复标准推断；在误设定（misspecification）下，似然与GOF均按$\mathcal{O}(N)$缩放，其比值保持$\mathcal{O}(1)$，从而使置信区间自限在一个由模型不充分性决定的底限（floor）上，本质上降低了有效样本量。文中给出了分箱（binned）和无箱（unbinned）两种公式化版本，后者基于分类器双样本检验（classifier two-sample test）。

Result: 在正确设定下，well-tempered likelihood恢复标准似然推断结果；在误设定下，其置信区间不会随数据量增大而无限收缩，而是自限在一个由模型不充分性决定的底限。论文通过高斯示例以及利用合成电子-正电子（electron-positron）碰撞数据测量强耦合常数（strong coupling constant）的实验展示了该方法的效果。

Conclusion: Well-tempered likelihood能够有效应对模型误设定问题，在数据量增大时自动限制置信区间的过度收缩，避免产生过度自信的推断。该方法同时适用于分箱与无箱数据场景，为粒子物理学及更广泛物理科学中的鲁棒似然推断提供了一种实用的自限机制。

Abstract: Likelihood-based inference in particle physics, and in the physical sciences more broadly, relies on the assumption that the model accurately describes the data. When the model is misspecified, though, standard confidence intervals shrink to zero width with increasing data, producing overconfident and potentially misleading constraints. We propose the well-tempered likelihood, which divides the likelihood-ratio test statistic by a goodness-of-fit (GOF) statistic evaluated at the best-fit point. Under correct specification, the GOF is $\mathcal{O}(1)$ and standard inference is recovered. Under misspecification, both the likelihood and the GOF scale as $\mathcal{O}(N)$ for $N$ data points, so their ratio remains $\mathcal{O}(1)$ and the resulting well-tempered confidence interval self-limits at a floor determined by the model's inadequacy, essentially reducing the effective sample size. In other words, \textit{all models are correct, as long as your dataset is small enough}. We present binned and unbinned formulations of the well-tempered likelihood---the latter based on a classifier two-sample test---and demonstrate our method on a Gaussian example and on a measurement of the strong coupling constant using synthetic electron-positron collisions.

</details>

### [19] [An FBSDE Construction of the Sine-Gordon EQFT for $β^{2} < \frac{6}{7}\, 8π$ and Perturbative Renormalization in the Full Subcritical Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20632)
*Sarah-Jean Meyer*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在有限体积下构造了正弦-戈登测度（sine-Gordon measure）及其重整化有效势（renormalized effective potential），达到第七阈值（seventh threshold）。构造基于弱随机控制问题（weak stochastic control problem）、相关的弱前向-后向随机微分方程（weak FBSDE），并利用多极梅耶展开（multipole Mayer expansion）分析重整化流方程（renormalization flow equation）。整个分析采用完全归纳法，并在亚临界区域（subcritical regime）β² < 8π 内进行了完整的逐阶分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构造正弦-戈登测度及其重整化有效势，将其推广至第七阈值，这是对已有低阶构造工作的深化与拓展。

Method: 采用弱随机控制问题及其对应的弱FBSDE，并结合多极梅耶展开对重整化流方程进行分析。整个构造基于完全归纳法，在亚临界区域β² < 8π内执行逐阶分析。

Result: 成功在有限体积下构造了正弦-戈登测度及其重整化有效势，达到了第七阈值。在亚临界区域β² < 8π内完成了完整的逐阶分析。

Conclusion: 弱随机控制框架与多极梅耶展开相结合的归纳方法，可有效处理高阶阈值下的正弦-戈登测度构造问题。

Abstract: We construct the sine-Gordon measure and its renormalized effective potential in finite volume up to the seventh threshold. The construction relies on a weak stochastic control problem, its associated weak FBSDE, and an analysis of the renormalization flow equation using a multipole Mayer expansion. The analysis is fully inductive, and we include a complete order-by-order analysis in the subcritical regime $β^{2}<8π$.

### [20] [Affine Extension of the Free-Particle--Oscillator--Inverted-Oscillator Triangle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20711)
*Andrey Alcala,Mikhail S. Plyushchay*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维线性势系统，将其视为由自由粒子、谐振子（harmonic oscillator, HO）和反向谐振子（inverted harmonic oscillator, IHO）构成的共形三角形（conformal triangle）的仿射扩展（affine extension）。文章建立了该系统的经典与量子描述，包括加速系变换、波函数交织子（intertwiner）以及传播子（propagator），并展示了Airy能量本征态如何从三种不同途径导出。此外，论文还将分析扩展至均匀交叉电场与磁场中的二维系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自由粒子、谐振子和反向谐振子均属于sl(2,ℝ)代数下的二次齐次哈密顿量，而线性势哈密顿量涉及薛定谔代数（Schrödinger algebra）中的海森堡理想（Heisenberg ideal），构成了上述共形三角形的一种非平凡仿射扩展，值得系统研究。

Method: 论文在经典作用量、正则变换、波函数交织子和传播子等多个层面，将线性势系统与自由粒子通过正则加速系变换（regular accelerated-frame transformation）联系起来；通过与谐振子和反向谐振子的奇异位移振子极限（singular displaced-oscillator limits）建立对应；并采用三次相位变换（cubic-phase transform）、高激发能级凝聚以及亚主导抛物柱面散射分支极限等方法导出Airy本征态。

Result: Airy能量本征态可从自由粒子动量本征态的三次相位变换、谐振子高激发能级的凝聚极限，以及反向谐振子亚主导抛物柱面散射分支的极限三种途径得到。在平面扩展中，线性势对应于均匀电场，而均匀磁场则引入朗道耦合（Landau coupling）和离心反向谐振子项，引导中心动力学（guiding-center dynamics）产生霍尔漂移（Hall drift）。

Conclusion: 线性势系统作为共形三角形的仿射扩展，其与自由粒子、谐振子和反向谐振子之间存在多种明确的理论联系，并可在交叉电磁场中自然实现，体现了加速与旋转动力学在量子系统中的作用。

Abstract: We study the one-dimensional linear-potential system as an affine extension of the conformal triangle formed by the free particle, harmonic oscillator (HO) and inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO). Unlike these homogeneous quadratic Hamiltonians in the $sl(2,\mathbb R)$ sector, the linear-potential Hamiltonian involves the Heisenberg ideal of the Schrödinger algebra. Its direct relation to the free particle is a regular accelerated-frame transformation, developed here at the levels of the classical action, canonical transformation, wave-function intertwiner and propagator; its HO and IHO realizations instead arise through singular displaced-oscillator limits. The Airy energy eigenstates follow from a cubic-phase transform of free-particle momentum eigenstates, from condensation of highly excited harmonic-oscillator levels, and from the limit of a subdominant parabolic-cylinder scattering branch of the inverted oscillator. We also develop a planar extension in homogeneous crossed electric and magnetic fields, where uniform acceleration generates the electric interaction, while uniform rotation produces the Landau coupling and the centrifugal inverted-oscillator term; the guiding-center dynamics yields the Hall drift.

</details>


### [21] [High-resolution decomposition of canonical Hamiltonian systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20740)
*Kaja Krhac,Frederic P. Schuller*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文识别了哈密顿系统（Hamiltonian system）在哈密顿理论中隐藏的结构细节，并给出了其能够被重新表述为具有递增分辨率的结构化端口-哈密顿系统（port-Hamiltonian reformulations）所需的拓扑与动力学条件。研究发现，可达分辨率随构型空间分解出的因子流形（factor manifolds）数量呈指数增长，且仅受原哈密顿量简并性（degeneracies）的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索哈密顿系统在标准哈密顿理论框架下未能显现的结构细节，并寻求通过端口-哈密顿重新表述（port-Hamiltonian reformulation）来揭示这些隐藏结构。

Method: 通过分析拓扑与动力学条件，研究哈密顿系统是否能够被重构为分辨率递增的端口-哈密顿形式（port-Hamiltonian form），并考察分辨率与构型空间分解出的因子流形数量之间的关系。

Result: 结果表明，系统所能达到的分辨率随因子流形数量呈指数增长，而原哈密顿量的简并性会对该增长产生抑制效应。

Conclusion: 标准哈密顿理论中隐藏的结构可以通过端口-哈密顿重新表述被系统性地揭示，其分辨率受构型空间分解结构与哈密顿量简并性的共同影响。

Abstract: We identify the topological and dynamical conditions for a Hamiltonian system to possess port-Hamiltonian reformulations with increasing resolution of structural detail that remains hidden in the Hamiltonian theory. We find that the principally attainable resolution grows exponentially with the number of factor manifolds into which the configuration space of a canonical Hamiltonian system decomposes and is tempered only by degeneracies of the original Hamiltonian.

### [22] [An Operator-Algebraic Exposition of the Thirring-Wehrl Theory of the Quasi-Spin BCS Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21158)
*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文以拟局域C*-代数（quasi-local C*-algebras）与态分解的语言，重述了BCS分析的若干经典和算子代数平均场结果，并通过规范对称性的中心分解统一了简并模型中的基态、热态和动力学描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将历史上分散的BCS分析形式体系（Haag、Emch–Guenin、Thirring–Wehrl等）及后续算子代数平均场结果（Bóna、Raggio–Werner、Bru–de Siqueira Pedra）整合到一个统一的拟局域C*-代数框架中。

Method: 将准自旋模型（quasi-spin model）实现在$2^{\infty}$型UHF代数（UHF algebra of type $2^{\infty}$）上，利用von Neumann不完全无穷张量积（incomplete infinite tensor products）描述乘积扇区（product sectors）。分别定义了强度量的强极限、广延量的域限制极限以及扇区化的Bogoliubov–Haag极限，并给出其算子判据、能隙方程（gap equation）和极限动力学。

Result: 在简并模型中，基态和热规范平均允许在规范圆（gauge circle）上做中心直积分分解（central direct-integral decomposition），且热分解在零温时收敛到基态分解。将规范相位作为中心经典变量加入后，可将依赖于相位的Bogoliubov动力学合并为$C(\mathbb{S}^{1},\mathcal{A})$上的一个自同构群（automorphism group）。

Conclusion: 该框架为BCS型平均场理论提供了严格的算子代数基础，揭示了规范对称性在态分解与动力学统一中的核心作用。

Abstract: This expository review reformulates the BCS analyses of Haag, Emch--Guenin, and Thirring--Wehrl, together with subsequent operator-algebraic mean-field results of Bóna, Raggio--Werner, and Bru--de Siqueira Pedra, in the language of quasi-local $C^{\ast}$-algebras and state decompositions. The quasi-spin model is realized on the UHF algebra of type $2^{\infty}$, with product sectors described by von Neumann's incomplete infinite tensor products. This framework distinguishes strong limits of intensive observables, domain-restricted limits of extensive observables, and sectorwise Bogoliubov--Haag limits, including their operator criterion, gap equation, and limiting dynamics. In the degenerate model, the ground-state and thermal gauge averages admit central direct-integral decompositions over the gauge circle, and the thermal decomposition converges to the ground-state decomposition at zero temperature. Adjoining the gauge phase as a central classical variable combines the phase-dependent Bogoliubov dynamics into one automorphism group on $C(\mathbb{S}^{1},\mathcal{A})$.

</details>

Method: 采用泛函分析中的预解式范数估计方法，研究连续算子与通过特定嵌入方式构造的离散对应物之间的差异；针对不同离散化方案，分别分析是否需要引入修正项以保证广义范数预解收敛。

Result: 研究表明，部分离散化方案能够直接实现网格参数趋于零时的广义范数预解收敛；而对于另一些方案，则必须添加适当的修正项才能确保收敛性成立。

Conclusion: 本文关于块算子矩阵的连续极限分析揭示了离散化方案的收敛性差异，为相关量子系统（如双层石墨烯）的数值模拟提供了理论依据，并指出了需额外修正的离散化条件。

Abstract: Building upon a recent result by H. Cornean, H. Garde, and A. Jensen concerning continuum limits of discrete Dirac operators, we extend the analysis to a wide class of block operator matrices. This class includes, among others, the bilayer graphene Hamiltonian. Our main goal is to find norm estimates for the difference between the resolvents of continuous operators and their discrete counterparts embedded in the continuum in a specific way. While some discretization schemes lead directly to convergence in the generalized norm resolvent sense as the mesh parameter tends to zero, others require the addition of a suitable correction term to ensure the convergence.

### [24] [Representation of the causal logic for the Dirac system and the electron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21266)
*Domenico P. L. Castrigiano,Carmine De Rosa,Valter Moretti*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于狄拉克概率流守恒和一般性的流到局域化（current-to-localization）程序，构建了狄拉克系统与电子的因果逻辑（causal logic）的协变表示。通过非定相（non-stationary phase）论证推导出多项式衰减估计，验证了定义协变非定时局域化（covariant achronal localization）所需条件，并建立了该局域化在欧几里得空间、全时空区域以及正能子空间上的结构性质，包括位置算子修正、微观因果性、高能极限下的洛伦兹收缩等。最后讨论了电子-正电子分解及位置测量诱导的正电子产生普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为狄拉克系统和电子构建一种协变的因果逻辑表示，解决现有局域化方案（如Newton-Wigner算子）在相对论框架下的协变性和因果性问题。

Method: 基于守恒的狄拉克概率流（Dirac probability current），采用一般性的流到局域化程序（current-to-localization procedure）作用于非定时区域（achronal regions）；通过非定相（non-stationary phase）论证推导多项式衰减估计以验证定义条件；将局域化延拓至完整时空区域以获得因果逻辑表示。

Result: 在欧几里得空间上，狄拉克局域化与标准投影值局域化一致，其位置算子与Newton-Wigner算子相差一个有界自伴修正。完整狄拉克非定时局域化为投影值（projection valued），以正交性表示非定时分离，满足微观因果性。压缩到电子子空间后成为正算子值（positive-operator valued），同时保持因果性。高能极限下获得了精确概率意义上的洛伦兹收缩。位置测量诱导的正电子产生具有普适性，与具体测量装置无关。

Conclusion: 本文建立的协变非定时局域化框架统一了狄拉克系统与电子的因果逻辑表示，揭示了其与标准投影值局域化及Newton-Wigner算子的关系，并在微观因果性、洛伦兹收缩、测量诱导的正电子产生等方面得到了关键结构性质。

Abstract: We construct a covariant representation of the causal logic for the Dirac system and the electron, based on the conserved Dirac probability current and a general current-to-localization procedure for achronal regions. A polynomial decay estimate, derived by a non-stationary phase argument, verifies the conditions required to define covariant achronal localization for the full Dirac system. Extending this localization to complete spacetime regions yields the corresponding causal-logic representation; restriction to the positive-energy invariant subspace gives the analogous construction for the electron. We establish several structural properties. On Euclidean space, Dirac localization agrees with canonical projection-valued localization, while its position operator differs from the Newton--Wigner operator by an explicitly determined bounded self-adjoint correction. Full Dirac achronal localization is projection valued and represents achronal separateness by orthogonality, thus satisfying microscopic causality. After compression to the electron subspace, it becomes positive-operator valued while preserving causality. We further extend known results from spatial to general achronal regions, prove separation and norm-one criteria, and analyze the high-boost limit, obtaining Lorentz contraction in a precise probabilistic sense. Finally, we discuss the electron--positron decomposition and the state transformation induced by position measurements, showing that measurement-induced positron production is universal and independent of the specific measuring device.

### [26] [Two-phase source and reaction coefficient Stefan type problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21388)
*Targyn A. Nauryz*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究抛物型热方程的反向两相Stefan型问题，通过傅里叶谱展开（Fourier spectral expansion）和适当的变换，从多种附加数据中重建未知的含时源系数和反应系数，证明了弱解与强解的存在性、唯一性、有界性和正则性，并验证了系数在含噪数据下的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两相Stefan问题在相变过程（phase-change process）中广泛存在，但其含时源系数和反应系数的反演识别问题尚未得到充分解决。本文旨在为这类问题提供严格的数学基础，并建立有效的系数重建方法。

Method: 首先通过合适的变换将原始的自由边界问题（free-boundary problem）转化为固定空间区域上的等价方程；然后利用傅里叶谱展开（Fourier spectral expansion）推导未知系数的重建公式。针对两种不同设定：第一种设定中，从积分、逐点和非局部附加数据识别源系数，导出Volterra积分方程（Volterra integral equation）；第二种设定中，采用指数变换恢复反应系数。

Result: 两个移动边界各自提供独立的Stefan条件（Stefan condition），这足以确定两个未知的含时系数，无需额外的超定条件（overdetermination condition）。在适当假设下，建立了弱解和强解的存在性、唯一性、有界性和正则性。数值算例表明重建程序可行，且在含噪数据下系数保持稳定。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法为识别两相相变过程中含时热参数（time-dependent thermal parameters）提供了严格的数学基础，具有理论完备性和实际适用性。

Abstract: This paper investigates inverse two-phase Stefan-type problems for parabolic heat equations with unknown time-dependent source and reaction coefficients. Suitable transformations reduce the original free-boundary problems to equivalent equations on fixed spatial domains, and Fourier spectral expansions are used to derive reconstruction formulas for the unknown coefficients. In the first formulation, the source coefficients are identified from integral, pointwise, and nonlocal additional data, leading to Volterra integral equations. In the second formulation, an exponential transformation is applied to recover the reaction coefficients. A principal advantage of the model with two moving boundaries is that each boundary provides its own Stefan condition which sufficient to determine the two unknown time-dependent coefficients without additional overdetermination conditions. Under appropriate assumptions the existence, uniqueness, boundedness and regularity of weak and strong solutions are established. Illustrative examples confirm the applicability of the reconstruction procedure and show that the coefficients remain stable under the noisy data. The proposed approach provides a rigorous base for identifying time-dependent thermal parameters in two-phase phase-change processes.

### [27] [SQUID Readout of a High-$Q$ Superconducting $LC$ Resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20831)
*Roman Kolevatov,Saptarshi Chaudhuri,Lyman Page*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文利用直流SQUID配合SQUID串联阵列放大器读出链路，实现了对超导LC谐振器（约250 kHz，Q ≈ 2×10^6）的读出。实验发现谐振器品质因数Q依赖于SQUID的磁通偏置点，并据此推断出SQUID的有效输入阻抗和谐振器电路的有效温度，表明该系统可作为未来基于集总元件谐振器与SQUID读出实验（尤其是DMRadio项目中的低质量轴子搜索）的工作原型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现对高品质因数超导LC谐振器的灵敏读出，并探究SQUID读出电路对谐振器性能（如品质因数Q和有效温度）的影响，为未来低质量轴子搜索等实验提供可行的工作原型。

Method: 采用直流SQUID（dc SQUID）后接SQUID串联阵列放大器（SQUID series-array amplifier）作为读出链路，测量超导LC谐振器（谐振频率约250 kHz，Q ≈ 2×10^6）在不同SQUID磁通偏置点（flux-bias point）下的响应，通过分析谐振峰在噪声谱中的变化来推断SQUID有效输入阻抗和谐振器电路的有效温度。

Result: 谐振器品质因数Q依赖于SQUID磁通偏置点：在SQUID调制曲线（modulation curve）的缓斜率点（shallow-slope point）附近Q增大，在陡斜率点（steep-slope point）附近Q减小，与之前观察到的SQUID阻尼效应（damping effects）一致。从Q的变化中推断出SQUID有效输入阻抗（effective input impedance）；从噪声谱的谐振峰推断出谐振器电路的有效温度（effective temperature），并发现该温度也依赖于SQUID磁通偏置点，暗示可能存在SQUID反作用噪声（back-action noise）的贡献。

Conclusion: 该系统展示了基于SQUID读出的集总元件谐振器（lumped-element resonator）的可行工作原型，尤其适用于DMRadio项目中需要低质量（low-mass）轴子搜索（axion searches）的未来实验。

Abstract: We demonstrate the readout of a superconducting $LC$ resonator, with $Q \approx 2 \times 10^{6}$ at approximately 250 kHz, using a dc SQUID followed by a SQUID series-array amplifier readout chain. We find that $Q$ depends on the SQUID flux-bias point, increasing near the shallow-slope point of the SQUID modulation curve and decreasing near the steep-slope point, consistent with the previously observed SQUID damping effects. From this variation, we infer the SQUID effective input impedance. We further infer the effective temperature of the resonator circuit from the resonance peak in the noise spectrum and show that it also depends on the SQUID flux-bias point, suggesting a possible contribution from SQUID back-action noise. This system provides a working prototype for future experiments based on lumped-element resonators with SQUID readout, in particular low-mass axion searches within the DMRadio program.

### [28] [Cross-streamline diffusiophoretic migration of colloids in Taylor-dispersed channel flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20898)
*Yiran Li,Mobin Alipour,Amir A. Pahlavan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了胶体在压力驱动通道流中扩散泳输运的中间时间尺度行为，发现泰勒弥散后的溶质场保留了随 \(t^{-1/2}\) 衰减的残余横向梯度，该梯度虽在浓度上很小，但在 \(\nabla\ln c\) 上足够大，从而驱动胶体跨流线迁移，导致吸引锋面前沿锐化与排斥锋面后沿展宽，并通过数值模拟和微流实验验证了该动力学过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体在压力驱动通道流中的扩散泳输运，以往研究多局限于早期全二维溶质场极限或晚期宏观输运（macrotransport）极限，然而大量实验实际运行在中间时间窗口 \(a^2/D_{\mathrm s}\ll t\ll a^2/D_{\mathrm p}\)——溶质已进入泰勒弥散（Taylor dispersion）阶段，但胶体颗粒在间隙方向上仍几乎不扩散。因此，需要揭示该中间区间中溶质残余梯度对胶体迁移的驱动作用及其动力学后果。

Method: 采用渐近泰勒区溶质场模型结合非扩散轨迹模型（non-diffusive trajectory model）描述胶体运动；通过直接数值模拟（direct simulations）和微流控实验（microfluidic experiments）验证预测的前沿锐化与展宽动力学。

Result: 泰勒弥散后的溶质保留了一个与轴向梯度相比被佩克莱数（Péclet number）增强的残余横向梯度，该梯度仅以 \(t^{-1/2}\) 衰减；这一梯度在浓度上很小，但在对数浓度梯度 \(\nabla\ln c\) 上足够大，能驱动胶体的跨流线迁移。吸引锋面（\(c_{\mathrm f}>c_{\mathrm i}\)）使颗粒向更快的中心流线移动，导致前沿锐化并加速清除；排斥锋面（\(c_{\mathrm f}<c_{\mathrm i}\)）使颗粒向较慢的近壁流线移动，导致后沿展宽并延迟清除。数值模拟和微流实验均证实了这些锋面锐化与展宽动力学。

Conclusion: 泰勒弥散后的溶质场在颗粒视角下可以保持动态二维性，即使其浓度在横截面上几乎均匀；所提出的渐近溶质场与非扩散轨迹模型能够很好地捕捉观察到的锋面几何、密度分布和清除动力学。

Abstract: Diffusiophoretic transport of colloids in pressure-driven channel flow is commonly analysed in two limits: an early-time regime in which the solute field is fully two-dimensional, and a late-time macrotransport regime in which cross-sectional homogenization leaves only a weak axial bias on the particles. For colloids, however, many experiments operate in the broad intermediate window \(a^2/D_{\mathrm s}\ll t\ll a^2/D_{\mathrm p}\): the solute has entered the Taylor-dispersion regime, but the particles remain effectively non-diffusive across the gap. We show that the Taylor-dispersed solute retains a residual transverse gradient that is Péclet-enhanced relative to the axial gradient and decays only as \(t^{-1/2}\). This gradient is small in the solute concentration but large enough in \(\nabla\ln c\) to drive cross-streamline migration of colloids. Attractive fronts (\(c_{\mathrm f}>c_{\mathrm i}\)) move particles toward faster centreline streamlines, sharpening the leading edge and accelerating removal; repulsive fronts (\(c_{\mathrm f}<c_{\mathrm i}\)) move particles toward slower near-wall streamlines, broadening the trailing edge and delaying removal. Direct simulations and microfluidic experiments confirm these front-sharpening and front-broadening dynamics. An asymptotic Taylor-regime solute field, combined with a non-diffusive trajectory model, captures the observed front geometries, density profiles, and removal dynamics. The results show that Taylor-dispersed solute fields can remain dynamically two-dimensional for particles, even when their concentration is nearly cross-sectionally uniform.

Method: 采用由两条半柔性链组成的模型，调节碱基配对相互作用的强度与扭转能量的相对大小，研究双螺旋结构的稳定性；通过计算高斯连接数来定量表征不同形态相之间的拓扑转变。

Conclusion: 碱基配对的强度与扭转弹性之间存在微妙的平衡，这种平衡对于在无外部约束条件下保持DNA双螺旋结构至关重要；高斯连接数可作为表征形态相变的有效拓扑指标。

Abstract: The mechanical and structural properties of dsDNA have been successfully described by models with varying levels of complexity and coarse-graining schemes. Prior work has characterized local stacking/twist effects and force-torque phase diagrams under external constraints. However, the role of base-pairing and torsional elasticity in global morphological transitions remain poorly characterized in the absence of external constraints. Here we investigate the delicate balance required for the strength of base-pairing interactions and the twisting energy to preserve the double-helix structure in a model made up of two semiflexible chains. We found that the model exhibits several distinct morphological phases: flat, random coil, double-helix, and the unwound double-helix. We calculate the Gauss linking number to characterize transitions between these phases.

### [30] [Two-Temperature Induced Phase Separation: Non-equilibrium Phase Behavior, Ordering, and Kinetics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21269)
*Nayana Venkatareddy,Jaydeep Mandal,Jayeeta Chattopadhyay,Prabal K. Maiti*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了双温诱导相分离（2-TIPS）作为一种标量活性系统中的通用非平衡机制，重点总结了其在不同软物质系统中的最新进展，包括由粒子形状各向异性、手性、约束和拓扑结构导致的有序相，以及密度依赖的相分离动力学和粗粒化描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双温诱导相分离（2-TIPS）已被提出作为具有异质性活性的标量活性系统（scalar active systems）中的一种通用非平衡机制，但该机制在不同软物质系统中的普适性及涌现有序相仍需系统梳理。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）形式，系统归纳了2-TIPS在多种软物质系统（soft-matter systems）中的研究进展，涵盖粒子形状各向异性（particle shape anisotropy）、手性（chirality）、约束（confinement）和拓扑（topology）等因素的影响。

Result: 研究发现，2-TIPS完全由非均匀的能量注入及由此产生的不同粒子种类间的热流（heat flux）驱动，区别于平衡态相分离（equilibrium phase separation）或运动诱导相分离（MIPS）。此外，密度依赖的相分离动力学（density-dependent phase-separation kinetics）和粗粒化描述（coarse-grained descriptions）为连接微观动力学与宏观行为提供了桥梁。

Conclusion: 2-TIPS作为活性系统中的通用非平衡机制，对理解异质性活性系统中的相行为具有重要意义；文中还指出了未来研究的关键方向。

Abstract: Two-temperature induced phase separation (2-TIPS) has emerged as a generic non-equilibrium mechanism in scalar active systems with heterogeneous activity, where particles coupled to different thermal reservoirs spontaneously demix into dense cold and dilute hot phases. Unlike equilibrium phase separation or motility-induced phase separation (MIPS), 2-TIPS is driven solely by unequal energy injection and the resulting heat flux between particle species. This review summarizes recent advances in 2-TIPS across diverse soft-matter systems, highlighting both its universal non-equilibrium mechanisms and the emergent ordered phases arising from particle shape anisotropy, chirality, confinement, and topology. We further discuss density-dependent phase-separation kinetics and coarse-grained descriptions linking microscopic dynamics to macroscopic behavior, and outline key directions for future research.

</details>


### [31] [A single length scale rules ballistic aggregation: travels of a droplet train](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21315)
*Nathan Vani,Stefan Kooij,Aritro Mukherjee,Antoine Parrenin,Cees J. M. van Rijn,Daniel Bonn*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文首次通过液滴喷射实验实现一维弹道聚集（ballistic aggregation），验证了其标度律（scaling law）由单一长度尺度主导，并发现空气阻力虽改变速度相关性符号，但一维有序约束仍保护了弹道聚集的质量标度指数和尾部形态等体特性；同时证明当碰撞携带方向记忆时，Smoluchowski型平均场（mean-field）描述失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弹道聚集作为跨尺度（从颗粒气体到行星吸积）的重要非平衡过程（non-equilibrium process），其动力学行为在实验层面尚缺乏直接验证。该研究旨在通过一维液滴实验实现弹道聚集，检验理论标度预测，并探究空气阻力等实际因素对过程特性的影响。

Method: 研究者利用液体射流破碎形成的液滴串（droplet train）构建一维弹道聚集实验系统，同时辅以数值模拟，对液滴间的碰撞、聚集过程进行标度分析和速度相关性测量。

Result: 实验与模拟结果确认了理论预测的标度行为，表明全局过程由单一长度尺度（single length scale）主导。空气阻力使相邻液滴的速度相关性符号反转，但一维有序约束保护了弹道聚集的标度指数（scaling exponent）和大质量尾部形状等体特性（bulk characteristics）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，当碰撞过程携带方向记忆（directional memory）时，Smoluchowski型平均场方法失效，正如本文在射流喷雾（jet-generated sprays）中所证明的那样。该工作为弹道聚集提供了首个一维实验实现，并揭示了实际流体力学扰动下该过程的鲁棒性。

Abstract: Ballistic aggregation is a canonical non-equilibrium process, relevant across scales from granular gases to planetary accretion. Collisions are driven by differences in velocities, building up persistent correlations between neighbors. Here, we provide the first experimental realization of one-dimensional ballistic aggregation in a train of droplets formed by the breakup of a liquid jet. Experiments and simulations confirm the analytically predicted scaling, with the global process shown to be governed by a single length scale. While air drag inverts the sign of neighbor velocity correlations, a 1D ordering constraint protects bulk characteristics of ballistic aggregation such as the scaling exponent and the shape of the large mass tail. More broadly, our results show that Smoluchowski-like mean-field descriptions fail when collisions carry directional memory -- as demonstrated here for jet-generated sprays.

</details>


### [32] [Pressure and asymmetry govern the shape and stiffness of inflatables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21378)
*Nathan Vani,Tom Joblin,Alejandro Ibarra,José Bico,Étienne Reyssat,Benoît Roman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由两片不同刚度的薄片构成的可充气平行管网络（networks of parallel tubes），其全局形状由相邻管道的结合角（binding angle）控制，刚度不对称性（stiffness asymmetry）诱导出与压力相关的卷曲和硬化行为。通过将管截面建模为两根耦合杆（coupled rods），定量描述了其几何与力学特性，包括刚度与压力的平方根关系以及接触诱导硬化，并展示了其在多功能形状变形（shape-morphing）中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统软体机器人（soft robots）的充气结构通常依赖薄片（thin sheets）的不可拉伸性，默认直管形状由体积最大化决定；然而，作者希望利用薄片刚度差异和管道间的结合角度来实现对整体形状的主动调控，突破这一默认行为，从而获得更丰富的形变控制能力。

Method: 将每个充气管的横截面建模为两根耦合的弹性杆（coupled rods），考虑两片薄片的不同刚度（stiffness asymmetry）以及相邻管道之间的结合角（binding angle），建立描述充气网络几何与力学的理论模型。

Result: 模型定量重现了由于刚度不对称和结合角导致的压力依赖性卷曲和硬化行为；发现刚度与压力的平方根成正比（stiffness scaling as square root of pressure），以及相邻管道间接触诱导的硬化现象（contact-induced stiffening）。与仅限于高压区域的传统研究不同，该模型在连续压力范围内均有效，从而实现了对曲率的连续可编程控制。

Conclusion: 由非对称薄片构成的可充气管网络是一种通用的多功能形状变形（shape-morphing）平台，能够通过压力实现多程控制（multiprogrammable control），为轻量化软体机器人提供了一种可扩展的新方案。

Abstract: Inflatables made of thin sheets constitute a lightweight, scalable alternative to conventional soft robots. Since sheets are essentially inextensible while offering low resistance to bending, the shape of a straight tube should be trivially set by volume maximization. We show that networks of parallel tubes made from two sheets differing in stiffness defy this expectation as their global shape is governed by the binding angle at the junctions of adjacent tubes. Through this angle, the stiffness asymmetry induces a pressure-dependent curling and stiffening of the networks. Modeling a tube cross-section as two coupled rods, we quantitatively describe the geometry and mechanics of this new class of inflatables. Our model captures unexpected mechanical features such as a stiffness scaling as the square root of pressure and a contact-induced stiffening between neighboring tubes -- challenging common assumptions on thin-sheet inflatables. Unlike prior work restricted to the high-pressure regime, the pressure-dependent description further enables multiprogrammable control over a continuous range of curvatures. Discussing a variety of examples, we finally show that networks of asymmetric tubes are a versatile platform for functional shape-morphing objects.

</details>


### [33] [A statistical-physics framework for translocation elastometry of deformable particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21506)
*Pierre Ronceray*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个数学框架，将驱动软粒子通过窄孔的随机穿越速率测量转化为定量力学测量，通过一维布朗动力学（Brownian dynamics）在弹性势垒上的穿越问题，识别出热激活（thermally activated）与摩擦受限（friction-limited）两种动力学区间，并以此提取粒子的形变能量与几何信息，为纳米孔传感（nanopore sensing）中的“穿越弹性测量术（translocation elastometry）”提供了自校准途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 软粒子（soft particle）通过比自身更窄的孔时需发生形变，穿越速率取决于粒子被挤压的难易程度。目前缺乏一种系统的方法，将这种驱动随机穿越的速率测量转化为定量的力学测量，从而获取粒子的弹性与形状信息。

Method: 将粒子进入孔道的过程建模为一维布朗动力学在弹性势垒（elastic barrier）上的穿越问题，对传输问题进行了精确求解（solved exactly），并识别出两种动力学区间：低驱动力下的热激活区间（形变能量主导）和高驱动力下的摩擦受限区间（摩擦主导）。

Result: 识别出两种动力学区间：在低驱动力时，穿越过程受热激活控制，受限于粒子形变所需的能量；在高驱动力时，穿越过程受摩擦受限。通过结合这两个区间的测量数据，可提取粒子的形变能量（deformation energy）及相关几何信息。

Conclusion: 该方法可应用于纳米孔传感领域（驱动力为外加电压），提供一个自校准的途径——穿越弹性测量术（translocation elastometry）——从电流-电压测量中获取单个软纳米粒子的弹性与形状。

Abstract: A soft particle driven through a pore narrower than itself must deform to pass, and how quickly it does so is set by how hard it is to squeeze. We propose a mathematical framework for turning rate measurements of this driven, stochastic passage into quantitative mechanical measurements. Treating the entry of the particle as one-dimensional Brownian dynamics across an elastic barrier, we solve the transport problem exactly and identify two dynamical regimes: at low drive the passage is thermally activated and limited by the energy needed to deform the particle, and at high drive it is friction-limited. We propose a framework to extract the particle's deformation energy and relevant geometrical information by combining measurements in these two regimes. This method could be used in the context of nanopore sensing, where the drive is an applied voltage: the framework then provides a self-calibrating route---translocation elastometry---from a current-voltage measurement to the elasticity and shape of individual soft nanoparticles.

</details>

### [34] [Solar axion searches with RES-NOVA: projected sensitivity and first prototype limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21363)
*D. Alloni,G. Benato,P. Carniti,M. Cataldo,L. Chen,M. Clemenza,M. Consonni,G. Croci,I. Dafinei,F. A. Danevich,J. De Miguel,C. de Vecchi,D. Di Martino,R. Elleboro,N. Ferreiro Iachellini,F. Ferroni,F. Filippini,V. Fonoll,S. Ghislandi,A. Giachero,M. Giannotti,L. Gironi,P. Gorla,C. Gotti,D. L. Helis,D. V. Kasperovych,V. V. Kobychev,A. Lella,G. Lucente,G. Marcucci,A. Melchiorre,A. Menegolli,S. Nisi,M. Musa,L. Pagnanini,L. Pattavina,G. Pessina,S. Pirro,S. Pozzi,M. C. Prata,A. Puiu,S. Quitadamo,M. P. Riccardi,M. Rossella,R. Rossini,E. Sala,F. Saliu,A. Salvini,V. I. Tretyak,L. Trombetta,D. Trotta,H. Yuan*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: RES-NOVA实验——原设计用于探测超新星中微子——被证明也是太阳轴子（solar axions）的有效探测手段。研究计算了多种太阳轴子通量分量经探测通道折叠后的信号，给出了在三个耦合参数平面上的投影灵敏度，并利用考古铅制成的PbWO4原型探测器首次在真实数据上获得了太阳轴子的排除限（exclusion limit）。结果表明RES-NOVA能同时探测轴子-光子（g_aγ）、轴子-电子（g_ae）和轴子-核子（g_aN）耦合，与现有实验互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RES-NOVA原本设计用于探测超新星中微子，但其高密度、高原子序数（Z）吸收体和亚keV能量分辨率同样适用于探测太阳轴子。研究旨在评估RES-NOVA在轴子多耦合参数空间中的探测能力，并利用已有原型数据首次对太阳轴子进行真实数据约束。

Method: 计算了太阳轴子通量中Primakoff、ABC（原子复合与退激发、轫致辐射、康普顿散射）、纵向等离激元（longitudinal plasmon, LP）和57Fe核线四种分量，经逆Primakoff和光电子效应（axioelectric effect）两类探测通道在PbWO4中产生的信号。采用最优区间分析（optimum-interval analysis）方法，在无背景模型依赖的条件下处理13 g考古铅PbWO4原型探测器的真实数据。

Result: 对于1 ton·年曝光的RES-NOVA演示装置，给出了在(g_ae,g_aγ)、(g_ae,g_aN)和(g_aγ,g_aN)三个耦合平面上的投影灵敏度。g_ae的探测极限与XENONnT相当（相差约2倍内），尽管本底高约四个数量级。逆Primakoff对g_aγ的约束基于吸收而非相干转换，因此与轴子质量无关（不同于磁日光望远镜）。利用13 g原型数据获得了首个基于真实数据的太阳轴子排除限。

Conclusion: RES-NOVA被确立为一种有前景的多耦合太阳轴子探测装置，能同时敏感于g_ae、g_aγ和g_aN三个耦合参数，与现有日光望远镜（helioscope）和直接探测实验形成互补。

Abstract: RES-NOVA is a cryogenic experiment based on PbWO4 scintillating bolometers produced from archaeological lead, originally designed to detect coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CEvNS) from galactic core-collapse supernovae. We show that the same high-density, high-Z absorbers and sub-keV energy resolution make RES-NOVA an appealing probe of solar axions. We compute the expected signal from the Primakoff, ABC (atomic recombination and de-excitation, Bremsstrahlung, Compton), longitudinal-plasmon (LP), and 57Fe nuclear-line components of the solar axion flux, folded through the inverse-Primakoff and axioelectric detection channels in PbWO4, which probe the axion couplings to photons (g_a-gamma), electrons (g_ae), and nucleons (g_aN), respectively. We derive projected sensitivities for a 1 ton*y exposure of the RES-NOVA demonstrator in the (g_ae,g_a-gamma), (g_ae,g_aN), and (g_a-gamma,g_aN) planes. The projected reach in g_ae approaches that of XENONnT to within a factor of ~2, despite a background roughly four orders of magnitude higher, thanks to the large target mass, the high-Z enhancement of the axioelectric and inverse-Primakoff cross sections, and the sub-keV energy resolution. Because the inverse-Primakoff constraint on g_a-gamma relies on absorption rather than coherent conversion, it is independent of the axion mass, unlike bounds from magnetic helioscopes. We complement these projections with the first solar-axion exclusion limit obtained on real data with a 13 g PbWO4 prototype grown from archaeological lead, using a background-model-independent optimum-interval analysis. These results establish RES-NOVA as a promising multi-coupling probe of solar axions, with simultaneous sensitivity to g_ae, g_a-gamma and g_aN that is complementary to existing helioscope and direct-detection searches.

</details>


### [35] [A converged architecture for processing 32 Tbps of physics data in real-time at the LHCb experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21492)
*Roel Aaij,Christina Agapopoulou,Thomas Boettcher,Dorothea vom Bruch,Daniel Hugo Cámpora Pérez,Adrian Casais Vidal,Tommaso Colombo,Daniel C. Gligorov,Arthur Hennequin,Louis Henry,Brij Kishor Jashal,Saverio Mariani,Rosen Matev,Niklas Nolte,Niko Neufeld,Arantza Oyanguren,Alberto Perro,Flavio Pisani,Renato Quagliani,Florian Reiss,Kate A. Richardson,Alessandro Scarabotto,Rainer Schwemmer,Patrick Spradlin,Marian Stahl,Jiahui Zhuo*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于零拷贝（zero-copy）技术和全GPU（fully-GPU-based）滤波器的商用现成（off-the-shelf）网络架构，能够实时处理大型强子对撞机（LHC）LHCb探测器升级后产生的32 Tbps粒子碰撞数据，这是目前任何物理实验中达到的最高实时数据处理速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LHCb探测器经过升级后，移除了预过滤级（pre-filtering stage），导致数据速率提升了40倍，达到32 Tbps。为了应对这一极高的实时数据处理吞吐量需求，需要设计一种能够高效处理海量粒子碰撞数据的新架构。

Method: 采用商用现成（off-the-shelf）网络硬件，结合零拷贝（zero-copy）技术减少数据搬运开销，并利用基于全GPU（fully-GPU-based）的滤波算法进行实时数据筛选。

Result: 该融合架构（converged architecture）能够实时处理完整的32 Tbps粒子碰撞数据，这是迄今任何物理实验中实现的最高实时数据处理速率。

Conclusion: 该成果扩展了LHCb物理研究计划（physics programme）的覆盖范围，并为粒子物理实验中的实时数据处理设立了新标准。

Abstract: The LHCb detector at the Large Hadron Collider has been upgraded to acquire an unprecedented 32 Tbps of particle-collision data to provide new insights in the High Energy Physics domain. The data produced by the detector is filtered in real-time to select interesting collisions. As part of the upgrade, a pre-filtering stage has been removed leading to a factor 40 increase in data rate. To deal with the high throughput demands of LHCb real-time data processing, we present an off-the-shelf network architecture using zero-copy techniques in conjunction with an efficient, fully-GPU-based filter. Our converged architecture is able to process the full 32 Tbps of particle-collision data in real-time, the highest in any physics experiment to date. Our result extends the reach of the LHCb physics programme and sets a new standard for real-time data processing at particle physics experiments.

### [36] [Measurements of the electroweak production of a $W$ boson in association with two jets at $\sqrt{s}=13\,\mathrm{TeV}$ with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21531)
*ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用ATLAS探测器收集的140 fb⁻¹、质心能量13 TeV的质子-质子对撞数据，测量了高双喷流不变质量区域中W玻色子与两个喷流（jets）的电弱产生过程。测量在通过矢量玻色子散射（vector-boson fusion, VBF）增强的 fiducial 区域内进行，给出了积分产生截面（integrated production cross-section）以及多种微分截面（differential cross-sections），并将其与有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）解释对比，给出了迄今为止最严格的反常三规范玻色子耦合（anomalous triple-gauge-boson couplings）上限之一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电弱W+双喷流过程是研究矢量玻色子散射（VBF）的关键探针，VBF本身对电弱规范耦合及超出标准模型（BSM）的新物理敏感。高双喷流不变质量区域可有效增强VBF信噪比，从而更精确地检验标准模型电弱相互作用并约束反常规范耦合（anomalous gauge couplings）。

Method: 利用140 fb⁻¹的ATLAS质子-质子对撞数据，在 fiducial 区域内选取至少两个喷流、一个电子或缪子以及一个中微子（对应轻子型W衰变）的事件。测量了积分产生截面，并基于粒子层级（particle level）进行反卷积（unfolding），得到关于两个最高能量喷流的角变量、W玻色子运动学以及领头喷流和带电轻子横动量等观测量的微分截面。结果在有效场论（EFT）框架下进行解释。

Result: 给出了积分产生截面以及多个微分截面的粒子层级测量值。在有效场论框架下提取了反常三规范玻色子耦合的上限，该上限在扩展拉格朗日量线性项（linear terms）的约束中属于迄今最严格的结果之一。

Conclusion: 本文的电弱W+双喷流测量在高双喷流不变质量区域提供了对标准模型电弱相互作用的精确检验，并对新的物理效应（尤其是反常三规范玻色子耦合）给出了强约束。测量结果和EFT限制进一步验证了VBF过程在探索新物理中的有效性。

Abstract: Measurements of the electroweak production of a $W$ boson in association with two jets at high dijet invariant mass are performed using a dataset from $140\,\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ of $\sqrt{s}=13\,\mathrm{TeV}$ proton-proton collisions recorded by the ATLAS detector at the LHC. The measurements are made in a fiducial region where the $W$ boson's production via vector-boson fusion is enhanced. The fiducial region requires at least two jets, an electron or a muon, and a neutrino, assuming a leptonic $W$ decay. In addition to the integrated production cross-section, differential cross-sections unfolded to particle level are determined as functions of observables which characterise angular properties of the two highest-energy jets, the kinematics of the $W$ boson, and the transverse momenta of the highest-energy jet and the charged lepton. Results are interpreted in the context of an effective field theory, and the limits placed on anomalous triple-gauge-boson couplings are among the most stringent to date for linear terms of the extended Lagrangian.

</details>

### [37] [Design and Optimization of Metasurfaces for Silicon Photonics: PhD Thesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21091)
*Mathys Le Grand*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文系统解决了超表面（metasurface）逆向设计中的维数灾难与计算成本两大障碍：首先评估了严格麦克斯韦求解器的可靠性，然后开发了基于全卷积神经网络（fully convolutional neural network）的近场代理模型（surrogate model），最后在统一FDTD协议下基准测试了三种逆向设计策略，其中基于扩散模型（diffusion model）和薛定谔桥（Schrödinger bridge）的生成式框架在远超训练尺寸的表面上实现了尺度不变的保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超表面逆向设计面临两个核心障碍：设计空间的巨大维数（immense dimensionality）以及对整个器件进行严格电磁模拟（rigorous electromagnetic simulation）的 prohibitive 计算成本，使得穷举搜索在器件尺度上不可行。

Method: 分三阶段展开：1) 比较三种Li因式分解规则（Li's factorization rules）的RCWA实现，并以FDTD为基准评估其可靠性；2) 构建局部相位近似模型（local phase-approximation model）以及在全卷积架构上训练的代理模型，利用问题对称性（symmetries）将训练数据库扩充四倍；3) 在统一FDTD协议下基准测试三种逆向设计策略——Gerchberg-Saxton迭代检索（Gerchberg-Saxton retrieval）和局部模型、基于代理模型和启发式初始化的梯度下降（gradient descent），以及基于扩散模型和薛定谔桥的生成式框架。

Result: Gerchberg-Saxton与局部模型在目标远场上的$R^2$约为0.925；基于代理模型的梯度下降方法$R^2$约为0.975；生成式框架结合混合后验采样（hybrid posterior sampling）与振幅约束（amplitude constraint），在比训练尺寸大230倍以上的表面上保持尺度不变保真度（scale-invariant fidelity），产生多样且对制造误差容忍的设计；数据库增强将每种方法的$R^2$提升至约0.97。

Conclusion: 通过系统性的三阶段研究——求解器可靠性评估、计算瓶颈消除以及多种逆向设计策略的基准测试——本文证明了利用机器学习代理模型和生成式框架可以有效克服超表面逆向设计中的维数灾难与计算成本障碍，实现远超训练尺寸的高保真度、可制造性良好的设计。

Abstract: Metasurfaces, two-dimensional arrangements of subwavelength nanopillars, provide local control over the phase of light, enabling flat optical functions beyond conventional refractive components. Their inverse design, finding the pillar distribution producing a target response, faces two obstacles: the immense dimensionality of the design space and the prohibitive cost of rigorous electromagnetic simulations, precluding exhaustive exploration at device scale.
  This thesis addresses the challenge in three stages. The first assesses the reliability of rigorous Maxwell solvers: comparing three implementations of Li's factorization rules for RCWA shows that spectral convergence does not guarantee physical fidelity, as these rules implicitly distort the simulated permittivity, most severely in the plasmonic regime. FDTD, immune to such artifacts, is retained as ground truth throughout.
  The second stage removes the computational bottleneck: a local phase-approximation model, then fully convolutional surrogates trained on FDTD simulations of large pillar metasurfaces, predict the near field almost instantaneously. Exploiting problem symmetries quadruples the training database, and the surrogates generalize to much larger apertures while remaining differentiable.
  The third stage benchmarks three strategies under a common FDTD protocol ($R^2$ between realized and target far fields): Gerchberg-Saxton retrieval and Local Model ($R^2\approx0.925$), surrogate-based and heuristic-initialized gradient descent ($R^2\approx0.975$), and a generative framework based on diffusion models and Schrödinger bridges. Hybrid posterior sampling and amplitude constraints restore scale-invariant fidelity on surfaces over 230 times larger than training, with diverse, fabrication-tolerant designs. Database enhancement lifts every approach to $R^2\approx0.97$.

</details>


### [38] [Monolithic Magneto-Optical Mach-Zehnder Isolator Using Laser-Annealed Iron Garnet on a Silicon Waveguide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20964)
*Tomoya Sugita,Reona Motoji,Yuki Yoshihara,Dan Maeda,Hiroki Yamamoto,Hibiki Miyashita,Kazushi Ishiyama,Taichi Goto*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于真空局部激光退火（local laser annealing）的方法，在硅基马赫-曾德尔干涉仪（Mach-Zehnder interferometer）中直接结晶铈掺杂钇铁石榴石（Ce:YIG），避免了传统炉退火导致的高温损伤，实现了13.6 dB隔离比的光隔离器（optical isolator），验证了热敏感硅光子器件与磁光薄膜的高通量集成可行性。
