  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅光子电路需要单片集成基于磁光石榴石（magneto-optical garnet）的光隔离器，但传统炉退火（furnace annealing）使整个芯片暴露于高温，导致硅波导和金属电极退化。因此需要一种局部、低热影响的退火方法来实现高质量磁光薄膜的结晶。

Method: 使用真空环境下的915 nm激光对离子束溅射（ion beam sputtering）沉积的无籽层（seed layer）Ce:YIG薄膜进行局部退火，利用微米级沟槽（micrometer-scale trenches）约束激光加热区域；将结晶后的Ce:YIG直接集成在硅基马赫-曾德尔干涉仪中，通过透射电子显微镜（TEM）表征界面结构。

Result: 在1540 nm波长下测得隔离比（isolation ratio）为13.6 dB，对应的法拉第旋转（Faraday rotation）为0.092°/μm，插入损耗（insertion loss）20.4 dB，传播损耗（propagation loss）9.5 dB。TEM显示Ce:YIG已结晶，并在与硅波导的界面处存在约10 nm的边界区域。

Conclusion: 局部激光退火能够在不损伤热敏感硅光电器件的前提下实现磁光薄膜的高温结晶，提供了一种与大规模生产兼容的高通量集成技术，为硅基光子电路中单片光隔离器的制造开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Stable silicon photonic circuits require monolithically integrated optical isolators based on magneto-optical garnet. However, crystallizing the garnet by conventional furnace annealing exposes the entire chip to high temperature and degrades the silicon waveguides and the metal electrodes. Here we avoid this degradation by using local laser annealing in vacuum to crystallize cerium-substituted yttrium iron garnet (Ce:YIG), deposited by ion beam sputtering without a seed layer, directly within a silicon-based Mach-Zehnder interferometer. A 915 nm beam heats only the garnet region confined in micrometer-scale trenches, leaving the surrounding circuit and electrodes intact. The device achieves an isolation ratio of 13.6 dB at a wavelength of 1540 nm, corresponding to a Faraday rotation of 0.092$°$/$μ$m, with an insertion loss of 20.4 dB and a propagation loss of 9.5 dB. Transmission electron microscopy reveals the crystallized Ce:YIG and a ~10 nm boundary region at the interface with the Si waveguide. These results demonstrate that thermally sensitive silicon photonic devices and magneto-optical thin films requiring high-temperature processing can be integrated by a high-throughput technique compatible with mass production.

Method: 采用单层MoS₂集成平面F-P腔结构，利用偏振依赖的相位奇点（polarization dependent phase singularities），在斜入射条件下使器件满足不同阶微分的传递函数（optical transfer functions），仅通过切换入射光偏振态即可切换运算阶数。

Conclusion: 平面F-P腔可作为仅由光偏振控制计算阶数的紧凑型可重构空间微分器，为可调谐光学计算提供了一种快速、便捷且易于集成的策略，在实时目标识别、特征提取和光学数据压缩等领域具有应用潜力。

Abstract: Reconfigurable analog optical computing requires rapid and efficient switching between core mathematical operations, such as first- and second-order spatial differentiation. Here, we demonstrate a monolayer MoS$_2$ integrated a planar Fabry-Pérot (F-P) cavity that performs polarization switchable analog spatial differentiation under oblique incidence. By exploiting polarization dependent phase singularities, the device satisfies distinct optical transfer functions for different-order differentiation at the same operating condition. As a result, first-order and second-order derivatives of input images are experimentally realized by simply switching the incident polarization. These results establish the planar cavity as a compact reconfigurable spatial differentiator, whose computational order is controlled solely by light polarization. This approach provides a fast, convenient, and integration friendly strategy for tunable optical computing, and enables polarization switchable edge detection for image processing, with potential applications in real-time object recognition, feature extraction, and optical data compression.

### [40] [An integrated all-van der Waals nanobeam laser](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21566)
*Aris Koulas-Simos,Pietro Metuh,Athanasios Paralikis,Kartik Gaur,Maximilian Klonz,Imad Limame,Bárbara L. T. Rosa,Chirag C. Palekar,Battulga Munkhbat,Stephan Reitzenstein*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本论文演示了一种基于WS₂/MoSe₂/WS₂异质结构的全范德华（all-van der Waals, all-vdW）高β纳米束激光器，通过光子自相关测量直接验证了激光行为，并观察到从热统计到泊松统计的转变以及接近1的β因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将MoSe₂单层直接集成到基于WS₂的光学谐振腔中，实现最优增益-模式重叠（gain-mode overlap）；构建全vdW高β纳米束激光器，并在低温下测量其激子-腔耦合、发射特性、输入-输出曲线、线宽及激发功率依赖的光子自相关函数（photon-autocorrelation）。

Result: 器件在低温下实现高效激子-腔耦合，具有强定向线性偏振发射、软非线性输入-输出特性和线宽窄化，β因子接近1；光子自相关测量显示g⁽²⁾peak(0)从阈值附近的1.28±0.09降至阈值以上的1.07±0.07，证实从热统计到泊松统计（Poissonian photon statistics）的转变；自相关的时间展宽揭示了涨落主导的激光动力学（fluctuation-dominated lasing dynamics）。

Conclusion: 全vdW异质结构是一种极具吸引力的集成相干光源平台，适用于层状材料光子架构和可扩展量子光子电路（scalable quantum-photonic circuits）。

Abstract: Transition-metal dichalcogenides offer a promising platform for integrated coherent light sources, yet lasing has largely relied on hybrid photonic architectures without direct quantum-optical verification. Here, we demonstrate an all-van der Waals (all-vdW) high-$β$ nanobeam laser based on a WS$_2$/MoSe$_2$/WS$_{2}$ heterostructure, with the MoSe$_2$ monolayer directly integrated in the WS$_{2}$-based optical resonator for optimal gain-mode overlap. The devices exhibit efficient exciton-cavity coupling at cryogenic temperatures, strongly directional and linearly polarized emission, soft nonlinear input-output characteristics and linewidth narrowing, enabling lasing operation with $β$ near unity. Excitation-power-dependent photon-autocorrelation measurements reveal a transition from thermal to Poissonian photon statistics, with $g_{\mathrm{peak}}^{(2)}(0)$ decreasing from $(1.28\,\pm\,0.09)$ near threshold to $(1.07\,\pm\,0.07)$ above threshold, directly verifying lasing operation. Furthermore, temporal broadening of the autocorrelation uncovers fluctuation-dominated lasing dynamics. These results establish all-vdW heterostructures as a highly attractive platform for integrated coherent light sources in layered-material photonic architectures and scalable quantum-photonic circuits.

### [41] [On the Spatially Homogeneous Boltzmann Equation with Mass Exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20684)
*Siwei Luo,Jian-Guo Liu*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有连续质量交换的空间齐次Boltzmann方程，证明了在Grad截断硬势碰撞核下，对于有界连续对称质量交换率，任意具有有限数、质量和动能的非负初值均存在全局非负L¹积分弱解，并建立了高阶矩传播、能量守恒、唯一性以及线性增长质量交换率下的局部理论，证明基于一种新的两阶段自举（bootstrap）方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立具有连续质量交换的空间齐次Boltzmann方程（spatially homogeneous Boltzmann equation with continuous mass exchange）的全局弱解存在性、矩传播、唯一性以及局部理论，填补该领域缺乏系统分析结果的空白。

Method: 采用一种新提出的两阶段自举方法（two-stage bootstrap method）：第一阶段排除质量在m=0处的集中，第二阶段结合该控制与碰撞几何（collision geometry）建立一致可积性（uniform integrability），从而获得紧性（compactness）以构造全局解并识别非线性碰撞形式。证明无需详细平衡（detailed-balance）或相对熵（relative-entropy）结构。

Result: 对于有界连续对称质量交换率，任意满足有限数、质量和动能的非负初值均存在全局非负L¹积分弱解，且数和质量守恒、动能耗散。若初值具有(1+δ)阶高阶矩，则该矩在有限时间区间内传播且动能守恒。在额外1+γ阶矩假设下，解在同初值的所有能量耗散L¹积分弱解中唯一。对于线性增长质量交换率，建立了局部H_p-解理论，且H_p-解可在H_{1+γ}(f)∈L¹(0,T)条件下延续到任意有限时间T。

Conclusion: 成功建立了具有连续质量交换的Boltzmann方程在Grad截断硬势碰撞核下的全局分析与局部理论，所提出的两阶段自举方法为处理质量交换型碰撞算子提供了新的技术工具。

Abstract: We study the spatially homogeneous Boltzmann equation with continuous mass exchange on $X=(0,\infty)_m\times\mathbb R^d_v$, with a Grad cut-off hard-potential collision kernel. For bounded continuous symmetric mass-exchange rates, every nonnegative initial datum with finite number, mass, and kinetic energy admits a global nonnegative $L^1$-integral weak solution in $W^{1,\infty}(0,\infty;L^1(X))$ with number and mass conserved, kinetic energy dissipated. If $\int_X (m|v|^2)^{1+δ} f_0(x)dx<\infty,$ for some $δ>0$, this higher-energy moment propagates on every finite time interval and kinetic energy is conserved through the constructed solution. Moreover, every energy-dissipating solution propagates any such moment. Under the additional $1+γ$ moment assumption, the solution is unique among all energy-dissipating $L^1$-integral weak solutions with the same initial datum. We also establish a local theory for a linearly growing mass-exchange rate. With $H_p(f)=\int_X (1+m+m|v|^2)^pfdx,$ every datum with $H_p(f_0)<\infty$, where $p\ge1+γ$ admits a conservative local $H_p$-solution. Moreover, an $H_p$-solution continues across every finite time $T$ for which $H_{1+γ}(f)\in L^1(0,T).$ This proof requires no detailed-balance or relative-entropy structures. It is based on a new two-stage bootstrap method. The first stage rules out mass concentration at $m=0$, while the second stage combines this control with collision geometry to establish uniform integrability. These estimates provide the compactness needed for the global solution and for the identification of the nonlinear collision form.

### [42] [Writhe-Based Polymer Link Classification Using Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20657)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 链环与纽结的唯一快速分类是一个尚未解决的数学问题，对高分子熔体、DNA和蛋白质等（生物）物理系统具有重要应用价值。

Method: 沿用Sleiman等人（2024, Soft Matter）提出的框架，采用前馈神经网络基于扭结密度矩阵（writhe density matrix）进行训练，对前六种素链环的热平衡构型进行分类。

Result: 网络分类准确率达97%；在不同温度和链长条件下保持高精度；添加破坏拓扑的高斯噪声后精度迅速下降，表明扭结密度矩阵包含对拓扑敏感的特征。

Conclusion: 基于扭结密度矩阵的神经网络能够高效分类两分量链环，为更复杂拓扑（如Borromean环、多分量链环）的快速分类提供了有前景的机器学习工具，尤其当精确数值计算拓扑不变量的计算代价过高时。

Abstract: Unique and rapid classification of knots and links is an open mathematical problem that is relevant to a range of (bio)physical systems, including polymer melts, DNA, and proteins. In this paper, we explore a data-driven approach to the classification problem of link topology. Extending the framework introduced in Ref. 1 (Sleiman et al, 2024 Soft Matter, 20(1), pp.71-78), we show that a feedforward neural network trained on the writhe density matrix classifies thermally equilibrated configurations of the first six prime links with 97% accuracy. We demonstrate that this accuracy remains high across a range of temperatures and lengths of link components, while rapidly deteriorating with the addition of topology-altering Gaussian noise; a result consistent with the writhe density matrix containing features sensitive to topology. Our results show that neural networks based on the writhe density matrix efficiently classify two-component links, establishing machine learning as a promising tool for rapid classification of more complex link topologies, e.g. Borromean rings and multi-component links, as the computational cost of exact numerical calculation of topological invariants becomes prohibitive.

### [43] [Lithium-Projected Phonon Spectral Distributions as Robust Descriptors of Ionic Conductivity in Solid Electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20591)
*Gajendra Bohara,Ramakrishna Podila*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究测试了锂投影声子态密度（Li-PDOS）作为室温离子电导率描述符的可重复性，发现全谱Li-PDOS的Wasserstein核在预测性能上显著优于总声子态密度和静态组成-结构核，表明移动离子分辨的谱分布可作为有用的比较筛选描述符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管晶格动力学（lattice dynamics）被广泛用于固体电解质设计，但声子信息通常被压缩为能带中心或某个标量软度指标，缺乏对完整声子谱作为描述符的系统性评估。

Method: 利用MatterSim力和Phonopy生成OBELiX数据集中晶体学已解析条目的谐波总声子态密度（total DOS）和锂投影声子态密度（Li-PDOS），通过组成与结构审核定义主要队列（260种材料）、严格队列（241种）和精确组成队列（168种），并使用Wasserstein核和Spearman相关系数进行预测与关联分析。

Result: 20个独立声子计算数据库比较中，总DOS和Li-PDOS的平均Wasserstein-1距离分别为0.542 THz和0.731 THz，表明存在系统性投影依赖软化。Li-PDOS的Wasserstein核在保留测试集上达到R²=0.444，显著高于总DOS的0.012和静态组成-结构核的0.181，并在严格和精确队列中保持稳定（R²≈0.45）。

Conclusion: 移动离子分辨的谱分布（mobile-ion-resolved spectral distributions）可作为有用的比较筛选描述符（comparative screening descriptors），但不宜视为普适的因果软度定律（universal causal softness law）。

Abstract: Lattice dynamics are widely invoked in the design of solid electrolytes, yet phonon information is commonly compressed into a band center or another scalar softness measure. Here we test whether the complete lithium-projected phonon density of states (Li-PDOS) provides a reproducible descriptor of experimental room-temperature ionic conductivity. MatterSim forces and Phonopy were used to generate harmonic total and Li-projected spectra for crystallographically resolved entries in the OBELiX dataset. A composition and structure audit defined a primary cohort of 260 materials (212 train and 48 test), a strict cohort of 241, and an exact-composition cohort of 168. Across 20 independently generated phonon-calculation database comparisons, the mean Wasserstein-1 distance was 0.542 THz for total DOS and 0.731 THz for Li-PDOS, revealing broad agreement but systematic, projection-dependent softening. Higher conductivity was associated with redistribution of normalized Li spectral weight toward low frequencies: in the untouched test set, the Li fractions below 2 and 5 THz had Spearman coefficients of 0.333 and 0.374, while the 5$\%$ cumulative-frequency quantile had a coefficient of $-0.393$. A Wasserstein kernel on the full Li-PDOS achieved held-out $R^2=0.444$, compared with 0.012 for total DOS and 0.181 for a static composition--structure kernel. The Li model remained stable in the strict ($R^2=0.462$) and exact ($R^2=0.451$) cohorts. Family adjustment attenuated scalar associations, and Li-versus-total whole-spectrum dependence was cohort sensitive. The results therefore support mobile-ion-resolved spectral distributions as useful comparative screening descriptors, not as a universal causal softness law.

### [44] [Magnetic ground states of CrPS$_4$ and NiPS$_3$ monolayers from long-range exchange interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20631)
*Balazs Nagyfalusi,Ritesh Das,Alvaro Bermejillo-Seco,Herr S. J. van der Zant,Yaroslav M. Blanter,Amador Garcia-Fuente,Jaime Ferrer*

TL;DR: 该研究通过结合第一性原理计算、二阶自旋模型和蒙特卡洛模拟，发现长程交换相互作用对单层CrPS₄和NiPS₃的磁性质具有定性影响，并因此修正了此前对铁磁基态和临界温度的预测，使其与实验一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法仅截取少数几个壳层的交换相互作用并通过拟合总能来确定参数，可能导致对二维硫代磷酸盐单层材料磁性质的错误预测。本文旨在直接提取完整的长程磁交换张量，并揭示其对磁序和临界温度的影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）、二阶自旋模型（second-principles spin models）和蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）相结合，利用密度泛函理论（DFT）中的LKAG形式直接提取磁交换张量（magnetic exchange tensors），直到数值收敛为止，而非截断至少数壳层。

Result: 在CrPS₄中，长程交换相互作用使此前预测的铁磁基态（ferromagnetic ground state）失稳，形成自旋螺旋相（spin-spiral phase），临界温度降至约21 K，与实验结果一致；其磁相图包含多个可通过温度和磁场调控的共线及非共线相。在NiPS₃中，仅当交换相互作用包含至第五壳层时，才出现实验观测到的锯齿形反铁磁序（zigzag antiferromagnetic order）。

Conclusion: 硫代磷酸盐单层（thiophosphate monolayers）的定量预测自旋模型必须包含长程交换相互作用，该研究为准确描述二维范德华磁体（two-dimensional van der Waals magnets）提供了可预测的分析框架。

Abstract: We investigate the magnetic properties of monolayer CrPS$_4$ and NiPS$_3$ by combining first-principles calculations, second-principles spin models, and Monte Carlo simulations. Unlike conventional approaches that truncate exchange interactions after only a few shells and determine them by fitting total energies, we extract the magnetic exchange tensors directly from density functional theory using the LKAG formalism and include interactions until numerical convergence is achieved. We show that long-range exchange interactions qualitatively modify the magnetic behavior of both materials. In CrPS$_4$, they destabilize the previously predicted ferromagnetic ground state and stabilize a spin-spiral phase, reducing the critical temperature to about 21\,K, in agreement with available experiments. The resulting magnetic phase diagram contains multiple collinear and non-collinear phases that can be tuned by temperature and external magnetic fields. In NiPS$_3$, the experimentally observed zigzag antiferromagnetic order only emerges when exchange interactions up to the fifth shell are included. These results demonstrate that quantitatively predictive spin models for thiophosphate monolayers require long-range exchange interactions and provide a predictive framework for accurately describing two-dimensional van der Waals magnets.

### [45] [A high-dimensional neural network potential for finite-temperature phenomena in NiTi martensite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20681)

Conclusion: 所开发的HDNNP为马氏体NiTi体系的原子模拟提供了稳健基础，能够支持包含数十万原子、纳秒时间尺度的复杂结构与功能行为的计算研究。

Abstract: We present a high-dimensional neural network potential (HDNNP) for the martensitic phase of the NiTi shape-memory alloy trained to density functional theory (DFT) data. A central aspect of this work is the systematic validation of the potential with respect to the underlying DFT reference method for key properties governing structural evolution, including equilibrium crystal structures, elastic constants, generalized-stacking fault energies, and vibrational spectra. The HDNNP accurately describes the relative stability of the B19$^\prime$ and B33 phases, including subtle energy differences on the order of meV/atom. The predicted stacking-fault energy landscape is strongly anisotropic and reveals a preferential shear pathway, providing atomistic insight into deformation and twinning mechanisms. Finite-temperature molecular dynamics simulations further enable the investigation of unconstrained structural evolution as a function of temperature. Overall, the developed HDNNP provides a robust basis for atomistic simulations of the complex structural and functional behavior of martensitic NiTi systems containing hundreds of thousands of atoms on nanosecond time scales.

### [46] [Analytical Forces from the Bethe-Salpeter Equation for Large-Scale Excited-State Relaxation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20728)
*Yu Jin,Victor Wen-zhe Yu,Marco Govoni,Giulia Galli*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）的激发态解析原子力高效平面波实现方案，结合密度矩阵微扰理论与拉格朗日方法，避免了传统方法中昂贵的空态求和与原子位移响应计算，并通过GPU加速使含数百原子的固态体系BSE力计算成为可能。在两个点缺陷体系上的验证表明，该方法为异质凝聚体系中的激发态弛豫与振动耦合研究提供了可扩展框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于Bethe-Salpeter方程（BSE）的激发态原子力计算存在计算成本过高的问题，尤其对于固态体系，需要显式空态求和（explicit empty-state summations）以及对每个原子位移进行响应计算（response calculations），这严重限制了BSE力在大规模固态体系中的应用。

Method: 将密度矩阵微扰理论（density-matrix perturbation theory）与拉格朗日方法（Lagrangian approach）相结合，避免了显式空态求和以及对每个原子位移的独立响应计算；同时采用GPU加速（GPU acceleration）提升计算效率。

Result: 该方法使得含数百原子的固态体系（solid-state systems）的BSE力计算变得可行。在金刚石中的氮-空位中心（nitrogen-vacancy center）上，BSE与含时密度泛函理论（TDDFT）给出了一致的激发态弛豫结果；在二维六方氮化硼中的碳二聚体缺陷（carbon-dimer defect）上，BSE中包含的屏蔽电子-空穴相互作用（screened electron-hole interaction）稳定了局域缺陷激发，并修正了半局域TDDFT预测的弛豫模式。

Conclusion: 该工作为异质凝聚体系（heterogeneous condensed systems）中基于BSE水平的激发态弛豫（excited-state relaxation）与振动耦合（vibronic coupling）研究建立了一个可扩展的计算框架。

Abstract: We present an efficient plane-wave implementation of analytical nuclear forces for electronic excited states described by the Bethe-Salpeter equation (BSE). The formulation combines density-matrix perturbation theory with a Lagrangian approach, and avoids both explicit empty-state summations and the response calculations for each atomic displacement, required by conventional approaches based on density functional perturbation theory. Together with GPU acceleration, these advances make BSE forces calculations tractable for solid-state systems containing hundreds of atoms. We demonstrate the method on two point defects with distinct dielectric environments: the nitrogen-vacancy center in diamond, where BSE and time-dependent density functional theory (TDDFT) yield consistent excited-state relaxations, and the carbon-dimer defect in two-dimensional hexagonal boron nitride, where the screened electron-hole interaction included in the BSE stabilizes the localized defect excitation and corrects the relaxation pattern predicted by semilocal TDDFT. These results establish a scalable framework for BSE-level studies of excited-state relaxation and vibronic coupling in heterogeneous condensed systems.

### [47] [First-principles calculation of electron-phonon spectral functions for defects using phonon interpolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20788)
*Zoltan Santha,Gergo Thiering*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于声子插值的黄-里斯谱密度与光学线形函数计算方法，通过在超胞（hypercell）中重建跃迁诱导力并耦合密集采样的振动连续谱，克服了宽带隙半导体中缺陷光学谱的第一性原理计算受限于粗振动谱的问题。该方法在金刚石负电氮-空位（NV⁻）中心上得到验证，可在包含约1700万个原子的超胞上获得平滑、连续的黄-里斯谱密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宽带隙半导体中的点缺陷（point defects）其光谱强烈受电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）影响，但现有的第一性原理（first-principles）直接计算对应的声子边带（phonon sidebands）受限于最大缺陷超胞（supercell）的粗略振动谱（coarse vibrational spectrum），难以获得精细的光谱分辨率。

Method: 该方法基于重建与光学激发相关的跃迁诱导力（transition-induced force），利用该局域力源将缺陷跃迁耦合到密集采样的振动连续谱上；局部缺陷物理量由第一性原理超胞计算获得，而长波声学模与宿主声子谱的精细结构则通过在大型超胞中对角化插值动力学矩阵（interpolated dynamical matrices）来恢复。

Result: 在金刚石负电氮-空位中心（NV⁻ center）的基态³A₂与激发态³E之间的跃迁中，跃迁诱导力强烈局域化于缺陷周围，并在密度泛函理论（DFT）可及的4×4×4超胞中即可获得收敛的局域化度量。该方法在高达32×32×32（约1700万个原子）的超胞上插值电子-声子耦合，恢复了平滑、连续且具有超精细光谱分辨率的黄-里斯谱密度（Huang-Rhys spectral density）。主导耦合带位于约63 meV附近；低能声学贡献遵循预期的线性标度；实验中观测到的光学声子区精细范霍夫相关结构（van-Hove-related structures）也被成功恢复。

Conclusion: 所提出的声子插值方法有效克服了第一性原理计算中缺陷超胞振动谱粗糙的限制，能够在极大超胞上以超精细分辨率获得黄-里斯谱密度和光学线形函数，还原宿主声子谱的精细结构，为宽带隙半导体中缺陷光谱的理论计算提供了可行方案。

Abstract: Point defects in wide-band-gap semiconductors exhibit optical spectra strongly shaped by electron-phonon coupling, but direct first-principles calculation of the corresponding phonon sidebands is often limited by the coarse vibrational spectrum of the largest defect supercells accessible by ab-initio electronic structure codes. In this work, we present a phonon-interpolation method for Huang-Rhys spectral densities and optical lineshape functions on hypercells created by extending the defect-containing supercells on arbitrarily dense phonon $q$-point grids. The method is based on reconstructing the transition-induced force associated with the optical excitation and using this localized force source to couple the defect transition to a densely sampled vibrational continuum. In this formulation, the local defect physics is obtained from ab initio supercell calculations, while the long-wavelength acoustic modes and the detailed structure of the host phonon spectrum are recovered by diagonalizing interpolated dynamical matrices in large hypercells. We demonstrate the method on the negatively charged nitrogen-vacancy centre in diamond between its ground $^{3}A_{2}$ and excited $^{3}E$ states. The transition-force is shown to be strongly localized around the defect, with converged localization measures obtained in a $4\times4\times4$ supercell accessible by density functional theory calculations. We interpolate the electron-phonon coupling on hypercells up to $32\times32\times32$ corresponding to approximately 17 million atoms, thereby recovering smooth, continuous Huang-Rhys spectral densities with ultrafine spectral resolution. The dominant coupling band is found near 63~meV; the low-energy acoustic contribution follows the expected linear scaling; and we recover the finer van-Hove-related structures in the optical phonon regime observed in experiments.

### [48] [Photo-induced currents and short-term memory for reservoir computing in a ferroelectric semiconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20810)

TL;DR: 本文探索利用铁电半导体ErMnO₃的光致电流实现物理储层计算（physical reservoir computing），通过其非线性光电流演化与可控弛豫动力学，自然满足储层计算所需的高维投影与衰减记忆特性。实验表明，储层变换可将对“过去”输入脉冲的识别准确率从约33%提升至约93%，证实了六方锰氧化物在光致电流储层计算中的潜力。

Method: 以ErMnO₃作为模型系统，在白光照射下测量其光致电流的非线性演化与可控弛豫动力学，利用这些特性自然实现储层计算所需的高维投影（high-dimensional projection）与衰减记忆能力。通过施加储层变换（reservoir transformation）处理输入信号，评估对“过去”（Past）输入脉冲的识别准确率。

Result: ErMnO₃在光照条件下表现出非线性演化光致电流与可控的弛豫动力学。储层变换后，对“过去”输入脉冲的识别准确率从约33%提升至约93%。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，铁电六方锰氧化物（ferroelectric hexagonal manganites）是光致电流储层计算的一个有前景的平台，突显了光驱动氧化物半导体（light-driven oxide semiconductors）在时序信息处理（temporal information processing）中的潜力。

Abstract: Physical reservoir computing represents an energy efficient approach for processing temporal signals by exploiting the intrinsic nonlinear dynamics and fading memory of a physical system. Recently, ferroelectric semiconductors moved into focus as reservoir materials motivated by their versatile electronic responses to external stimuli. Here, we explore the fundamental possibility to recognize time-varying light pulses via photo-induced currents, using the small-band-gap p-type semiconductor ErMnO$_3$ as a model system. Under white light illumination, ErMnO$_3$ exhibits non-linearly evolving photo-induced currents and controllable relaxation dynamics that naturally realize the high-dimensional projection and fading memory capabilities required for reservoir computing. The reservoir capability of ErMnO$_3$ is reflected by the improved recognition accuracy of "Past" input pulses, which increases from ~33% to ~93% after applying reservoir transformation to the input signal. The results present ferroelectric hexagonal manganites as a promising platform for photo-induced current-based reservoir computing and highlight the potential of light-driven oxide semiconductors for temporal information processing.

### [49] [MatDiffract: A Material-Informed Automated Analysis Platform for X-ray Powder Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20880)
*Hongqing Wang,Mingwei Chen,Hongjie Luo,Yin Wen,Fazhi Qi,Xuqing Chai,Miao Liu,Fengyao HOU*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: MatDiffract 是一个基于第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）数据库构建的自动化 X 射线粉末衍射（XRPD）数据分析平台，通过扰动增强模拟衍射数据库、多尺度特征嵌入、分层向量检索与全谱 Rietveld 精修相结合，实现了单相与多相混合物的高精度物相识别与定量分析，为高通量材料发现提供了端到端解决方案。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: MatDiffract 基于第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT）衍生的无机晶体结构数据库 Atomly，构建扰动增强的模拟衍射数据库；将多尺度衍射特征嵌入为可索引向量，集成分层向量检索（hierarchical vector retrieval）与全谱拟合 Rietveld 精修（Rietveld refinement）及定量物相拟合（quantitative phase fitting）。

Conclusion: MatDiffract 的模块化向量架构支持向新材料系统的无缝增量扩展，为自主材料发现与高通量材料开发中表征通量缺口（characterization throughput gap）的弥合提供了端到端解决方案。

Abstract: High-throughput experimentation and self-driving laboratories are drastically accelerating materials discovery, yet automated interpretation of X-ray powder diffraction (XRPD) data remains a critical rate-limiting step. Conventional search-match workflows rely heavily on expert manual intervention, while pure data-driven machine learning approaches suffer from limited generalizability across chemical systems and lack rigorous crystallographic interpretability. Here we present MatDiffract, a material-informed automated analysis platform for high-throughput XRPD characterization. Built on a first-principles density functional theory (DFT)-derived inorganic crystal structure database, Atomly, MatDiffract constructs a perturbation-augmented simulated diffraction database, embeds multi-scale diffraction features into indexable vectors, and integrates hierarchical vector retrieval with full-pattern fitting Rietveld refinement and quantitative phase fitting. Benchmarked on 875 single-phase experimental patterns, the platform achieves 91.3% Top-1 and 97.2% Top-10 identification accuracy after automated refinement. For binary and ternary multiphase mixtures, it delivers 85.0% and 70.0% Top-1 accuracy with mass fraction mean absolute errors as low as 1.2% and 1.8%, respectively. Beyond mere phase labeling, MatDiffract outputs full crystallographic results including refined structural models, fitted profiles, and quantitative compositions within tens of seconds per sample. Its modular vector-based architecture supports seamless incremental expansion to new material systems, providing an end-to-end solution to close the characterization throughput gap for autonomous materials discovery and high-throughput materials development.

### [50] [Long- and Short-Range Anion Order in SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$ Perovskite Oxyhydrides: DFT+$U$ Sensitivity and HSE06 Cluster Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20885)
*Tzu-chen Liu,Chris Wolverton*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文针对钙钛矿氧氢化物SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$中的阴离子有序化问题，构建了融合HSE06杂化泛函能量的团簇展开（CE）框架，发现O$_4$H$_2$顺式构型具有显著稳定性（每个氢化物约200 meV），并揭示了DFT+$U$计算对有序化能的高度敏感性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钙钛矿氧氢化物中阴离子有序化在无序状态下仍可能显著，但氢化物替代带来的构型复杂性和Ti 3$d$还原问题使得基于密度泛函理论（DFT）的精确模拟面临挑战。此外，基于团簇展开（CE）的有序化分析对DFT+$U$参数的敏感性此前未被充分探索。

Method: 作者构建了针对SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$的团簇展开框架，整合HSE06混合DFT能量。通过对比不同DFT+$U$参数下的混合能和有序化稳定性，以HSE06计算结果为基准，确定$U$ = 3.3 eV作为HSE06的代理参数，从而在限制高成本HSE06计算的同时实现广泛的构型探索。

Result: DFT+$U$计算的混合能和有序化稳定性对参数选择高度敏感，最大偏差达约100 meV/阴离子。基态有序化、八面体构型与结构稳定性之间的关联，以及CE模型的蒙特卡洛（MC）采样均支持SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$中O$_4$H$_2$顺式构型的强偏好，两个氢离子占据最近邻阴离子位点，该偏好在此前的研究中被忽视，其稳定化能约200 meV/氢化物。

Conclusion: O$_4$H$_2$顺式构型是SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$中的主导有序化模式，其稳定化能与已报道的阴离子迁移能及极化子形成能相当，揭示了该构型在氧氢化物中不可忽视的作用。本研究还强调了CE分析中DFT+$U$参数选择的重要性，为相关体系的精确模拟提供了方法学指导。

Abstract: Anion ordering in perovskite oxyhydrides can remain significant even in disordered states, particularly at non-dilute hydrogen concentrations. Nevertheless, hydride substitution poses challenges for accurate simulations based on density functional theory due to configurational complexity and Ti 3$d$ reduction. Here, we develop a cluster expansion (CE) framework for SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$ incorporating HSE06 hybrid-DFT energetics. We first demonstrate that calculated mixing energies and ordering stability are highly sensitive to the choice of DFT+$U$, with maximum variations on the order of 100 meV/anion. We benchmark ordering energetics against HSE06 calculations and identify $U$ = 3.3 eV as an HSE06 proxy, which enables extensive configurational exploration while limiting costly HSE06 calculations to key configurations for efficient learning of ordering energetics. Together, ground-state orderings, correlations between octahedral configurations and structural stability, and MC sampling of CE models all support a strong preference for the O$_4$H$_2$ cis configuration in SrTiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$, in which two hydride ions occupy first-nearest-neighbor anion sites. This cis-type preference was overlooked in previous ATiO$_{3-x}$H$_x$ studies, despite its sizable stabilization of ~200 meV per hydride comparable to reported anion-migration and polaron-formation energies. This study addresses both the previously underexplored sensitivity of CE-based ordering analyses to DFT+$U$ and anion-ordering in perovskite oxyhydrides.

### [51] [Orbital Hall Effect Enables Field-Free Magnetization Reversal in Ferrimagnets without Additional Conversion Layer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20888)

Abstract: The spin Hall effect provides a well-established route for electrical magnetization control, while the orbital Hall effect offers a powerful yet less explored source of angular momentum. Achieving field-free deterministic switching in straightforward orbital-torque architectures remains challenging. Here, we demonstrate orbital-Hall-current-driven switching in a Mo/CoGd bilayer without the need for a separate orbital-to-spin conversion layer across a wide temperature range. In this simplified geometry, Mo serves as both an orbital and spin current source. Abstract: Microwaves provide coherent access to low-energy excitations and serve as effective probes of high-frequency spin dynamics in quantum and magnetic systems. Here we use time-resolved Lorentz transmission electron microscopy to visualize microwave-driven dynamics in a hybrid antiskyrmion structure composed of a central antiskyrmion and surface skyrmions. ### [53] [Uni-XAS: Alignment-Driven Bidirectional Multimodal Learning for X-ray Absorption Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20906)
*Suyang Zhong,Yuhao Zhao,Boying Huang,Fanjie Xu,Pengwei Xu,Haoyi Tao,Xi Fang,Jun Cheng,Fujie Tang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出Uni-XAS，一个统一的基准和学习框架，将X射线吸收光谱（XAS）与3D原子结构之间的双向建模重新定义为跨模态对齐与条件生成问题，通过XASLip对齐策略、检索增强解码和置换整流流匹配（Permutation-Rectified Flow Matching）等方法，在包含328,839个结构-光谱对的大规模基准上实现了跨模态检索、绝对光谱预测和成分条件3D结构生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: X射线吸收光谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy, XAS）是探测局域原子环境的关键技术，但基于学习的建模需要弥合一维连续光谱与三维原子结构这两种异质模态之间的鸿沟。现有方法通常将前向光谱预测和反向结构推断解耦为独立的回归任务，阻碍了共享表征学习；此外，相同原子间严重的置换模糊性（permutation ambiguity）使得逆建模局限于粗粒度的结构描述符，难以生成显式的3D结构。

Method: Uni-XAS框架包含三个核心组件：1) XASLip对齐策略，结合物理感知光谱编码器（physics-aware spectral encoder）与吸收体感知流形优化（absorber-aware manifold optimization）以解析细粒度的元素内配位变化；2) 前向预测通过检索增强解码（retrieval-augmented decoding）实现锚定绝对光谱生成，防止物理尺度坍塌和能量漂移；3) 针对病态逆问题，提出置换整流流匹配（Permutation-Rectified Flow Matching），将类型级最优传输（type-wise optimal transport）集成到连续生成流中，在不依赖高阶等变架构的前提下解决配体置换模糊性。

Result: 在包含328,839个结构-光谱对的大规模标准化基准上，Uni-XAS在跨模态检索、精确绝对光谱预测和成分条件3D结构生成任务中均展现出强劲性能。

Conclusion: Uni-XAS为科学光谱学中的多模态学习和标准化评估建立了一个可扩展、可复现且协议一致的基准框架。

Abstract: X-ray absorption spectroscopy (XAS) is a key technique for probing local atomic environments, yet learning based modeling must bridge two heterogeneous modalities: 1D continuous spectra and 3D atomic structures. Existing approaches typically decouple forward spectrum prediction and inverse structure inference into separate regression tasks, hindering shared representation learning. Moreover, severe permutation ambiguity among identical atoms often limits inverse modeling to coarse structure descriptors rather than explicit 3D structure generation. In this work, we present Uni-XAS, a unified benchmark and learning framework that reframes bidirectional XAS modeling as a cross-modal alignment and conditional generation problem. We first propose XASLip, an alignment recipe coupling a physics-aware spectral encoder with an absorberaware manifold optimization strategy to resolve fine-grained intra-element coordination variations. Building upon this shared latent space, we formulate forward prediction as anchored absolute-spectrum generation via retrieval-augmented decoding, effectively preventing physical scale collapse and energy drift. For the inherently ill-posed inverse problem, we introduce Permutation-Rectified Flow Matching, which integrates type-wise optimal transport into a continuous generative flow to provide a principled solution to ligand permutation ambiguity without relying on heavy high-order equivariant architectures. Evaluated on a largescale standardized benchmark of 328,839 structure-spectrum pairs, Uni-XAS demonstrates strong performance in cross-modal retrieval, accurate absolute-spectrum prediction, and composition-conditional 3D structure generation, establishing a scalable, reproducible, and protocol-consistent foundation for multimodal learning and standardized evaluation in scientific spectroscopy.

Based on the analysis of the tunneling transport, the TMR effect is attributed to the spin polarized tunneling transport with momentum dependence and the interfacial magnetic structures, as well as the spin-polarized electric current in a bulk form of $\mathrm{Ru}_{1-x}\mathrm{Cr}_{x}\mathrm{O}_{2}(110)$.

### [57] [Machine learning based prediction of optical properties in two-dimensional Mo-W-S-Se-Te transition-metal dichalcogenide alloys through physics-informed sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21246)

Abstract: Two-dimensional transition-metal dichalcogenide (TMD) alloys provide a compositionally tunable platform for controlling the optical and electronic properties. However, systematic prediction of their dielectric response across multicomponent alloy spaces remains challenging owing to the combinatorial cost of first-principles calculations. In this work, we combined ab initio optical-property calculations with a tabular foundation-model regression to predict the real and imaginary components of the frequency-dependent dielectric function for Mo-W-S-Se-Te TMD alloys.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属铂是催化剂、电子材料及5d过渡金属体系中的重要元素，但此前缺乏对其中浅层与深层芯态能级谱线形状不对称性、卫星结构及相对论效应的系统性光谱学表征，需要建立统一且自洽的参考基准以支持相关材料的谱学解析。

Method: 采用RHEELS、SXPS和HAXPES三种互补实验手段，结合基于密度泛函理论（DFT）和G0W0方法的ab initio计算，对Pt的芯态及价带电子结构进行系统表征；通过对比光电子卫星结构与RHEELS损失特征，鉴定跃迁类型和等离激元（plasmon）模式。

Result: 识别并讨论了多个此前未被解析的卫星特征和自旋-轨道分裂（spin-orbit splitting）；实验价带谱与含/不含自旋-轨道耦合的DFT及G0W0计算的轨道投影态密度（projected density of states）对比表明，相对论效应（relativistic effects）对准确再现Pt价电子结构至关重要。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了金属铂的统一且内部自洽的光谱学参考基准，为含铂催化剂、电子材料及相关5d过渡金属体系的光电子能谱解析提供了稳健的框架。

Abstract: This work presents a comprehensive investigation of the electronic structure and many-body photoemission effects in metallic platinum using reflection high-energy electron energy-loss spec- troscopy (RHEELS), soft X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (SXPS), and hard X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (HAXPES), supported by ab initio calculations. Shallow and deep core state spectra enable the systematic characterisation of intrinsic line-shape asymmetries and satellite structures. Correlation of photoelectron satellites with RHEELS loss features allows the assignment of inter- band transitions, surface and bulk plasmons, plasmonic overtones, and semi-core ionisation losses across the Pt spectrum. Several previously unresolved satellite features and spin-orbit splittings are identified and discussed. Comparison of experimental valence band spectra with orbital-projected densities of states calculated using ab initio density functional theory (DFT) and G0W0 approaches, with and without spin-orbit coupling, demonstrates the critical role of relativistic effects in reproducing the Pt valence electronic structure. Together, these results establish a unified, internally consistent spectroscopic reference for metallic platinum, providing a robust framework for interpreting photoelectron spectra of Pt-containing catalysts, electronic materials, and related 5d transition metal systems.

### [59] [Gauge Auxiliary-Field Quantum Monte Carlo Method for Many-Fermion Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20917)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将高斯相空间量子蒙特卡洛（Gaussian phase-space QMC）中的随机规范自由度融入无相位辅助场量子蒙特卡洛（phaseless AFQMC）框架；将传统力偏差（force bias）重新解释为漂移规范（drift gauge）；基于混合估计子（mixed estimator）构建约化单粒子密度矩阵（reduced one-body density matrix）的自然轨道（natural orbitals），从而引入费米规范（Fermi gauges），产生随机的、含时类哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）动力学；并提出对称性投影采样（symmetry-projection sampling）方案以提高采样效率。

Result: 在 Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick 模型上的数值结果表明，随机规范（stochastic gauges）能够提升计算精度并降低统计涨落。

Abstract: We propose novel Quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) methods for interacting many-fermion systems by leveraging the stochastic gauge freedom, originally developed in Gaussian phase-space QMC, within the phaseless auxiliary-field QMC (AFQMC) framework. In particular, we reinterpret the conventional force bias in phaseless AFQMC as a drift gauge and explore Fermi gauges based on natural orbitals of a reduced one-body density matrix defined via a mixed estimator, yielding stochastic, time-dependent Hartree-Fock-like dynamics. We propose a symmetry-projection sampling scheme to enhance the sampling efficiency. As a proof of concept, we apply these gauge-augmented AFQMC methods to a simple shell-model Hamiltonian: the Lipkin-Meshkov-Glick model. Numerical results illustrate the potential of stochastic gauges to enhance accuracy and reduce fluctuations, underscoring the promise for advancing these new techniques toward more realistic shell-model applications.

### [60] [Tensor resonances in teleparallel Gauss-Bonnet branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20567)

Method: 采用一阶形式论（first-order formalism），由 sine-Gordon 超势生成解析厚膜解；推导膜分裂的解析条件，结合张量稳定性分析确定物理可行参数区域。

Result: 张量谱无快子模，存在可归一化的引力子零模；有质量谱段中奇宇称引力共振在稳定性边界附近出现准局域化（quasi-localization）显著增强。

Conclusion: 在遥平行高斯-博内膜世界中，膜分裂、张量稳定性与引力共振三者之间存在直接的关联。

Abstract: We construct an analytical thick-brane solution in linear teleparallel Gauss-Bonnet gravity using a first-order formalism generated by a sine-Gordon superpotential. The resulting asymptotically $\mathrm{AdS}_5$ configurations exhibit brane splitting controlled by the dimensionless parameter $q=4αk^2$. An analytical splitting condition is derived and combined with tensor-stability requirements to identify the physically viable parameter region. We show that the tensor spectrum is free of tachyonic instabilities and supports a normalizable graviton zero mode. The massive sector exhibits odd-parity gravitational resonances whose quasi-localization is significantly enhanced near the stability boundary. Our results establish a direct link between brane splitting, tensor stability, and gravitational resonances in teleparallel Gauss-Bonnet braneworlds.

### [61] [Moduli-Space Laplacians, Asymptotic Geometry, and the Emergent String Conjecture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20603)

Method: 采用理论论证，将最轻粒子塔的质量表述为模空间拉普拉斯算子的本征函数，并利用涌现弦猜想约束本征值的量子化行为；同时通过多个超对称程度不同的例子（涵盖4到32个超对称荷）进行验证。

Result: 最轻粒子塔的质量本征值由涌现弦猜想决定其量子化，该本征值同时控制渐近极限下轴子方向的指数衰减率，并与瞬子谱的量子化条件相关联。

Conclusion: 模空间拉普拉斯本征值的量子化结构为理解量子引力中粒子塔、轴子衰变和瞬子谱之间的统一图景提供了新视角。

Abstract: At asymptotic limits of moduli spaces of quantum gravity vacua, we argue that the masses of the lightest particle towers are eigenfunctions of the moduli-space Laplacian. The associated eigenvalues are quantized by the Emergent String Conjecture and determine the exponential decay rates of axionic directions in these limits. We also connect the quantization of Laplacian eigenvalues to the spectrum of instantons for the theory. We support our claims with diverse examples that preserve between 4 and 32 supercharges.

### [62] [Towards Generalized Dimers for GTPs: $\mathcal{N}=2$ Fractional Branes at Infinite Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20607)
*Sebastián Franco,Diego Rodríguez-Gómez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将广义环面多边形（GTPs）与相应的箭图理论（quiver theories）及膜铺砌（brane tilings）联系起来的方法，通过引入$\mathcal{N}=2$条带凝聚（strip condensation）机制，将GTPs中多条5-膜终止于同一7-膜的特征转化为平行曲折路径（zig-zag paths）的合并，从而在镜像对称（mirror symmetry）框架下解释了GTPs与普通环面图（toric diagrams）之间通过多胞体突变（polytope mutations）建立的对应关系，并验证了该机制对规范群数目、无穷耦合极限以及相关形变（relevant deformations）的正确预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义环面多边形（GTPs）将5维超共形场论（$5d$ SCFTs）的几何实现从传统的环面Calabi-Yau 3-流形推广到包含终止于7-膜的$(p,q)$ 5-膜网络，但GTPs对应的膜铺砌与箭图理论尚未建立完整的推广框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立GTPs与箭图理论之间的系统对应。

Method: 聚焦于通过与多胞体突变（polytope mutations）相联系的GTPs，利用平行5-膜腿定义的$\mathcal{N}=2$分式膜（fractional branes）及其对应的平行曲折路径（zig-zag paths）构建膜铺砌。提出$\mathcal{N}=2$条带凝聚（strip condensation）机制，即将多条5-膜终止于同一7-膜的行为等价为将这些曲折路径合并、致使相应$\mathcal{N}=2$分式膜收缩至零尺寸。通过将牛顿多项式（Newton polynomial）系数调至GTP点，从镜像对称（mirror symmetry）推导条带凝聚，并通过多个非平凡自洽性检验验证该机制。

Result: 条带凝聚正确再现了预期的规范群数目，该数目等价于突变相关环面图的规范群数目，或GTP铺砌中$T$-锥（$T$-cones）的数目。该结果在所有已有文献案例以及一个包含任意大$T$-锥的无穷新GTP族上得到验证。条带凝聚将相应规范群驱动至无穷耦合，随后形成的禁闭（confinement）产生与突变相关环面图的箭图仅相差矢量对（vector pairs）和阿德约场（adjoint fields）的箭图，表明GTP箭图可通过相关形变（relevant deformations）与相应环面图的箭图相联系。

Conclusion: 本文建立了GTPs与膜铺砌及箭图理论之间的系统对应关系，将多胞体突变与相关形变之间的已知对应推广到了GTPs范畴，为理解5维超共形场论在更一般几何背景下的实现提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Generalized Toric Polygons (GTPs) extend the geometric realization of $5d$ superconformal field theories beyond toric Calabi-Yau 3-folds to general $(p,q)$ 5-brane webs ending on 7-branes. We take significant steps towards the generalization of brane tilings for GTPs, or equivalently, the corresponding quiver theories. We focus on GTPs connected to ordinary toric diagrams by polytope mutations. Parallel 5-brane legs of a $(p,q)$ web define $\mathcal{N}=2$ fractional branes bounded by the corresponding parallel zig-zag paths in the brane tiling obtained by treating the GTP as an ordinary toric diagram. We propose that terminating multiple 5-branes on a common 7-brane, the defining feature of GTPs, translates into bringing these zig-zag paths together, thereby shrinking the corresponding $\mathcal{N}=2$ fractional branes to zero size in a process we call $\mathcal{N}=2$ strip condensation. We show that strip condensation follows from mirror symmetry when the coefficients in the Newton polynomial are tuned to the GTP point. We further support this proposal through several non-trivial consistency checks. In particular, it correctly reproduces the expected number of gauge groups, given equivalently by that of the mutation-related toric diagram or by the number of $T$-cones in a tessellation of the GTP. We verify this for all examples previously considered in the literature, as well as for a new infinite family of GTPs with arbitrarily large $T$-cones. Strip condensation drives the corresponding gauge groups to infinite coupling. Confinement then yields quivers that coincide with those of the mutation-related toric diagrams up to vector pairs and adjoint fields, suggesting that GTP quivers are related to those of the corresponding toric diagrams by relevant deformations, extending to GTPs the known correspondence between polytope mutations and relevant deformations.

</details>


### [63] [New Type IIB Poly-instanton Effects and Axion Quintessence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20613)

Main category: hep-th

<details>

Method: 通过对瞬子零模进行一般性分析，研究刚性循环存在形变时的情形，同时要求O3-平面局域化在欧几里得D3-膜的世界体积上；并提供具体的卡拉比-丘例子及显式的定向折对合（orientifold involution）和膜组态（brane setup）。

Result: 发现了当刚性循环存在形变且O3-平面局域化在欧几里得D3-膜的世界体积上时，存在新型的多重瞬子效应；给出了具体的卡拉比-丘例子，其中一例特别适合描述轴子山顶精粹模型；多重瞬子效应的双指数压制（double exponential suppression）可以在自然参数值下再现观测到的真空能（vacuum energy）。

Conclusion: 研究发现了新型多重瞬子效应，并提供了具体的弦论实现，其中双指数压制机制使得轴子山顶精粹模型能够以自然参数值解释观测真空能。

Abstract: Previous studies of poly-instantons in type IIB Calabi-Yau orientifolds found that these effects arise when Euclidean D3-branes wrap rigid cycles with a Wilson line. In this work, we extend this result through a general analysis of instanton zero modes, revealing the existence of new poly-instanton effects for rigid cycles with a deformation, provided that O3-planes are localised on the worldvolume of the Euclidean D3-brane. We provide concrete Calabi-Yau examples with explicit orientifold involution and brane setup. One of them is particularly well suited for realising axion hilltop quintessence. In particular, the double exponential suppression of poly-instanton effects allows to reproduce the observed vacuum energy for natural values of the underlying parameters.

### [64] [Sp(4,Z) actions on 3d U(1)^2 symmetric theories: Order-five duality and bilayer quantum Hall hierarchies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20622)
*Yasin F. Alam,Andreas Karch,Da-Chuan Lu,Ryan C. Spieler*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将4维Maxwell理论的SL(2,Z)电磁对偶性所诱导的边界理论生成操作从单U(1)情形推广到U(1)^2情形，并探索其在双层分数量子霍尔系统中的应用，特别是推广Haldane–Halperin层级构造以产生新的候选分数量子霍尔态。

Method: 通过构造体态Sp(4,Z)作用并推导对应的边界操作，利用K-矩阵形式论（K-matrix formalism）实现阿贝尔Chern-Simons理论的理论生成网络，并将Haldane–Halperin层级构造重新表述为SL(2,Z)操作的序列，推广至具有电荷U(1)_c和赝自旋U(1)_s对称性的双层系统。

Result: 识别出一个五阶本征二元元素（推广了单U(1)理论中的三阶ST元素），其边界操作闭合时需伴随解耦的U(1)_1可逆相，暗示混合对偶-引力反常（mixed duality-gravitational anomaly）。在双层层级构造中得到了包含层间关联玻色子(221)子代分支的候选阿贝尔态，对应偶数分母等层填充3/8+3/8和5/12+5/12，并通过任意子基的整数变换证明了这些态与相应阿贝尔复合费米子描述的等价性。

Conclusion: 建立了U(1)^2对称性下体态-边界对偶操作的理论框架，揭示了混合对偶-引力反常的存在，并将该形式应用于双层分数量子霍尔系统，推广了Haldane–Halperin层级构造，提出了新的偶数分母填充候选态及其与复合费米子描述的等价关系，同时讨论了将电磁背景场视为自旋-c联络时的自旋-电荷约束。

Abstract: The $\mathrm{SL}(2,\mathbb{Z})$ electromagnetic duality of 4d Maxwell theory induces theory-generating operations on 3d theories with $U(1)$ global symmetry. For theories with $U(1)^n$ symmetry, this structure generalizes to $\mathrm{Sp}(2n,\mathbb{Z})$. Focusing on the $U(1)^2$ case, we formulate the bulk $\mathrm{Sp}(4,\mathbb{Z})$ action and derive the corresponding boundary operations. We identify an intrinsically two-component element of order five, which generalizes the order-three $ST$ element of the single-$U(1)$ theory. Although its fifth power acts trivially in the bulk, the corresponding boundary operation closes only up to a decoupled $U(1)_1$ invertible phase, suggesting a mixed duality-gravitational anomaly. We realize the resulting theory-generating web for Abelian Chern-Simons theories within the $K$-matrix formalism and apply it to bilayer fractional quantum Hall systems. Recasting the Haldane--Halperin hierarchy construction as a sequence of $\mathrm{SL}(2,\mathbb{Z})$ operations, we generalize it to systems with charge $U(1)_c$ and pseudospin $U(1)_s$ symmetries. The resulting bilayer hierarchies contain branches terminating in an interlayer-correlated bosonic $(221)$ daughter sector, yielding candidate Abelian states at the even-denominator equal-layer fillings $3/8+3/8$ and $5/12+5/12$. Integral changes of anyon basis establish the equivalence of these states to their corresponding Abelian composite-fermion descriptions. We further discuss the spin-charge constraints that arise when the electromagnetic background field is treated as a spin-$c$ connection.

### [65] [Uniqueness of null-local modular flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20678)
*Gautam Satishchandran,Jonathan Sorce*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究零曲面（null slice）上量子场论态的瞬时局域模流（instantaneously local modular flow），发现其受到高度约束：紫外普适性（ultraviolet universality）要求零局域模流几乎是唯一的。作者在闵可夫斯基时空的无质量Klein-Gordon理论中构造了一类具有任意正则未来指向向量场作为瞬时模流的状态，并证明该类中任意两个不同状态不可能存在于同一局域希尔伯特空间（local Hilbert space）中。此外，在真空扇区（vacuum sector）中，因果钻石（causal diamond）内唯一的零局域模流由真空态本身提供。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前arXiv:2306.01837猜想可以构造一大类具有空间切片上“瞬时局域”模流的量子场论态。本文旨在检验该猜想在零曲面情形下的可行性，并揭示其基本约束。

Method: 采用无质量Klein-Gordon理论的显式计算，在闵可夫斯基时空中因果钻石的过去零边界（past null boundary）上对任意足够规则的正则未来指向向量场构造相应状态；利用局域希尔伯特空间的不相容性论证以及真空扇区中的抽象推理。

Result: 1) 对任意足够规则的正则未来指向向量场，可以构造一个以该向量场为瞬时模流的状态；2) 该类中任意两个不同状态无法在同一个局域希尔伯特空间中实现；3) 在真空扇区中，因果钻石内唯一的零局域模流来自真空态本身。

Conclusion: 零曲面上的瞬时局域模流受到强烈约束，远不如空间切片情形自由；该结果也推广到有质量标量场、自由Maxwell场、自由引力子以及弯曲背景。

Abstract: In arXiv:2306.01837, it was conjectured that one can engineer a large class of quantum field theory states for which the modular flow on a spacelike slice is "instantaneously local." Here we show that on null slices, such flows are highly constrained; ultraviolet universality essentially requires null-local modular flow to be unique. Concretely, we study massless Klein-Gordon theory in Minkowski spacetime, and construct, for any sufficiently regular future-directed vector field on the past null boundary of a causal diamond, a state that has this vector field as its instantaneous modular flow. We then show by explicit computation that no two distinct states in this class can be realized in the same local Hilbert space. Using a more abstract argument, we also show that in the vacuum sector of the theory, the only null-local modular flow in a causal diamond is provided by the vacuum state itself. We also comment on the construction of null-local modular flow for massive scalars, free Maxwell fields, free gravitons, and in curved backgrounds.

</details>


### [66] [Flux Vacua Near the Boundary of Large Complex Structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20777)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于通量真空系综（flux vacuum ensemble）进行统计分析，在复结构模量空间（moduli space）中比较微扰势能与首个瞬子贡献的数值大小，评估高阶瞬子效应的可忽略性。

Result: 当通量配置使得某些模量方向上微扰势的幅度与首个瞬子贡献相当时，真空最小值主要由微扰项与首个瞬子修正决定，更高阶瞬子贡献可忽略；该现象在通量真空系综中统计上相当常见；此外还发现瞬子项可改变解的多重性并诱发单值性平移。

Conclusion: 在大复结构边界附近，三形式通量诱导的势能可以通过微扰项与首个瞬子修正有效描述，忽略高阶瞬子效应的近似在统计上是合理的；瞬子修正还可能对解的结构和模空间拓扑性质产生更复杂的非微扰影响。

Abstract: Three-form fluxes generate a potential for the complex structure moduli in type IIB string compactifications on Calabi-Yau threefolds. In the large complex structure patch, the potential consists of a perturbative contribution and a convergent series of instanton corrections. We present examples of vacua near the boundary of large complex structure, where the minimum of the potential is essentially determined by the perturbative contribution and the first instanton correction, while the effect of all higher instantons is negligible. This phenomenon occurs when fluxes are such that the magnitude of the perturbative potential in certain directions in moduli space is of the same size as the first instanton contribution. Analysing an ensemble of flux vacua, we find that this phenomenon is statistically quite common. We also discover more subtle phenomena where instanton terms affect the multiplicity of the solutions and induce monodromy shifts.

### [67] [Quantum Mpemba effect in holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20899)
*Xian-Hui Ge,Shuta Ishigaki,Yu-Qi Lei,Yu Tian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究在全息超流体（holographic superfluid）中发现了量子姆潘巴效应（quantum Mpemba effect），即初始对称性破缺更强的态反而更快地弛豫到对称性恢复的平衡态。通过将能流进入黑洞视界（black hole horizon）计算得到的 shifted 自由能作为单调距离度量，并结合准正则模（quasinormal modes）对非线性体动力学（nonlinear bulk dynamics）进行分解，揭示了该反常弛豫由一种动力学竞争机制主导：最慢衰减模式被抑制，而第二慢模式被放大。这些发现为涉及强耦合自由度的非平衡弛豫中的量子姆潘巴效应提供了全息视角。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机是探索量子姆潘巴效应在强耦合体系（strongly coupled systems）中的表现机制，该效应描述了初始对称性破缺更强的态反而更快地恢复对称性，是一种违反直觉的非平衡弛豫（nonequilibrium relaxation）现象。

Method: 采用全息对偶（holographic duality）方法构建超流体模型，将能量流入黑洞视界导出的 shifted 自由能作为刻画弛豫过程的单调距离度量；并利用准正则模分解非线性体动力学，分析弛豫过程中不同模式的贡献变化。

Result: 结果表明量子姆潘巴效应确实存在于全息超流体中；弛豫异常由动力学竞争主导，具体表现为最慢衰减模式受到抑制，而第二慢衰减模式被放大。

Conclusion: 该工作为理解强耦合体系中量子姆潘巴效应的起源提供了全息视角，揭示了准正则模之间的动力学竞争是产生反常弛豫的关键机制。

Abstract: We investigate the quantum Mpemba effect in a holographic superfluid, in which states with stronger initial symmetry breaking relax faster toward the symmetry-restored equilibrium. We demonstrate its emergence by identifying the shifted free energy computed from the energy flux into the black hole horizon as monotonic distance measure. By decomposing the nonlinear bulk dynamics based on quasinormal modes, we reveal that the anomalous relaxation is governed by a dynamical competition in which the slowest-decaying mode is suppressed while the second mode is amplified. These findings provide a holographic perspective on the quantum Mpemba effect in nonequilibrium relaxation involving strongly coupled degrees of freedom.

### [68] [Coherent states versus Glauber-Sudarshan States: Bootstrapping, Schwinger-Keldysh Contours and Lefschetz Thimbles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20927)
*Heliudson Bernardo,Tatsuya Daniel,Keshav Dasgupta,Brayden Hull,Yue Katherine Lei,Yiya Selina Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文研究在四维微分同胚不变理论（four-dimensional diffeomorphism-invariant theory）中，如何构造瞬态激发态（Glauber-Sudarshan态），并分析其与相干态的区别、在多种有效作用量框架下的一致性、引导场（gauge-fixing）与鬼影（ghost）部分中的自举关系（bootstrap relation），以及它们在Wheeler-DeWitt方程和量子引力中时间概念的角色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高约束系统（如具有零体哈密顿量且度规与额外自由度存在非平凡相互作用的四维微分同胚不变理论）中，通常难以构造非超对称且具有正能量的激发态；本文旨在利用Glauber-Sudarshan态构造此类瞬态激发，并系统研究其动力学与结构一致性。

Method: 采用正则形式（canonical formalism）和边界哈密顿量（boundary Hamiltonian）以及in-in路径积分（Schwinger-Keldysh contour）分析时间演化；通过1PI有效作用量、Wilson有效作用量（Wilsonian/exact renormalization group effective action）以及Picard-Lefschetz（Lefschetz-thimble）分解三种互补描述验证构造一致性；引入自举关系（bootstrap relation）约束瞬态构型在超对称闵可夫斯基真空（supersymmetric Minkowski vacuum）和准de Sitter轨迹附近的行为。

Result: Glauber-Sudarshan态通常是非超对称的（non-supersymmetric），虽非势能极小值（minima of any potential），但允许具备正能量的度规构型，可有效模拟四维准de Sitter背景（quasi-de Sitter background）。在引导场和鬼影存在下，这些瞬态构型的动力学由非平凡的自举关系控制。此外，Wheeler-DeWitt方程和体薛定谔方程（bulk Schrödinger equation）得以自然出现，且该构造与弦论（string theory）二维世界面（world-sheet）中的顶点算符（vertex operator）具有结构类比。

Conclusion: 瞬态激发的Glauber-Sudarshan态为高度约束引力理论中构造正能量背景提供了一种系统方法，其动力学行为可通过多种有效作用量框架一致描述，且与弦论中的顶点算符结构类似，暗示深层理论联系。

Abstract: We investigate how, in a highly constrained system such as a four-dimensional diffeomorphism-invariant theory with vanishing bulk Hamiltonian and non-trivial interactions between the metric and additional degrees of freedom, transient excited states--called Glauber-Sudarshan states--can be constructed over supersymmetric minima. These states are generically non-supersymmetric and, although they are not minima of any potential, they admit positive-energy metric configurations that effectively mimic four-dimensional quasi-de Sitter backgrounds. We analyze how such states differ from conventional coherent states by studying their time evolution both in the canonical formalism--via boundary Hamiltonians--and in the in-in path-integral framework through Schwinger-Keldysh contours. We also examine the consistency of the construction across three complementary descriptions: the 1PI effective action, the Wilsonian (or exact renormalization group) effective action, and the Picard-Lefschetz (Lefschetz-thimble) decomposition of the Schwinger-Keldysh path integral, which provides the trans-series organization of the theory. In the presence of gauge-fixing and ghost sectors, we show that the dynamics of these transient configurations are governed by a nontrivial bootstrap relation that simultaneously constrains their behavior near supersymmetric Minkowski vacua and along quasi-de Sitter-like trajectories. Finally, we examine the Wheeler-DeWitt equation, the notion of time in the presence of transient excited states, and the emergence of the bulk Schrodinger equation. We further show that these states admit a natural structural interpretation analogous to the vertex operators that arise in the two-dimensional world-sheet formulation of string theory.

</details>


### [69] [Boundary Completion of Vacuum Persistence Probability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20936)
*Yu Zhou,Hai-Qing Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文指出，计算真空持续概率时，Bogoliubov方案与格林函数方案给出的表达式看似不一致，但该歧义源于格林函数方案忽略了端点真空波函数泛函（endpoint vacuum wavefunctionals）的贡献。通过包含该贡献完成边界补全（boundary completion），两种方案的结果得以统一，且最终结果与Bogoliubov表达式一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真空持续概率（vacuum persistence probability）是衡量真空不稳定性（vacuum instability）和粒子产生（particle production）的基本指标，但其在计算中可能因采用不同方案（Bogoliubov方案与格林函数方案）而出现表达式不一致的问题。本文旨在解释并消除这一表观歧义。

Method: 通过分析两种方案（Bogoliubov prescription 与 Green's function prescription）的数学结构，揭示格林函数方案遗漏了端点真空波函数泛函（endpoint vacuum wavefunctionals）的非平凡贡献。将该贡献纳入完整的in-out振幅后，完成格林函数方案的边界补全（boundary completion），从而与Bogoliubov方案的结果比较。

Result: 发现格林函数方案因忽略端点真空波函数泛函而导致表达式不同；纳入该贡献后，边界补全使得两种方案的结果达成一致，完整结果与Bogoliubov表达式相同。

Conclusion: 真空持续概率计算中的表观歧义得以消除，其根源在于格林函数方案缺乏完整的边界项。修正后的结果统一于Bogoliubov方案的表达式。

Abstract: The vacuum persistence probability, encoded in the imaginary part of the in-out effective action, is a basic measure of vacuum instability and particle production. However, its evaluation may appear prescription-dependent: the Bogoliubov prescription and the Green's function prescription can yield different expressions. We show that this apparent ambiguity arises because the Green's function prescription omits the nontrivial contribution from the endpoint vacuum wavefunctionals, which should be present in the complete in-out amplitude. Including this contribution accomplishes the boundary completion of the Green's function prescription. The ambiguity is thereby resolved, and the complete result agrees with the Bogoliubov expression.

Conclusion: 标准流体动力学的适用范围可以超越传统的低频低温极限，扩展到温度远低于频率和波数的扩展流体动力学区域；全息乘积公式为非阿贝尔系统提供了一个有效的扩展流体动力学近似方案。

The two-point correlators of charged currents are then computed holographically at finite quark and isospin chemical potentials. In the near-extremal hydrodynamic regime, $ω, k, T, μ_3 \ll μ\equiv \sqrt{μ_q^2+μ_3^2}$, relevant for cold strongly coupled matter, the IR properties of the correlators are studied. It is shown that in this regime, the correlators agree with the non-Abelian hydrodynamic predictions. Therefore, the traditional regime of validity of standard hydrodynamics extends beyond $ω, k \ll T \ll μ$ to the so-called extended hydrodynamic regime $T\ll ω, k \ll μ$. The holographic product formula is applied to the present non-Abelian system, and is used to propose an extended hydrodynamic approximation capturing both hydrodynamic-like poles and the leading effect of AdS$_2$ poles, by resumming the low-$ω$ logarithms. The results are verified through a detailed numerical analysis of the exact correlators and quasi-normal mode spectrum.

Abstract: Complex extremal surfaces naturally arise in holographic observables associated with timelike subregions in AdS/CFT and with holographic observables in dS/CFT, but their integration contours are generally ambiguous. In this work, we propose a method for constructing complex bulk metrics from families of complex extremal surfaces, thereby generating candidate complex geometries relevant to the gravitational path integral. This construction provides a concrete realization of how complex bulk geometry may emerge from timelike entanglement, extending the familiar idea that spacetime geometry is encoded in quantum entanglement. We use the Kontsevich--Segal--Witten (KSW) criterion as a strong consistency condition to constrain the corresponding contours. The same framework also explains why spacelike entanglement naturally selects a real Lorentzian section. In several AdS and dS examples, the KSW condition uniquely determines the admissible contour within the class considered. We also identify configurations for which the resulting complex geometry violates the KSW bound near the asymptotic boundary, revealing both the scope and the limitations of the construction. These results highlight KSW admissibility as a useful organizing principle for complex saddles in real-time holography.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Randall-Sundrum II膜世界模型，并在体时空（bulk）中引入p-膜气体（p-brane gas），以在膜（brane）上局域化地描述多种物质主导的宇宙学场景。利用Grinberg与Maldacena提出的测地线公式（geodesic formula）计算大量子算符的热单点函数，并通过第二Israel连接条件（second Israel junction condition）导出膜随时间演化的径向位置。

Result: 得到了不同物质主导宇宙（包括单组分和多组分场景）中大量子算符的时间依赖热单点函数，这些函数由膜的演化径向位置导出。同时，分析了早期和晚期宇宙中该热单点函数的具体渐近行为。

Conclusion: 本文在膜世界框架下成功计算了膨胀宇宙中大量子算符的时变热单点函数，揭示了不同物质主导阶段对该函数的影响，为后续在弯曲时空背景下研究热关联函数的动力学提供了理论工具。

Abstract: In this article, we have calculated the time-dependent thermal one-point function of massive operators within an expanding universe. We employ the Randall-Sundrum II braneworld model combined with a $p$-brane gas in the bulk, enabling us to represent various matter-dominated cosmological scenarios localised on the brane. Applying the geodesic formula introduced by Grinberg and Maldacena in \cite{Grinberg:2020fdj}, we have calculated the thermal one-point functions of massive operators within the universe. The time-dependent one-point functions for different matter-dominated universes, both single-component and multi-component, are derived from the brane's evolving radial position. The time-dependent positions of the branes have been obtained using the second Israel junction condition. Additionally, we have analyzed the early and late-time behaviors of the thermal one-point function across various matter-dominated universes.

Abstract: We study energy-energy correlators (EEC) in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory at strong 't Hooft coupling $λ$. We consider the EEC in states created by half-BPS operators of arbitrary dimension $p$, and determine the corresponding event-shape function up to order $λ^{-3/2}$ from the worldsheet representation of the AdS Virasoro-Shapiro amplitude with Kaluza-Klein external states. Abstract: We study the defect contribution to the entanglement entropy of a spherical region centred on four-dimensional superconformal RG interfaces. These interfaces are supersymmetric codimension one defects separating the Leigh--Strassler SCFT vacuum and the $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM theory deformed by spatially varying mass terms. Exploiting the holographic dual to these interfaces, we extract a cutoff-independent interface contribution to the entanglement entropy, $\mathcal{C}^I$. ### [79] [High-Order Pole-Skipping in Near-Extremal Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21386)
*Xiang Li,Haiming Yuan,Xian-Hui Ge*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种系统性的解析方法，用于研究近极端全息黑洞（near-extremal holographic black holes）中的高阶极点跳跃（high-order pole-skipping）。在近极端极限 $T\to 0$ 下，近视界几何呈现 $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times \mathbb{R}^{d-1}$ 结构，模式指标 $q$ 被识别为涌现的 $\mathrm{AdS}_2/\mathrm{CFT}_1$ 对应中的红外共形维数（IR conformal dimension）$\Delta_{\mathrm{IR}} = q$。该方法根据温度幂次对近视界 Frobenius 展开进行重整化，揭示了温度分层的层次结构，将 $n$ 阶极点跳跃条件简化为因子化代数方程：每个极点跳跃动量仅依赖于模式指标 $q$，与阶数 $n$ 无关。这种 $n$ 无关性在 $T\to 0$ 时产生高度简并，所有阶数的极点跳跃动量坍缩到由近视界几何和标量场质量决定的离散值集合上。在 $n \gg 1$ 极限下，主导极点跳跃动量渐近增长为 $k_{n,n} \propto n$。通过 Dyonic Gubser–Rocha 模型的数值分析验证了预测，确认低温下的高阶极点跳跃由近视界物理支配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准行列式方法（determinant methods）无法触及高阶极点跳跃（high-order pole-skipping），且极点跳跃在近极端低温全息系统中的物理意义尚不清晰，特别是子主导极点跳跃塔（subleading pole-skipping tower）缺乏具体的物理解释。

Method: 基于近极端黑洞（near-extremal black holes）近视界区域在 $T\to0$ 极限下涌现的 $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times \mathbb{R}^{d-1}$ 几何，将模式指标 $q$ 与红外共形维数 $\Delta_{\mathrm{IR}} = q$ 对应。通过按温度幂次重整化近视界 Frobenius 展开（near-horizon Frobenius expansion），建立温度分层的层次结构，将 $n$ 阶极点跳跃条件化为因子化代数方程。

Result: 发现极点跳跃动量仅依赖于模式指标 $q$ 而非阶数 $n$（$n$ 无关性），导致低温下各阶极点跳跃动量高度简并，坍缩到由近视界几何和标量场质量决定的离散值，这些值可用熵密度（entropy density）和比热（specific heat）等热力学量表达。在 $n \gg 1$ 且 $nT$ 保持很小的极限下，主导极点跳跃动量渐近行为为 $k_{n,n} \propto n$。通过 Dyonic Gubser–Rocha 模型的数值分析验证了解析预测。

Conclusion: 确认低温下高阶极点跳跃由近视界物理（near-horizon physics）主导；该方法提供了远超标准行列式方法的解析途径，用以获取极点跳跃点，并阐明了低温全息格林函数（holographic Green's functions）的结构。

Abstract: We develop a systematic analytic method for studying high-order pole-skipping in near-extremal holographic black holes. In the near-extremal regime, approaching the limit $T\to0$, the near-horizon geometry develops an approximately $\mathrm{AdS}_2 \times \mathbb{R}^{d-1}$ structure; we show that the mode index $q$ labeling pole-skipping points is identified with the IR conformal dimension $Δ_{\mathrm{IR}} = q$ in the emergent $\mathrm{AdS}_2/\mathrm{CFT}_1$ correspondence, providing a concrete physical interpretation of the subleading pole-skipping tower. The method reorganizes the near-horizon Frobenius expansion according to powers of temperature. This reveals a temperature-graded hierarchical structure that reduces the $n$-th-order pole-skipping condition to a factorized algebraic equation:each pole-skipping momentum depends only on the mode index $q$, not on the order $n$. This $n$-independence produces a high degeneracy as $T\to 0$, where pole-skipping momenta at all orders collapse onto a discrete set of values determined by near-horizon geometry and the scalar field mass; these values can be expressed in terms of thermodynamic quantities such as entropy density and specific heat. In the limit $n \gg 1$ (with $nT$ remaining small), the leading pole-skipping momenta grow asymptotically as $k_{n,n} \propto n$. We compute leading temperature corrections and verify our predictions through numerical analysis of the Dyonic Gubser--Rocha model. The results confirm that high-order pole-skipping at low temperature is governed by near-horizon physics. This provides analytic access to pole-skipping points well beyond those accessible by standard determinant methods and clarifies the structure of holographic Green's functions in the low-temperature regime.

</details>


### [80] [Wilson Towers as Local Bulk Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21397)
*Vishal Gayari,Chethan Krishnan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明，三维热AdS时空中的多绕Wilson圈（Wilson spools）可以改写为单绕Wilson圈之和，每个单绕圈对应一个多迹初级场（multi-trace primary）；进一步利用Verlinde线和模块变换S-核（modular S-kernel），将光滑BTZ黑洞视界解释为大量重Wilson线量子态的系统平均。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索2+1维引力的Wilson spools能否统一描述局域自由体场（local free bulk fields）的一圈配分函数，以及如何通过AdS/CFT对应将多粒子扇区（multi-particle sectors）与CFT中的多迹初级场（multi-trace primaries）对偶起来。

Method: 使用标准对称函数方法（symmetric-function methods）将热AdS₃中的Wilson spool重写为单绕Wilson圈之和；引入拓扑Verlinde线（topological Verlinde line）替换轻插入（light insertion）；利用模块化S-核（modular S-kernel）的真空行作为重初级场（heavy primaries）的近似密度。

Result: 成功将Wilson spool分解为单绕Wilson圈的求和，且每个多迹初级场的SL(2)后代与边界引力子（boundary gravitons）共同复现了该模块的完整Virasoro特征标（Virasoro character）；平滑BTZ视界上的局域场一圈行列式获得了微观描述。

Conclusion: 光滑视界本质上是一个量子态系综（ensemble of quantum states）的替代，每个量子态由一条重Wilson线产生，在半经典极限下表现为奇异视界（singular horizon）。

Abstract: Multi-winding Wilson loops (``Wilson spools'') in 2+1-dimensional gravity can reproduce one-loop partition functions of local free fields in the bulk. Bulk free fields have a second-quantized Fock space, and the AdS/CFT correspondence suggests that the associated multi-particle sectors are dual to multi-trace primaries in the CFT. In this note, we use standard symmetric-function methods to show that the Wilson spool in thermal AdS$_3$ can be recast as a sum over $single$-winding Wilson loops --- one for each multi-trace primary. In a companion paper to appear, we will view Wilson networks and TQFTs as the natural language of non-perturbative bulk quantum gravity. The present note illustrates how this can apply to $local$ bulk fields, and not just defects: a bulk (generalized free) field is to be viewed as a full tower of multi-trace Wilson lines. We further show that the $SL(2)$ descendants of each multi-trace primary, together with the boundary gravitons of the AdS$_3$ background, correctly reproduce the full Virasoro character of each module. In this language, the role of a light insertion on a heavy primary is played by a topological Verlinde line. This allows us to obtain a ``microscopic" description of one-loop determinants on the smooth BTZ handlebody. A spatially wound probe Wilson line on a torus with a contractible $thermal$ cycle can be traded for a Verlinde line inserted on a dense family of heavy Polyakov loops --- with the roles of the two cycles exchanged, so that the $spatial$ cycle is now contractible. The vacuum row of the modular $S$-kernel acts as the (approximate) density of the heavy primaries. This reinforces the case made in arXiv:2601.18775 that a smooth horizon is a stand-in for an ensemble of quantum states, each produced by a heavy Wilson line that appears as a singular horizon in the semi-classical limit.

### [81] [Relational path integral, effective actions and quantum frame covariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21463)
*Sergio E. Aguilar-Gutierrez,Renata Ferrero,Philipp A. Hoehn,Luca Marchetti*

TL;DR: 本文利用量子参考系（QRF）这一新工具，提出了引力路径积分的关系性丛几何表述，从而建立了一个无鬼影、无反常的显式规范不变路径积分，并展示了其在QRF变换下的协变性及一系列定性预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力路径积分中存在规范冗余、鬼影（ghost）和反常（anomaly）问题，需要引入规范固定（gauge fixing）来处理。本文旨在通过量子参考系（quantum reference frames）构建关系性可观测量（relational observables），实现无需规范固定的显式规范不变路径积分。

Method: 提出一种关系性丛几何（relational bundle-geometric）表述，利用量子参考系构建规范协变坐标（gauge-covariant coordinate systems）。路径积分基于关系性可观测量构建，将QRF视为框架，并通过QRF变换实现不同框架之间的视角中立（perspective-neutral）编码。

Result: 该路径积分无鬼影、无反常，且与Faddeev-Popov规范固定版本等价。预测包括：一组QRF视角中的局域关联函数（local correlators）与时间演化在另一视角中变得模糊；出现一系列关系性真空态（relational vacua），包括依赖于框架的no-boundary和渐近基态，一个视角中的真空在另一视角中一般呈现激发态。

Conclusion: 通过将源（sources）仅耦合到关系性可观测量，构建了规范不变但依赖于框架的有效作用量（effective actions），为重整化（renormalization）的关系性定义奠定了基础。

Abstract: We propose a relational bundle-geometric formulation of the gravitational path integral by invoking the new tool of quantum reference frames (QRFs), which in gravity are gauge-covariant coordinate systems constructed from the available field content. Formulated in terms of relational (frame-dressed) observables, this yields a manifestly gauge-invariant path integral without ghosts and anomalies, and in which observables and their correlators are local to a frame. While eliminating the need for gauge fixing, it is equivalent to Faddeev-Popov versions in which the QRF is gauge-fixed, recovering certain previous proposals. A key feature is its covariance under QRF changes: it is a perspective-neutral path integral which encodes all internal QRF perspectives and the transformations between them. This leads to several qualitative predictions: local correlators and time evolution of relational observables in one QRF perspective become fuzzy in another, and a new spectrum of relational vacua arises. Comprised of frame-dependent no-boundary and asymptotic ground states, a vacuum from one perspective appears generally excited in another. Finally, we construct gauge-invariant, yet frame-dependent effective actions by coupling sources exclusively to relational observables, setting the stage for a relational definition of renormalization.

</details>


### [82] [A universal scaling function for giant graviton OPE coefficients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21472)
*Miao He,Yunfeng Jiang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究平面 𝒩=4 超杨-米尔斯理论中，两个最大巨引力子（giant graviton）与一个有限扭曲自旋算符之间 OPE 系数在大自旋极限下的幂律标度行为，证明了标度指数 d(g) 不受有限尺寸修正影响，并在弱耦合与强耦合区间分别给出了精确结果与预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确计算大自旋极限下 OPE 系数的标度指数 d(g)，验证其是否受有限尺寸修正影响，并在整个耦合区间（从弱耦合到强耦合）建立系统计算方法。

Method: 采用大自旋极限 S→∞ 并结合平面 𝒩=4 超杨-米尔斯理论，发展一种系统方法计算标度函数 d(g) 在任意 't Hooft 耦合常数 g 下的取值；利用全圈渐进表达式提取精确指数。

Result: 证明标度指数 d(g) 不存在有限尺寸修正；弱耦合下结果与已有三圈场论结果完全一致；强耦合下给出了前三阶的具体预言；有限耦合结果展示了从弱耦合到强耦合的平滑插值行为。

Conclusion: 该 OPE 系数的幂律标度指数 d(g) 可以精确解析得到，且在弱耦合与强耦合之间光滑过渡，为理解 AdS/CFT 对应下的算符乘积展开（OPE）结构提供了新的精确信息。

Abstract: We consider the large spin limit $S\to\infty$ of the OPE coefficient for two maximal giant gravitons and a spinning operator with finite twist in planar $\mathcal{N}=4$ super-Yang-Mills theory. Up to an overall normalization factor, this OPE coefficient exhibits a power-law scaling of the form $S^{d(g)}$. We provide strong evidence that the exponent $d(g)$ is free from finite size corrections. Consequently, the all-loop asymptotic expression for the OPE coefficient can be used to determine $d(g)$ exactly. We develop a systematic method to compute the scaling function $d(g)$ for arbitrary values of the 't Hooft coupling $g$. At weak coupling, our result agrees perfectly with the available field-theoretic results up to three-loop order. At strong coupling, we present the first three orders as concrete predictions. We further provide the finite-coupling result and show that it interpolates smoothly between the weak- and strong-coupling regimes.

### [83] [Aspects of Closed Matricial Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21509)
*Dionysios Anninos,Samuel Brian*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文以二维Λ>0量子引力为起点，研究闭空间截面上具有正宇宙学常数（Λ>0）的简单引力理论的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）结构。通过重新审视矩阵模型文献中的精确结果，结合惠勒-德维特方程（Wheeler-DeWitt equation）和引力路径积分（gravitational path integral）两种视角分析引力波函数，揭示了大体积效应、拓扑修正等非平凡特征，并探讨了规范希尔伯特空间的内积问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究的动机源于四维Λ>0爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦理论（Einstein-Maxwell theory）中具有S²×Σ_h拓扑的引力鞍点（gravitational saddles）的存在，其中Σ_h是亏格为h的黎曼曲面（Riemann surface）。以此为出发点，作者将问题简化为二维Λ>0量子引力作为具体的研究起点。

Method: 作者重新阐述并扩展了矩阵模型（matrix model）文献中的精确结果。从惠勒-德维特方程和引力路径积分两个角度研究引力波函数（gravitational wavefunctions），建立了直到亏格六（genus-six）的显式结果。

Result: 研究发现若干具有普遍意义的特征：大体积效应（large volume effects）破坏微扰展开；路径积分波函数的拓扑修正（topological corrections）违反精确惠勒-德维特方程；球面路径积分Z^(0)_grav在Λ中具有非平凡结构。在空间尺寸较大时，亏格为h的引力圆盘路径积分（gravitational disk path integral）的主导贡献表现为二维拓扑引力（two-dimensional topological gravity）的行为。此外，要使Z^(0)_grav为离散化黎曼曲面产生正计数问题（positive counting problem），必须具有负的前因子（pre-factor）。

Conclusion: 作者讨论了由Lian和Zuckerman发现的无限维规范引力希尔伯特空间（canonical gravitational Hilbert space）的候选内积（inner products）。最后将分析与时域刘维尔理论（timelike Liouville theory）这一更现实的情形进行了对比。

Abstract: We investigate the Hilbert space structure for simple theories of gravity with $Λ>0$ on closed spatial sections. Our motivation ties to the presence of gravitational saddles in four-dimensional $Λ>0$ Einstein-Maxwell theory with $S^2\times Σ_h$ topology, where $Σ_h$ is a genus-$h$ Riemann surface. Here, as a concrete starting point, the problem is explored for two-dimensional $Λ>0$ quantum gravity. We revisit and elaborate on exact results in the matrix model literature. We study gravitational wavefunctions from both the perspective of the Wheeler-DeWitt equation and the gravitational path integral. Though simple, the setting displays many features of general interest such as large volume effects that disrupt the perturbative expansion, topological corrections to the path-integral wavefunction that offend the exact Wheeler-DeWitt equation, and a sphere path integral ${Z}^{(0)}_{\text{grav}}$ with non-trivial structure in $Λ$. We discuss candidate inner products for the infinite-dimensional canonical gravitational Hilbert space uncovered by Lian and Zuckerman. By establishing explicit results up to genus-six, we argue that the dominant contribution to the genus-$h$ gravitational disk path integral at large spatial size mimics the behavior of two-dimensional topological gravity. In passing, we show that for ${Z}^{(0)}_{\text{grav}}$ to give rise to a positive counting problem for discretised Riemann surfaces, it must have a negative pre-factor. We contrast our analysis to the more realistic case of timelike Liouville theory.

### [84] [Revealing the conformal symmetry of the discrete series scalars in dS${}_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21514)
*Lukas William Lindwasser*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了在具有非零常Ricci曲率的二维流形上（特别是dS₂和AdS₂时空），标量场通过共形Killing张量（conformal Killing tensor）表述所展现的全局共形对称性（global conformal symmetry），并证实了该对称性生成共形等距变换（conformal isometry transformations），且运动方程在该变换下协变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在回答如下问题：在二维dS₂时空中，标量场的关联函数虽服从全局共形Ward恒等式（conformal Ward identities），但这一全局共形对称性如何具体作为变换作用在标量场上。需通过共形Killing张量这一等价描述来弥合对称性表象上的缺口。

Method: 利用标量场的共形Killing张量等价描述，将对标量场的非局域作用转化为对共形Killing张量的局域作用。在此基础上分析共形变换下运动方程的协变性，并在dS₂和AdS₂中构造局域定义的、无迹的应力张量（traceless stress tensor）。

Result: 发现了一种共形对称变换，该变换局域作用于共形Killing张量，但非局域作用于标量场。运动方程在该共形变换下协变。在dS₂和AdS₂中均找到了由共形Killing张量局域定义的无迹应力张量，该张量生成全局共形等距变换。

Conclusion: 通过共形Killing张量框架，成功揭示了二维非零常Ricci曲率流形上标量场的全局共形对称性的具体实现方式，表明该对称性可通过局域定义的无迹应力张量生成，且运动方程在该变换下保持协变。

Abstract: On two-dimensional manifolds with nonzero constant Ricci curvature, there exists an infinite sequence of scalar fields with nonzero mass parameter that admit a pair of (anti)-holomorphic currents. After suitably defining the theory in de Sitter space ($\mathrm{dS}_2$), correlation functions of these currents obey global conformal Ward identities. We address the question of how this global conformal symmetry manifests as an action on the scalar field. An essential step is in leveraging an equivalent description of the scalar field in terms of a conformal Killing tensor. Through this, we find a conformal symmetry transformation that acts locally on the conformal Killing tensor, but non-locally on the scalar field. We show that the equation of motion transforms covariantly with respect to these conformal transformations, and further find a traceless stress tensor in both $\mathrm{dS}_2$ and $\mathrm{AdS}_2$, locally defined in terms of the conformal Killing tensor, which generates the global conformal isometry transformations.

### [85] [On the strong coupling limit of Yang-Mills matrix models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21593)
*Adrien Martina,Harish Murali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究质量变形的Yang-Mills矩阵模型的强耦合极限，发现超对称Yang-Mills矩阵模型在强耦合下实现矩阵可交换性，并展现巨大算符下的普适性，而可交换性与普适性虽相关但并非同一概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解质量变形的Yang-Mills矩阵模型在强耦合极限下矩阵何时变得可交换，从而判断是否可将矩阵解释为涌现空间（emergent space）的坐标。

Method: 在强耦合极限下分析含费米子（fermionic degrees of freedom）的Yang-Mills矩阵模型，考察费米子自由度数量变化对矩阵对易性的影响，同时检验在O(N^2)量级（即巨大算符）变形下的归一化本征值密度的普适性（universality）。

Result: 费米子会剧烈改变竞争格局。当费米子自由度达到临界值N_c=2(D-2)（即超对称Yang-Mills矩阵模型的配置）时，矩阵在强耦合下可交换，且在此临界点上模型在巨大算符变形下表现出普适性；超过临界点后矩阵仍可交换，但巨大算符普适性消失。

Conclusion: 可交换性（commutativity）与巨大算符普适性（huge-operator universality）是相关但不同的性质，超对称Yang-Mills矩阵模型位于二者兼有的临界边界上。

Abstract: We study the strong coupling limit of mass deformed Yang--Mills matrix models, with the aim of understanding when the matrices become effectively commuting. The Yang--Mills interaction classically drives the matrices toward mutually commuting valleys, where the matrices can potentially be interpreted as coordinates of an emergent space. However, taking into consideration the integration measure, commutativity is not automatic since the commuting locus is entropically suppressed, and in the bosonic models with $D\geq3$ the strong coupling limit remains non-commuting. We find that fermions change this competition in a sharp way. As the number of fermionic degrees of freedom is increased, there is a critical value $\mathcal N_c=2(D-2)$, realized by the supersymmetric Yang--Mills matrix models, at which the matrices commute at strong coupling. The same critical models also exhibit universality under deformations by $O(N^2)$, or huge, operators: the normalized eigenvalue densities are insensitive to the microscopic details of the huge operators. Increasing the number of fermions beyond the critical point still gives commuting matrices, but the huge-operator universality is lost. Thus commutativity and universality are related but distinct: the matrix models with supersymmetric field content sit at the critical boundary where we have both.

</details>
