### [86] [Quasiparticle specific heat of two-component Fermi mixtures: The atomic 163Dy-40K mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21254)
*Neda Ebrahimian*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用平均场理论（mean-field theory）结合局域密度近似（local density approximation, LDA），研究了质量不平衡的费米-费米混合物在BCS（Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer）侧的正常超流体相分离行为，分析了相互作用强度和质量比对相图、超流态密度及准粒子比热的影响，并发现镝-钾混合物中的比热可作为质量不对称配对的热学信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷费米气体可进入正常超流体相分离（normal superfluid phase separation）区域，但质量不平衡（mass imbalance）对该相分离态的具体影响尚需系统研究，尤其理解相互作用强度和质量比如何调控相图及热力学性质。

Method: 采用平均场理论（mean-field theory）结合局域密度近似（local density approximation, LDA），假设由Feshbach共振诱导的s波配对，并对相分离态施加相平衡条件（phase-equilibrium conditions）。通过自洽求解能量间隙（energy gap）和Hartree-Fock势，在选取的化学势参数范围内避免其他可能相的出现。

Result: 在研究的参数范围内，增强相互作用强度会提高平均化学势和失衡化学势（imbalance chemical potential），同时减小能量间隙和超流态密度（superfluid density of states）。总准粒子比热（quasiparticle specific heat）随失衡化学势和相互作用强度增大而下降，但随质量比增大而上升。镝-钾原子混合物的比热表现出质量不对称配对的热学特征。

Conclusion: 比热可作为探测质量不对称超流配对（mass-asymmetric pairing）的一种有效热学探针，为超冷费米混合物中的相分离行为提供可观测的实验信号。

Abstract: Ultracold Fermi gases can enter a regime of normal superfluid phase separation, with an unpolarized superfluid component surrounded by a partially polarized normal component. Mass-imbalanced two-component Fermi mixtures on the Bardeen Cooper Schrieffer side of the crossover are studied using mean-field theory within the local density approximation, assuming s-wave pairing induced by a Feshbach resonance and imposing the phase-equilibrium conditions for the phase-separated state. The imbalance chemical potential is chosen to be smaller than the energy gap, so that other possible phases are avoided in the regime considered here. The energy gap and Hartree Fock potentials are obtained self- consistently. The effects of interaction strength and mass ratio on the phase diagram, superfluid density of states, and quasiparticle specific heat are then examined. Within the investigated parameter range, increasing the magnitude of the interaction strength increases the average and imbalance chemical potentials, while reducing the energy gap and the superfluid density of states. The total quasiparticle specific heat decreases with increasing imbalance chemical potential and interaction strength, but increases with mass ratio. Results for the Fermi Fermi mixture of dysprosium and potassium atoms show that the specific heat provides a thermal signature of mass-asymmetric pairing.

</details>


### [87] [Fluctuation-Induced Bistability in the Dissipative Dynamics of Generic Cavity-Matter Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21296)
*Luisa Tolle,Simon B. Jäger,Ameneh Sheikhan,Corinna Kollath,Catalin-Mihai Halati*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文证明，在具有强光-物质耦合的强相互作用多体系统中，涨落诱导双稳态（fluctuation-induced bistability）是一种鲁棒且普适的现象。作者识别出基于光子跃迁与多体能标之间共振的微观机制，将该现象统一到自旋、费米子和玻色子等多种耦合腔模型中，并通过解析与数值方法（包括穿缀态速率方程和张量网络模拟）系统研究了其稳态与动力学性质，确立其为耗散腔耦合多体系统的通用特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多体系统与腔模式强耦合的背景下，涨落诱导双稳态是否是一种鲁棒且普适的现象尚不明确，缺乏统一的微观机制理解以及适用于不同模型的理论框架。

Method: 本文发展了两类互补方法：一是穿缀态速率方程（dressed-state rate equation approach），用于研究涨落诱导双稳态的稳态性质、有限时间动力学形成及其系统尺寸依赖；二是数值精确的张量网络模拟（tensor-network simulations），用于验证速率方程在小系统有限时间尺度上的预测。

Result: 识别出光子跃迁与多体能量尺度之间的共振（resonances between photonic transitions and many-body energy scales）是统一的微观机制；穿缀态速率方程揭示了丰富的亚稳态动力学（metastable dynamics）；张量网络模拟证实，即使在有限时间的小系统中也能观察到涨落诱导双稳态的特征信号。

Conclusion: 涨落诱导双稳态是耗散腔耦合多体系统（dissipative cavity-coupled many-body systems）的通用特征，本文提供的理论框架适用于各类混合量子平台（hybrid quantum platforms）的非平衡动力学研究。

Abstract: We demonstrate that fluctuation-induced bistability is a robust and generic phenomenon in strongly interacting many-body systems with strong light-matter coupling. We identify a common microscopic mechanism based on resonances between photonic transitions and many-body energy scales, unifying the emergence of fluctuation-induced bistability across a broad class of models, including interacting spins, fermions, and bosons coupled to cavity modes. We develop complementary methods to study both the steady-state properties of fluctuation-induced bistability and its dynamical formation at finite times. In particular, we introduce the dressed-state rate equation approach, which reveals rich metastable dynamics and enables the investigation of its system-size dependence. By comparing its predictions with numerically-exact tensor-network simulations, we identify signatures of fluctuation-induced bistability already in small systems on finite timescales. Our results establish fluctuation-induced bistability as a universal feature of dissipative cavity-coupled many-body systems and provide a general framework for the investigation of its non-equilibrium dynamics across a wide range of hybrid quantum platforms.

</details>


### [88] [Complexity transition in the Dicke model of light-matter interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21583)
*Yicheng Zhang,Erhai Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过研究Dicke模型中的Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）相图，发现改变耦合强度（coupling strength）可触发复杂度度量（complexity measures）的尖锐跃变，并利用Krylov空间中的波包动力学——受限弹跳与Rindler跳跃去局域化之间的竞争——阐明了该相变的本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别和理解远离平衡动力学中的非解析甚至不连续相变极具挑战性。尽管Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）为量子动力学中的算子增长、热化和混沌提供了新视角，但改变耦合强度是否以及如何引发复杂度度量的尖锐跃变仍不清楚。

Method: 通过绘制Dicke模型（Dicke model）的复杂度相图（complexity phase diagram），识别并表征动力学上的两个定性不同区域。利用Krylov空间中的波包动力学分析，研究受限线性势引起的弹跳与类似Rindler参考系（Rindler reference frame）跳跃导致的去局域化之间的竞争。

Result: 在相变点，Krylov复杂度（$C_K$）的斜率发生突变，并与Krylov熵（Krylov entropy）的跃变位置一致。Lanczos系数（Lanczos coefficients）的无序性（disorder）对受限弹跳与Rindler跳跃去局域化之间的竞争敏感。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了量子动力学中复杂度度量可因耦合强度调谐而出现尖锐相变，所建立的框架可推广至其他量子多体系统（quantum many-body systems）。

Abstract: Tuning the coupling strength $g$ of an interacting quantum system may drive a sudden change in its ground-state or thermal properties. To identify and grasp non-analytical, or even discontinuous, transitions in far-from-equilibrium dynamics proves more challenging. Recently Krylov complexity $C_K$ has offered fresh insights about operator growth, thermalization, and chaos in quantum dynamics. Yet it remains unclear if, and how, changing $g$ can trigger a sharp transition in the complexity measures. Here we present evidence for such a transition by mapping out the complexity phase diagram of the paradigmatic Dicke model describing two-level atoms coupled to a cavity photon mode. Two qualitatively different regimes of dynamics are identified and characterized. At the transition, the slope of $C_K$ changes suddenly to coincide with a jump in the Krylov entropy. We elucidate the nature of the regime change from the wave packet dynamics in Krylov space, where a particle is confined by a roughly linear potential but hops as if it lives in a Rindler reference frame. The competition between confinement, which leads to bouncing, and deconfinement by Rindler hopping, which leads to the destruction of wave packet analogous to gravitational spaghettification, is sensitive to the disorder in Lanczos coefficients. The framework outlined here can be applied to other quantum many-body systems.

</details>

# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [89] [An obstruction and residual-completion theory for Newman--Janis deformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20565)
*Reggie C. Pantig,Ali Övgün*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个用于Newman-Janis类型黑洞种子形变（deformations）的阻碍与残差完备化理论框架。该框架将Newman-Janis算法视为从静态种子到稳态轴对称试探几何的离壳映射，通过定义Newman-Janis阻碍张量（obstruction tensor）编码其失败，并将残差分解为动力学、几何/坐标可容许性和源保持三个通道。当阻碍非零时，残差完备化问题转化为线性可解性问题，其cokernel条件给出所选试探类中的不可行判据。作者以Schwarzschild真空引力为例，展示了非Kerr旋转试探度规及其阻碍的计算和最小修正过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Newman-Janis算法在从静态种子构造旋转黑洞解时缺乏统一的失败判据和系统修正方法，现有研究多以经验性寻找正确的复化规则（complexification rule）为主。本文旨在将这一过程形式化，建立可计算的阻碍与完备化判据，取代对复化规则的试错式搜索。

Method: 将Newman-Janis算法（包括原始复坐标变换及非复化变体）视为从静态种子到稳态轴对称试探度规的离壳映射，通过定义阻碍张量（obstruction tensor）量化其未满足场方程的程度。进一步将残差分解为动力学、几何/坐标可容许性和源保持三个通道，涵盖圆条件、Boyer-Lindquist可积性、应力张量类型、状态方程保持和物质模型可实现性等约束。在旋转参数的领先非零阶，将残差完备化转化为线性可解性问题，要求阻碍位于规范固定的完备化算子的像中，其cokernel条件给出该试探类中的不可行判据。

Result: 以真空GR中的Schwarzschild解为例，使用一种非Kerr生成方式的ONJA型复化得到非Kerr旋转试探度规，计算其阻碍得到$n_\star=2$和$\ell_\star=0$，并在同阶出现额外四极分量。通过最小偶宇称修正恢复Kerr复化可消除主导阶残差。该框架用可计算的判据替代了对正确复化规则的搜索。

Conclusion: 本文提出的阻碍与残差完备化理论为评判Newman-Janis类型形变的成功、完备化或阻碍提供了计算性判据，无需依赖经验选择复化规则。

Abstract: We formulate an obstruction and residual-completion theory for Newman-Janis-type deformations of black hole seeds, where Newman-Janis-type includes both the original complex-coordinate Newman-Janis algorithm and modified prescriptions such as non-complexification variants. The Newman-Janis algorithm is treated as an off-shell map from a static seed to a stationary-axisymmetric trial geometry, rather than as a solution-generating theorem. Its failure is encoded in a Newman-Janis obstruction tensor, defined as the residual obtained after substituting the trial configuration into the intended field equations. We decompose this residual into dynamical, geometrical/coordinate-admissibility, and source-preservation channels, separating field-equation failure from circularity, Boyer-Lindquist integrability, stress-tensor type, equation-of-state preservation, and matter-model realizability. When the obstruction is nonzero, residual completion asks whether a minimal correction of the metric and matter fields can cancel it. At leading nonzero order in the rotation parameter, this becomes a linear solvability problem: the obstruction must lie in the image of a gauge-fixed completion operator subject to boundary and source-sector constraints, while the cokernel condition gives a no-go criterion in the chosen ansatz class. We illustrate the framework with a Schwarzschild example in vacuum GR. Using an ONJA-type complexification different from the Kerr-generating one, we obtain a non-Kerr rotating trial metric and compute its obstruction. The example gives $n_\star=2$ and $\ell_\star=0$, with an additional quadrupolar component at the same order, and shows how the leading residual is removed by the minimal even-parity correction restoring the Kerr complexification. The framework replaces the search for the correct complexification rule with computable criteria for success, completion, or obstruction.

</details>


### [90] [Eikonal Quality-Factor Parameterization of Model-Conditional Static Black-Hole Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20573)
*Nikko John Leo S. Lobos,Emmanuel T. Rodulfo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究如何利用单个复拟正规频率（quasinormal frequency）在特定黑洞族内参数化其几何结构与模型条件热力学（model-conditional thermodynamics），并提出一种模型依赖的逆反演方案，但无法区分不同引力理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索仅通过一个拟正规频率（quasinormal frequency）能否反演出静态球对称黑洞的几何参数与热力学性质，并检验该方法在不同引力理论（如MOG）下的区分能力。

Method: 在eikonal极限下，对最小耦合无质量标量场定义比值 χ=ω_R/ω_I=2Q，该比值消除整体质量标度；若 χ 在单一无量纲参数上为单射（injective），则可重构该参数与几何标度。使用Chebyshev和WKB–Padé方法计算有限多极矩误差。

Result: 对于RN形式族，χ 可确定 u=q² 但无法判定电荷符号；恒定耦合静态MOG度规在映射 (ℳ=(1+α)m_MOG, u=α/(1+α)) 下等价于RN。两种分配具有相同温度但不同的作用依赖熵（action-dependent entropy），有限多极矩误差最大为2.1×10⁻³（l=2 RN网格）。

Conclusion: 该方案是模型依赖的逆反演（model-dependent inverse），而非理论选择器（theory selector）；将其应用于引力波观测需考虑张量、矢量和标量扰动扇区，超出测试场eikonal近似范围。

Abstract: We study how one complex quasinormal frequency can parameterize the geometry and model-conditional thermodynamics of a prescribed family of static, spherically symmetric black holes. For a minimally coupled massless test scalar in the eikonal limit, the ratio $χ=ω_Rτ=ω_R/ω_I=2Q$ removes the overall mass scale. If $χ$ is injective in one dimensionless parameter, that parameter and the geometric scale can be reconstructed within the chosen family. The normalized metric then fixes the horizon and Hawking temperature, whereas Wald entropy requires the gravitational action. For the RN-form family, $χ$ determines $u=q^2$ but not the sign of charge. The constant-coupling static MOG metric is exactly RN under $\mathcal M=(1+α)m_{\rm MOG}$ and $u=α/(1+α)$; consequently, the complete minimally coupled scalar spectrum is identical on mapped backgrounds for every multipole and overtone. The two assignments have equal temperature but different action-dependent entropy. Chebyshev and WKB--Padé calculations quantify the finite-multipole error, with a maximum eikonal ratio error of $2.1\times10^{-3}$ on the tested $l=2$ RN grid. The construction is therefore a model-dependent inverse, not a theory selector. Applying it to gravitational-wave observations requires the appropriate tensor, vector, and scalar perturbation sectors beyond the test-field eikonal approximation.

</details>


### [91] [Unstable de Sitter inflationary solution in sixth-order gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20575)
*Tuan Q. Do*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种包含R□R、R_{μν}□R^{μν}、二次曲率项及三次曲率项的六阶引力理论（sixth-order gravity），推导了其在FLRW背景下的场方程，并得到了精确的德西特解（de Sitter solution）。系数γ₁和γ₂不影响解的值，但影响其稳定性：当3γ₁+γ₂<0时解不稳定，数值验证证实该固定点为排斥子（repeller）。结果表明该六阶引力适用于早期宇宙暴胀阶段，而其二阶极限则给出稳定德西特解，适用于晚期宇宙加速膨胀。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验六阶引力理论（sixth-order gravity）是否存在精确且稳定的德西特解（de Sitter solution），从而评估该理论在宇宙学不同阶段（早期暴胀与晚期加速膨胀）的适用性。

Method: 基于欧拉-拉格朗日方程（Euler-Lagrange equations）的有效方法，在均匀各向同性的FLRW（Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker）背景时空下推导六阶微分场方程，并解析求解得出德西特解，将其等价为动力学系统的固定点（fixed point）。通过不等式分析稳定性条件，并辅以数值计算验证。

Result: 六阶引力理论存在精确的德西特解，γ₁和γ₂对解的值无贡献，但影响稳定性：当3γ₁+γ₂<0时德西特解不稳定，数值验证表明此时固定点为排斥子（repeller）。二阶极限始终产生稳定德西特解，四阶极限则未给出稳定结果。

Conclusion: 六阶引力理论更适用于描述早期宇宙的暴胀阶段（inflationary phase），因其德西特解在特定条件下不稳定；而其二阶极限始终给出稳定德西特解，适用于晚期宇宙的加速膨胀（accelerated expansion）。

Abstract: A sixth-order gravity, which involves not only two leading terms, $γ_1 R\Box R$ and $γ_2 R_{μν} \Box R^{μν}$, but also quadratic curvature terms along with cubic curvature ones, will be investigated in this paper to see if it admits an exact stable de Sitter solution. First, we will derive sixth-order differential field equations of this gravity under the homogeneous and isotropic Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker background spacetime, using the effective method based on the Euler-Lagrange equations. Then, we will analytically solve these field equations to figure out an exact de Sitter solution, which turns out to be equivalent to a fixed point of the corresponding dynamical system of the studied gravity. Interestingly, two coefficients, $γ_1$ and $γ_2$, do not contribute to the value of the obtained de Sitter solution. However, they affect on the stability of the de Sitter solution. In particular, if these two coefficients obey the following inequality, $3γ_1+γ_2 <0$, then the de Sitter solution will always be unstable. Furthermore, numerical calculations will be performed to verify that the de Sitter fixed point is indeed a repeller of the dynamical system once this inequality is satisfied. All these results indicate that the sixth-order gravity is more suitable for an inflationary phase of early universe. To be complete, two special limits of the studied gravity model, in which field equations are reduced to second-order and fourth-order, respectively, will be investigated. As expected, only the second-order limit can always give raise a stable de Sitter solution, compatible with an accelerated expansion of late-time universe.

</details>


### [92] [Black hole-neutron star binaries with high spins and large mass asymmetries: III. Properties of the ejected material and its electromagnetic signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20609)
*Konrad Topolski,Samuel D. Tootle,Paramvir Singh,Mattia Bulla,Luciano Rezzolla*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过广义相对论磁流体动力学（GRMHD）模拟，系统研究了黑洞-中子星（BH-NS）双星系统中动力学抛射物的几何与热力学性质，并结合核反应网络SkyNet和辐射转移代码POSSIS，计算了r过程元素丰度及千新星（kilonova）光变曲线，结果与AT2017gfo及S190814bv观测数据总体一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞-中子星并合是引力波与电磁波多信使天文学（multi-messenger astronomy）的重要源。本研究旨在填补大质量比、高自旋BH-NS系统动力学抛射物特性的认知空白，扩展已有对低质量比、无自旋系统的研究结果。

Method: 采用广义相对论磁流体动力学（general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamics, GRMHD）模拟，覆盖包含大质量比和高BH自旋的全面双星参数空间。通过追踪能量与角动量向物质的转移研究潮汐瓦解与动力学质量抛射；使用核反应网络SkyNet计算r过程元素丰度；利用辐射转移代码POSSIS生成千新星光变曲线。

Result: 揭示了双星参数对抛射物几何、热力学和运动学性质的影响；获得了r过程元素丰度及其对前身星性质的依赖关系；计算得到的千新星光变曲线在热光度与光学/近红外演化方面与AT2017gfo数据及S190814bv上限观测总体相符。

Conclusion: 对于大质量比、高BH自旋的BH-NS系统，动力学抛射物的性质可通过GRMHD模拟系统刻画，且基于模拟预测的千新星信号与已有多信使观测具有一致性，验证了该理论框架的有效性。

Abstract: Compact binary systems consisting of a black hole (BH) and a neutron star (NS) are expected to provide detectable signals both in the gravitational wave and in the electromagnetic channels, thus representing excellent sources for multi-messenger astronomy. In this third paper in a series, we report on the geometric and thermodynamic properties of the purely dynamical ejecta component modeled in our general-relativistic magnetohydrodynamical simulations of BHNS systems over a comprehensive binary parameter space consisting of large mass ratio and high BH spin. The tidal disruption and dynamical mass ejection is studied by monitoring the transfer of energy and angular momentum to matter for the particular case of a highly unequal-mass binary with large BH spin, extending known results for low-mass-ratio, irrotational BHNS binaries. By varying the binary parameters, we investigate their influence on the geometric, thermodynamic, and kinematic properties of the ejected matter. Furthermore, we employ the nuclear-reaction network SkyNet to obtain the elemental abundances resulting from the r-process active in the ejecta and study how they depend on the properties of the progenitor objects. Finally, using the radiative-transfer code POSSIS, we compute the kilonova light-curves from the results of our simulations, discuss their bolometric and optical/near-infrared evolution, and compare them with the AT2017gfo data and upper-limits for S190814bv, finding overall consistency.

</details>


### [93] [Cosmological Inflation in f(R,T) Gravity with Chern-Simons Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20654)
*Maryam Shiravand,Saeed Fakhry,Mehrdad Farhoudi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在包含Chern-Simons量子引力修正的线性f(R,T)引力框架下研究宇宙暴胀（cosmological inflation），推导了慢滚近似下的修正Friedmann方程，并通过与Planck 2018等观测数据的对比验证了模型的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在f(R,T)引力中引入由量子引力（quantum gravity）导出的Chern-Simons修正，构建暴胀模型并检验其与观测数据的一致性。

Method: 基于FLRW度规（FLRW metric）和慢滚近似（slow-roll approximations）导出修正Friedmann方程；考虑三角函数和指数函数两种Chern-Simons耦合函数形式，分别搭配暴胀子势（inflaton potential）；计算慢滚参数（slow-roll parameters）、标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）、张量谱指数（tensor spectral index）和张量标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio），并通过约束自由参数与Planck 2018等观测数据进行比较。

Result: 所提模型对暴胀可观测量（inflationary observables）的预测与Planck 2018数据吻合良好；指数型Chern-Simons耦合函数对张量标量比施加了更强的限制，且与Planck、BK15和BAO联合数据一致。不含Chern-Simons修正、不含线性f(R,T)以及采用非线性f(R,T)形式的对比分析表明，Chern-Simons修正在线性f(R,T)引力框架下大致优化了张量谱指数和张量标量比的值。

Conclusion: Chern-Simons修正的引入在线性f(R,T)引力暴胀模型中能够有效改善张量谱指数和张量标量比的预测精度，使模型更好地符合观测约束。

Abstract: We investigate cosmological inflation within the framework of a linear form of f (R, T ) gravity that incorporates an inflaton scalar field augmented by a Chern-Simons correction induced by aspects of quantum gravity. Utilizing the FLRW metric, we derive the modified Friedmann equations under the slow-roll approximations. We consider two specific forms of the Chern-Simons coupling function, trigonometric and exponential, each paired with the choice of an inflaton potential. Then, we define the essential slow-roll parameters and acquire their required expressions in the proposed model. Subsequently, we compute the scalar spectral index, the tensor spectral index, and the tensor-to- scalar ratio. By adequately constraining the free parameters, the proposed model provides accurate predictions for these inflationary observables that are in good agreement with the Planck 2018 data. Furthermore, the model predictions for the Chern-Simons exponential coupling function impose a stronger limit on the value of the tensor-to-scalar ratio and also provide good agreement with the joint Planck, BK15 and BAO data. Meanwhile, for comparative analysis and better comparison of the model motivations, we also examine the model without the Chern-Simons correction, without the linear form of f (R, T ) gravity, and with a non-linear form of f (R, T ) gravity. As a general conclusion, the obtained findings indicate that the inclusion of the Chern-Simons correction approximately refines the values of the tensor spectral index and tensor-to-scalar ratio in the context of the linear form of f (R, T ) gravity.

</details>


### [94] [A product template bank to search for compact binary coalescences microlensed by isolated point mass lenses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20661)
*Sudhir Gholap,Sanjeev V. Dhurandhar,Shasvath J. Kapadia*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对恒星级致密双星并合（CBC）产生的引力波（GW）被微透镜效应调制的问题，提出了一种构造微透镜引力波模板库（template bank）的方法。该模板库基于几何光学近似，添加了时间延迟（t_d）和相对放大率（μ_r）两个透镜参数，包含约4000个模板，可将失配度（mismatch）降低约一个数量级，并满足最小匹配准则0.97。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恒星级致密双星并合（compact binary coalescence, CBC）产生的引力波（gravitational wave, GW）在传播过程中若遇到史瓦西半径与GW波长相当的透镜，将发生微透镜效应（microlensing），导致观测信号出现频率依赖的调制。标准模板搜索（templated search）忽略这种波动光学效应，可能导致信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）损失高达30%，因此亟需构建针对微透镜引力波的专用模板库以提升探测效率。

Method: 作者以孤立点质量透镜造成的微透镜CBC为研究对象。尽管其频率依赖的放大因子具有闭式解析表达式，但构建模板库时仅需采用几何光学近似（geometric optics approximation），将微透镜信号有效建模为重叠信号。利用匹配滤波对相位敏感的特性，通过放大因子的相位计算度量元素（metric elements）。在标准CBC参数空间基础上增加两个透镜参数：图像间的时间延迟（time-delay, t_d）和相对放大率（relative-magnification, μ_r）。通过识别拟合因子（fitting factor, FF）因波动光学效应降至97%以下的透镜参数区域，构建覆盖该区域的约4000个模板的模板库，该模板库与未透镜化CBC参数取值无关。

Result: 研究表明，针对微透镜CBC的模板库可近似视为未透镜化CBC模板库与透镜参数模板库的笛卡尔积（Cartesian product）。评估结果表明，相较于使用未透镜化CBC模板库，使用乘积模板库可使失配度（mismatch）降低高达约一个数量级（因子~10），且与构建模板库时采用的0.97最小匹配（minimal match）准则保持一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法有效构建了针对微透镜引力波的模板库，显著降低了因忽略透镜效应导致的失配损失，为未来引力波探测中识别微透镜事件提供了可行方案。该方法以几何光学近似简化计算，同时通过拟合因子阈值识别关键透镜参数区域，保证了模板库的覆盖效率与准确性。

Abstract: Gravitational waves (GW) from stellar mass compact binary coalescences (CBCs) that encounter a lens whose Schwarzschild radius is comparable to the GW wavelength, will be microlensed, leading to frequency-dependent modulations in the observed signal. Neglecting such wave-optics effects in standard templated searches for CBCs can result in signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) losses as large as 30%. Here, we present a prescription for constructing a template bank targeted at microlensed GWs. We consider CBCs microlensed by isolated point mass lenses, whose frequency-dependent amplification factor is known to have a closed-form analytical expression. However, to construct the template bank, it suffices to use the geometric optics approximation, effectively modeling the microlensed signal as overlapping signals. Moreover, given that matched filtering is mostly sensitive to the phase of the GW signal, we use the phase of the amplification factor to compute the metric elements. The usual CBC parameter space is appended by two extra parameters: (i) the time-delay ($t_d$) between images and (ii) the relative-magnification ($μ_r$). By identifying the region of the lensing parameter space where the fitting factor (FF) falls below 97% due to wave-optics effects, we construct a template bank consisting of ~4000 templates covering the selected lensing region, independent of the values of the unlensed CBCs' parameters. We show that the bank targeting microlensed CBCs is, to a very good approximation, a Cartesian product of the unlensed CBC bank and the bank spanning the lensing parameters. We demonstrate the effectiveness of our method by evaluating fitting factors using both the unlensed CBC bank and the product template bank, finding a reduction of up to a factor of ~10 in the mismatch, as well as consistency with the prescribed minimal match criterion of 0.97 used in the construction of the banks.

</details>


### [95] [A First-Order Gauge Approach to de Sitter General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20687)
*P. Salgado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种德西特相对论的一阶规范场论表述（first-order gauge formulation），将伪半径 l(x) 提升为时空场，使 SO(4,1) 局域破缺至 SO(3,1)，从而将宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）重新诠释为对称性破缺的局域序参量（local order parameter），并通过广义诺特定理（generalized Noether theorem）导出统一的能量-动量流，指出无物质时局域真空能渐近消失、背景退化为闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）。该工作并未数值求解宇宙学常数问题，而是将其重新表述为动力学衰减问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于将德西特相对论（de Sitter relativity）纳入规范场论框架，通过几何补偿场（geometric compensator） l(x) 的局域化来诠释宇宙学常数的动力学起源，修正强等效原理（Strong Equivalence Principle），从而为宇宙学常数问题提供新的概念基础。

Method: 方法上，将伪半径 l(x) 提升为时空场，构建 SO(4,1) 至 SO(3,1) 的局域对称性破缺；通过 Inonu-Wigner 收缩（Inonu-Wigner contraction）将抽象生成元（abstract generators）转化为显式时空变换，并在宏观（l→∞）与微观（l→0）极限下给出非线性 Killing 向量（nonlinear Killing vectors）。利用广义诺特定理统一规范场与物质流的耦合，通过独立变分导出耦合的德西特场方程（coupled de Sitter field equations），并利用规范 Bianchi 恒等式（gauge Bianchi identities）证明 Λ(x) 是时空挠率（spacetime torsion）的内禀来源。

Result: 结果表明：无物质时，统一的能量-动量流恒为零，导致局域真空能渐近消失、背景退化为闵可夫斯基时空；Λ(x) 被严格识别为对称性破缺的局域序参量（local order parameter），且是时空挠率的内禀来源。通过代数证明，该规范场论表述与坐标流形上的张量分裂（tensorial splitting）等价。

Conclusion: 结论将宇宙学常数问题重新表述（recast）为对称性破缺序参量的动力学衰减问题，而非数值求解。从早期宇宙密度推导 Λ(x) 衰减至观测值仍属未来工作。

Abstract: We propose a first-order gauge formulation of de Sitter relativity in which the pseudo-radius l(x) is promoted to a spacetime field, locally breaking SO(4,1) to SO(3,1). Here, l(x) is a geometric compensator and dl(x) the associated order parameter. This modifies the Strong Equivalence Principle: the local vacuum follows the matter distribution instead of remaining fixed, while the propagating degrees of freedom of General Relativity are unchanged. At fixed l(x), the action is SO(3,1)-gauge invariant, but varying l(x) destroys covariance under the full translational sector of SO(4,1). Through the Inonu-Wigner contraction, abstract generators become explicit spacetime transformations, yielding nonlinear Killing vectors in both the macroscopic l tends to infinity and microscopic l tends to 0 limits. The generalized Noether theorem gives a unified energy-momentum current coupling the standard tensor to the proper conformal matter current. It vanishes identically without matter, causing the asymptotic extinction of local vacuum energy and the decay of the background to Minkowski spacetime. Independent variations yield the coupled de Sitter field equations, and we algebraically prove their equivalence to the tensorial splitting on the coordinate manifold. Gauge Bianchi identities further show that Lambda(x) is an intrinsic source of spacetime torsion, consistently identifying it with the local order parameter of the symmetry breaking. The cosmological constant problem is therefore recast, not numerically solved: deriving the decay of Lambda(x) from early-universe densities to its observed value remains future work.

</details>


### [96] [Gravitational Wave Birefringence in generalized Palatini Chern Simons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20689)
*Jose Perdiguero,Macarena Lagos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究在f(R)引力与动力学Chern-Simons项耦合的模型中引力波（gravitational wave）宇称性破缺导致的宇宙学双折射现象，分析了度规形式（metric formalism）和Palatini形式（Palatini formalism）下的差异，发现后者同时预言振幅双折射（amplitude birefringence）和速度双折射（velocity birefringence），而前者仅预言振幅双折射；双折射效应可被f(R)相互作用增强或抑制，且随源红移呈多项式增长，区别于现有的线性距离标度模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波双折射现象的研究多基于现象学模型，缺乏对具体引力理论框架（如f(R)引力与Chern-Simons项耦合）下双折射效应的系统分析，尤其是度规形式与Palatini形式之间的差异尚未被充分探讨。

Method: 在f(R)引力与动力学Chern-Simons（dCS）项耦合的框架下，分别在度规形式（metric formalism）和Palatini形式（Palatini formalism）中推导引力波的传播方程，分析宇称性破缺（parity symmetry breaking）对振幅和相位极化的影响；并以三种经宇宙学数据检验的f(R)模型（Hu-Sawicki、Exponential、Hyperbolic引力）为例计算双折射效应的大小。

Result: Palatini形式预言了振幅双折射（amplitude birefringence）和速度双折射（velocity birefringence），而度规形式仅预言振幅双折射；f(R)相互作用可以抑制或增强双折射效应，在三种常见f(R)模型中双折射相对于f(R)=R情形增强了1-10%（Palatini形式）乃至2倍（度规形式）；双折射效应随源红移（source redshift）呈多项式增长，而非现有现象学模型中通常假设的线性距离标度（linear-distance scaling）。

Conclusion: f(R)-dCS耦合模型为引力波宇宙学双折射提供了丰富的理论预言，度规形式与Palatini形式在可观测信号上存在本质差异；双折射随红移的多项式增长特征可作为区分该模型与现象学模型的关键检验手段；当前的引力波双折射观测约束可转化为对模型中的dCS耦合参数的界限。

Abstract: The cosmological propagation of gravitational waves (GWs) can exhibit amplitude and phase polarization distortions when parity symmetry is broken, a phenomenon known as cosmological birefringence. In this paper, we investigate the phenomenology of GW birefringence in a gravitational model $f(R)$ coupled to a dynamical Chern-Simons (dCS) term, analyzed in the metric and Palatini formalisms. At the background level, this model can lead to dynamical dark energy, while for GW propagation we find that the Palatini formalism predicts both amplitude and velocity birefringence, whereas the metric formalism predicts amplitude birefringence only. We also find that the birefringence effects can either be suppressed or enhanced by the $f(R)$ interactions, depending on the specific form of $f(R)$. Considering three common $f(R)$ models (Hu-Sawicki, Exponential, and Hyperbolic gravity) fit to recent cosmological data, we find that birefringence is enhanced relative to the $f(R) = R$ case, by $1-10\%$ in the Palatini formalism and up to a factor of 2 in the metric formalism. We also translate current GW birefringence constraints to bounds on the dCS coupling within our model. Finally, we show that in our model the birefringence effect grows polynomially with source redshift, in contrast to the linear-distance scaling commonly assumed in phenomenological models of GW birefringence in the current literature.

### [97] [Evolving Dark Energy from the Back-Reaction of Cosmological Perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20715)
*Vincent Comeau*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了宇宙学常数与物质分布不均匀性（inhomogeneities）的反作用（back-reaction）如何产生一个状态方程（equation of state）随时间演化的有效暗能量（effective dark energy），并分析了两种微扰处理方法下该时间依赖性的行为差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释现有观测中暗能量状态方程可能随时间演化的现象，并解决均匀性假设下宇宙学常数无法产生时间演化的矛盾。

Method: 基于平均化的弗里德曼方程（averaged Friedmann equations），对固定物质粒子体积（而非全局）取平均；分别通过标量扰动（scalar perturbations）和梯度展开（gradient expansion）两种微扰方式处理非均匀性。

Result: 在标量扰动的二次阶下，暗能量的时间依赖性化为边界项（boundary term），对全局平均可忽略；而在梯度展开下，相同的时间依赖性不再化为边界项，即使全局平均或空间曲率可忽略时仍显著，且符号在现今保持恒定，不允许暗能量在幻影（phantom）与非幻影行为之间交叉。

Conclusion: 非均匀性的反作用能够为宇宙学常数驱动的暗能量引入有物理意义的时间演化，其具体表现依赖于微扰处理方法的选择。

Abstract: We argue that the back-reaction of inhomogeneities, when combined with a pure cosmological constant, produces an effective dark energy whose equation of state can evolve with time. Our analytical computation agrees with recent numerical simulations, which have shown that the back-reaction of inhomogeneities can impact dark energy around the present time. Here, its equation of state is derived from an average version of the Friedmann equations, for which the average is taken over a fixed volume of matter particles (not necessarily global). When treating the inhomogeneities as small perturbations around a homogeneous background, dark energy acquires a time dependence which reduces to a boundary term, at least at quadratic order in the scalar modes of the perturbations. Thus, it becomes negligible for a global average. On the other hand, when treating instead the spatial derivatives of the inhomogeneities perturbatively in a gradient expansion, dark energy gets the same time dependence, which no longer reduces to a boundary term. This time dependence can be significant even for a global average or when the constant spatial curvature induced by the inhomogeneities is negligible. It also keeps the same sign around the present time, thus causing dark energy to remain either always phantom or never phantom, not allowing for any crossing from one type of behaviour to the other.

</details>

*Glenn Barnich*

TL;DR: 本文简洁地推导了受激（boosted）Schwarzschild黑洞的平衡热力学（equilibrium thermodynamics），并证明其与相对论性热力学（relativistic thermodynamics）的预期一致。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用简洁的推导方式（concise way），系统地分析了受激Schwarzschild黑洞的平衡热力学量，并将其结果与相对论性热力学的理论预期进行比较验证。

Conclusion: 受激Schwarzschild黑洞的平衡热力学可以用相对论性热力学框架自洽地描述，进一步支持了黑洞热力学与相对论性热力学之间的内在一致性。

Abstract: The equilibrium thermodynamics of boosted Schwarzschild black holes is worked out in a concise way and shown to agree with expectations from relativistic thermodynamics.

### [99] [Multi-Spin Perturbations, Thermodynamics, and Observational Signatures of Reissner-Nordstrom Black Holes in Bumblebee Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20839)
*Jayasri Choudhury,Yenshembam Priyobarta Singh,Dhruba Jyoti Gogoi,Telem Ibungochouba Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在蜜蜂引力（bumblebee gravity）框架下系统研究了带电Reissner-Nordström黑洞的动力学与热力学性质，分析了自发洛伦兹对称性破缺（LSB）参数与电荷对质量场扰动、准正则模（QNMs）、灰体因子、热力学量及相变行为的影响，并评估了其被引力波探测器观测的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在蜜蜂引力框架下探究带电RN黑洞在自发洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry breaking, LSB）影响下的动力学与热力学行为，以理解洛伦兹破缺效应对黑洞物理稳定性、热演化及相结构的具体作用。

Method: 利用Newman-Penrose形式下的统一Teukolsky主方程分析任意自旋（$s=0, 1/2, 1, 3/2, 2$）的无质量场微扰；通过推导有效势，采用Padé改进的6阶WKB近似和渐进迭代法（Asymptotic Iteration Method, AIM）计算准正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）频率及灰体因子（greybody factors）；热力学方面计算霍金温度、含对数热修正的熵及热容。

Result: LSB参数L与电荷Q对时空阻尼振荡和波传播产生显著修改；热力学分析显示存在二级相变（second-order phase transition），其临界半径主要由背景电荷决定；确定了当前及未来引力波探测器（LISA、Virgo、LIGO）可观测的黑洞质量范围。

Conclusion: LF洛伦兹破缺效应对带电黑洞的物理稳定性、热演化和相结构具有重要调控作用，为理解洛伦兹对称性破缺在引力系统中的表现提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this paper, we present a comprehensive investigation into the dynamical and thermodynamic properties of the charged Reissner-Nordström (RN) black hole (BH) in the bumblebee gravity framework, where spontaneous Lorentz symmetry breaking (LSB) occurs. To analyze the dynamical behavior, we apply the unified Teukolsky master equation within the Newman-Penrose formalism to evaluate massless field perturbations of arbitrary spins ($s=0, 1/2, 1, 3/2, 2$). By deriving the corresponding effective potentials, we compute the quasinormal modes (QNMs) frequencies using the Padé-improved 6th-order WKB approximation and the Asymptotic Iteration Method (AIM) and evaluate the greybody factors for all perturbing fields, demonstrating how the LSB parameter $L$ and the BH charge $Q$ modify the spacetime's damped oscillations and wave propagation. We further assess the observational prospects of these QNMs by determining the black-hole mass ranges accessible to current and future gravitational-wave detectors, including LISA, Virgo, and LIGO. Moreover, we investigate the modified thermodynamic structure, calculating the Hawking temperature, entropy with logarithmic thermal corrections and heat capacity. Our thermodynamic analysis reveals a second-order phase transition whose critical radius is heavily governed by the background charge. These combined findings provide valuable theoretical insights into how Lorentz violation affects the physical stability, thermal evolution, and phase structure of charged BHs.

### [100] [Static spheres in black hole spacetimes: pairing, energy conditions, and an upper bound on the innermost radius](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20850)
*Yong Song*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一般静态球对称渐近平坦黑洞时空中静态球（static spheres）的存在性、与能量条件（energy conditions）的关系以及径向边界。通过分析由质量和径向压力构造的径向函数的全局行为，证明了静态球必然要求负径向压力（张力），且非简并静态球必成对出现（内不稳定、外稳定）。在弱能量条件（WEC）始终成立的前提下，给出了内、外静态球处强能量条件（SEC）不等式的符号特征，并针对最内静态球推导了其半径的严格上界，建立了能量条件与静态球存在性之间的直接解析联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究静态球对称渐近平坦黑洞时空中静态球的存在条件，并建立其与能量条件之间的定量联系，从而为检验广义相对论及修改引力理论中的黑洞解、解释相关天文观测提供理论依据。

Method: 构造由质量函数与径向压力函数联合定义的径向函数，分析其全局行为；利用弱能量条件（WEC）和强能量条件（SEC）的成立或违反情况，推导静态球的成对出现性质、稳定性特征以及最内静态球半径的严格上界。

Result: 证明静态球必然要求负径向压力（张力）；非简并静态球必成对出现（内不稳定、外稳定）；在WEC始终成立条件下，内静态球违反SEC不等式（ρ+p+2p_T<0），外静态球恢复SEC不等式（ρ+p+2p_T>0），退化边界情形满足ρ+p+2p_T=0；推导出最内静态球半径的严格上界表达式。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了能量条件与静态球存在性之间的直接解析联系，对黑洞周围物质环境给出了定量约束，可应用于广义相对论和修改引力理论中黑洞解的检验及相关天文观测的解释。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the existence, relation to the energy conditions, and radial bounds of static spheres in general static, spherically symmetric, asymptotically flat black hole spacetimes. By analyzing the global behavior of a radial function constructed from the mass and radial pressure functions, we prove that a static sphere necessarily requires a negative radial pressure (tension). Furthermore, we show that non-degenerate static spheres must always appear in pairs: an inner unstable sphere and an outer stable one. Assuming the Weak Energy Condition (WEC) always holds, the inner static sphere is characterized by a violation of the strong energy condition (SEC) inequality $ρ+p+2p_T<0$, where $ρ$, $p$, and $p_T$ denote the energy density, radial pressure, and tangential pressure, respectively; the SEC inequality is restored ($ρ+p+2p_T> 0$) at the outer sphere; the degenerate marginal case satisfies $ρ+p+2p_T=0$. In addition, focusing on the innermost static sphere and assuming that the WEC holds while the SEC is uniformly violated between the event horizon and this sphere, we derive a rigorous upper bound on its radius,
  \[
  r^-_{\mathrm{sp}}\le \left[r_H^3+\frac{3r_H\bigl(1-8πr^2_Hρ(r_H)\bigr)}{8πκ}\right]^{1/3},
  \]
  where $r_H$ is the horizon radius, $ρ(r_H)$ the energy density at the horizon, and $κ$ characterizes the strength of the SEC violation. These results establish a direct, analytic link between the energy conditions and the existence of static spheres, and provide a quantitative constraint on the matter environment of black holes possessing such orbits. The findings have potential applications in testing black hole solutions in general relativity and modified theories of gravity, as well as in interpreting related astronomical observations.

### [101] [Graviton-induced which-path decoherence in matter-wave interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20867)
*Hiroki Matsui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文推导了线性化量子引力（linearized quantum gravity）中引力子（gravitons）被积分掉后引起的物质波干涉（matter-wave interferometry）的路径退相干（which-path decoherence），并表明该效应在现有实验中完全可以忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心动机是探究量子引力效应对物质波干涉仪中路径退相干的具体贡献，特别是由线性化引力子的辐射引起的影响。

Method: 论文通过对线性化量子引力中的引力子进行积分（tracing out），利用引力子由物质源线性驱动的性质，精确求解了分支依赖的演化（branch-dependent evolution）。退相干程度由初始引力子态的特征函数（characteristic function）在分支诱导场位移差处的取值给出。

Result: 真空中退相干指数（decoherence exponent）等于差分源辐射的引力子平均数量的一半。对光滑高斯轨迹，退相干指数为 Γ_vac=(8/15)Gm²d⁴/(ħc⁵τ⁴)，在现有物质波平台中的范围为 10⁻⁸⁹ 到 10⁻⁶¹。对一般压缩引力子真空态（squeezed graviton vacuum），压缩可抑制或增强真空响应；对暴胀产生的强压缩态，退相干指数为 Γ_inf=(π/20)Ω_inf(md²H₀/ħ)²，最乐观参数下至多约为 10⁻²⁷。

Conclusion: 辐射引力子引起的路径退相干在当前的物质波干涉仪中完全可以忽略不计。

Abstract: We derive which-path decoherence for matter-wave interferometry that arises from tracing out the gravitons of linearized quantum gravity. Because the gravitons are driven linearly by the matter source, the branch-dependent evolution can be solved exactly, and the reduced coherence is given by the characteristic function of the initial graviton state, evaluated at the difference of the branch-induced field displacements. In vacuum, the decoherence exponent equals half the mean number of gravitons radiated by the difference source. For a smooth Gaussian trajectory, it reduces to $Γ_{\rm vac}=(8/15)\,Gm^2d^4/(\hbar c^5τ^4)$, ranging from $10^{-89}$ to $10^{-61}$ across representative matter-wave platforms. For a general squeezed graviton vacuum, we obtain an exact expression in which squeezing either suppresses or enhances the vacuum response, depending on the squeezing phase. For the strongly squeezed state produced by inflation, this expression reduces to $Γ_{\rm inf}=(π/20)\,Ω_{\rm inf}(md^2H_0/\hbar)^2$ and reaches at most $\sim10^{-27}$ for optimistic parameters. Hence, the which-path decoherence induced by radiative gravitons is therefore negligible in current matter-wave interferometers.

</details>


### [102] [Using horizon shadows to distinguish a black hole and a white hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20945)
*Chengyu Bi,Zhoujian Cao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于广义相对论射线追踪技术，计算了克尔黑洞及其量子反弹后克尔白洞阶段的吸积盘成像。结果显示黑洞图像呈现月牙形辐射环与中心阴影，而白洞因参考系拖曳（frame-dragging）和透镜效应形成偏心不对称嵌套强度环结构。进一步引入偏振射线追踪，发现白洞偏振图像在环间存在偏振不连续性，该特征与黑洞不同，可为未来甚长基线干涉测量（VLBI）区分黑洞与白洞提供理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）等理论框架下，黑洞可能通过量子反弹（quantum bounce）演化为白洞。然而，现有观测手段尚难以区分黑洞与白洞的形态特征。本文旨在通过计算和对比两者在不同演化阶段的射线追踪成像与偏振特征，寻找可克服形态观测简并（morphological observational degeneracies）的识别依据。

Method: 采用广义相对论射线追踪（general relativistic ray-tracing）技术，分别计算克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）阶段和反弹后克尔白洞（Kerr white hole）阶段吸积盘的合成成像。在此基础上引入偏振射线追踪（polarized ray-tracing），分析偏振矢量在穿过白洞视界（horizon）及内部时空时受引力场和自旋拖曳影响后的偏振图像特征。

Result: 黑洞成像呈现月牙形辐射环（crescent emission ring）和中心阴影。白洞成像因来自前一宇宙的辐射穿透旋转白洞，在参考系拖曳和透镜效应作用下形成偏心不对称的嵌套强度环结构。偏振图像显示白洞的偏振矢量在空间旋转模式（spatial rotation patterns）和同心干涉条纹（concentric interference fringes）中呈现显著的环间偏振不连续性（inter-ring polarization discontinuity），该现象与黑洞的偏振行为不同。

Conclusion: 白洞独特的强度环结构和偏振环间不连续性特征为多波段和偏振干涉测量基线提供了克服形态观测简并的途径，可为未来甚长基线干涉测量（VLBI）区分黑洞与白洞提供理论指导。

Abstract: Within theoretical frameworks such as loop quantum gravity, black holes may evolve into white holes through a quantum bounce. This paper uses general relativistic ray-tracing techniques to calculate the ray-traced imaging of accretion disks from the previous cosmic stage during the Kerr black hole and post-bounce Kerr white hole phases. Calculations show that the black hole image presents a crescent emission ring and a central shadow. In contrast, after radiation from the previous universe penetrates the rotating white hole, eccentric and asymmetric nested intensity ring structures form in the synthetic image due to frame-dragging and lensing effects. We analyze the influence of spin parameters, observation inclinations, and accretion disk geometric configurations on the distribution of this nested ring structure using synthetic images and intensity profiles. Building upon this, we introduce polarized ray-tracing calculations for radiation across evolutionary stages. This process results in the polarization image features after the polarization vector is subjected to the gravitational field and spacetime spin dragging during the photon propagation through the white hole horizon and internal spacetime. The spatial rotation patterns and concentric interference fringes in the white hole polarization images exhibit a distinct inter-ring polarization discontinuity. This phenomenon differs from the polarization behavior of black holes. The intensity ring structures and polarization inter-ring discontinuity features provide multi-band and polarimetric interferometry baselines to overcome morphological observational degeneracies. This provides theoretical guidance for future very-long-baseline interferometry (VLBI) to distinguish black holes and white holes.

</details>

### [104] [The leading-soft cubic graviton self-interaction on the black-hole horizon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21066)
*Ayanendu Dutta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在GGV近视界框架的偶Regge-Wheeler规范下，将Einstein-Hilbert作用量展开至Schwarzschild视界附近的三阶，推导出引力子自相互作用，证明了领头软阶纵向极化自耦合为零的“消失定理”，并通过IBM Qiskit/Aer模拟了演化动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞视界附近量子引力效应中高阶引力子自相互作用的性质，特别是纵模（longitudinal polarization）在软极限下的耦合行为及其可模拟的实时量子动力学。

Method: 在偶Regge-Wheeler规范下，利用GGV近视界框架，将Einstein-Hilbert作用量展开至Schwarzschild视界附近的三阶（cubic order）并推导引力子自相互作用顶点。通过显式封闭形式约化逐项验证消失定理。在IBM Qiskit/Aer上模拟所得哈密顿量的实时动力学，并与精确对角化进行交叉校验。

Result: 核心结果是“消失定理”（vanishing theorem）：领头软阶（leading soft order）下，纯无迹纵模的自耦合恒为零，原因在于关闭迹/横标量扇区后，涨落退化为一个二维块，其√-g·R在每一阶κ均为欧拉导数（Euler derivative）。在唯一可模拟的多重态（ℓ=2）上，量子化顶点继承了约20%的软/方案系统误差。模拟结果验证了纵模通道的微扰刚性（perturbatively rigid），并测量了残差 dressing。对称精确的总占据截断首次获得了扇区分辨的能级统计。

Conclusion: 消失定理是框架特定的结论（偶RW规范、GGV扇区、领头软阶），并非广义相对论的规范不变定理。守恒荷仅被三次顶点破坏，打开了φφ→hh→4φ通道；升压谱无共振（gap→1/2）。所有电路结果与精确对角化一致，硬件执行因量化噪声预算而推迟。

Abstract: We expand the Einstein-Hilbert action to cubic order about the Schwarzschild horizon, in the even Regge-Wheeler gauge of the Gaddam-Groenenboom-'t~Hooft (GGV) near-horizon framework, and derive the cubic graviton self-interaction. Our central result is a `vanishing theorem': at leading soft order the self-coupling of the purely traceless longitudinal polarizations is identically zero, because with the trace/transverse-scalar sector switched off the fluctuation reduces to a two-dimensional block whose $\sqrt{-g}\,R$ is a total (Euler) derivative at every order in $κ$. We prove this by an explicit closed-form reduction and exhibit the cancellation term by term. It is a `framework-specific' statement, even RW gauge, GGV sector, leading soft order, not a gauge-invariant theorem of general relativity. The theorem is exact, but the quantized vertex inherits a $\sim\!20\%$ soft/scheme systematic at the only simulable multiplet ($\ell=2$), which we state explicitly. We then simulate the real-time dynamics of the resulting Hamiltonian on IBM Qiskit/Aer with exact cross-checks. Two structural facts, a conserved charge that only the cubic vertex violates, opening $φφ\to hh\to4φ$, and a provably resonance-free boost spectrum (gap $\to1/2$), already predict that the longitudinal channel is perturbatively rigid; the simulation confirms this quantitatively and measures the residual dressing ($d_{\rm eff}=1.06$; multiplicity far from thermal, Poisson, and Haar references) rather than discovering it. A symmetry-exact total-occupation truncation yields the first sector-resolved level statistics, indicative of intermediate behaviour on Hilbert spaces too small to be decisive. All circuit results agree with exact diagonalization, every headline number carries a stated systematic, and hardware execution is deferred behind a quantified noise budget.

### [105] [Spin-mediated modulation of chaos bound violation in Lorentz-violating black hole spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21165)
*Deyou Chen,Chuang Yang,Bingbing Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Bumblebee引力框架下，研究了粒子自旋如何调制洛伦兹破缺黑洞时空中的混沌边界（chaos bound）违反。通过分析静态球对称(A)dS黑洞中带电旋转粒子，揭示了自旋-曲率耦合、洛伦兹对称性破缺和宇宙学常数对混沌动力学的塑造作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索粒子自旋在洛伦兹破缺引力背景下对混沌边界违反的调制机制，以及自旋-曲率耦合、洛伦兹破缺参数和宇宙学常数如何共同影响黑洞时空的混沌动力学行为。

Method: 在Bumblebee引力框架下，构建洛伦兹破缺的静态球对称(A)dS黑洞时空；分析带电旋转粒子的运动动力学；检验混沌边界（chaos bound）违反条件，并考察自旋、洛伦兹破缺参数及宇宙学常数对临界角动量阈值和临界电荷的影响。

Result: 自旋提供了一种精细调节混沌边界违反的机制：较大自旋的粒子允许在较低角动量下进入违反区域；洛伦兹破缺参数通过缩小允许参数区域并降低临界电荷来抑制违反；更负的宇宙学常数既减小违反的参数区域，又增强了仍处于违反状态构型的违反幅度。

Conclusion: 自旋与洛伦兹对称性破缺效应共同调节轨道不稳定性（orbital instability）与视界性质之间的关系，从而决定了混沌边界违反的整体行为。

Abstract: We investigate how the particle spin modulates chaos bound violations in Lorentz-violating black hole spacetimes within the framework of Bumblebee gravity. By analyzing spinning charged particles in static spherically symmetric (A)dS black holes, we reveal the roles of spin--curvature coupling, Lorentz symmetry breaking, and the cosmological constant in shaping chaotic dynamics. The results show that the spin provides a fine-tuning mechanism for the chaos bound violation by modifying the critical angular momentum threshold, allowing particles with larger spin to access the violation regime at lower angular momenta. The Lorentz-violating parameter suppresses the violations by narrowing the allowed parameter region and reducing the critical charge. Meanwhile, the cosmological constant exhibits a dual influence: a more negative cosmological constant decreases the parameter region of violation while enhancing the violation magnitude for configurations that remain beyond the bound. These findings demonstrate that the spin and Lorentz symmetry breaking effects jointly modify the relationship between orbital instability and horizon properties.

### [106] [Zipoy--Voorhees spacetime with Maxwell and dilaton fields: exact solution and equatorial geodesics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21283)
*Haryanto M. Siahaan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过将Zipoy-Voorhees真空种子解（vacuum seed）依次进行提升（uplift）、洛伦兹推进（boost）和约化（reduction）操作，推导出四维Kaluza-Klein理论的一个新精确解——Zipoy-Voorhees-dilaton时空（Zipoy-Voorhees-dilaton spacetime）。该解是静态、轴对称、渐进平坦的构型，由种子尺度参数M、变形参数k和控制电荷的推进参数α刻画。文章系统分析了该时空的黑洞/奇点性质、ADM质量、电荷与膨胀子荷（dilaton charge）、赤道测地线、光子环阈值、最内稳定圆轨道（ISCO）、引力红移及阴影特征尺寸等物理量，并将结果与Schwarzschild情形进行比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kaluza-Klein理论中精确解析解的构造对于理解高维引力与低维有效理论之间的关系具有重要意义。Zipoy-Voorhees种子解提供了丰富的真空引力构型，引入膨胀子（dilaton）场和电荷后可拓展对非球对称带电引力系统的认识。

Method: 采用提升-推进-约化（uplift-boost-reduction）程序，将五维真空Zipoy-Voorhees种子解提升至五维，施加Lorentz推进后约化回四维，从而得到带膨胀子场和电荷的静态轴对称解。

Result: 当k=1时该解允许规则的黑洞解释；当k≠1时继承种子解在r=2M处的裸奇点。膨胀子荷满足与四极矩变形无关的代数约束。赤道光子环的阈值位于k=1/2，该结论对任意α均成立，推广了真空Zipoy-Voorhees情形的已知阈值。最内稳定圆轨道在(k,α)平面上的分布依赖于使用种子质量还是ADM质量单位。引力红移在r=2M面发散，使近奇点轨道不可见。以ADM质量单位计量的临界碰撞参数（影子特征尺寸）随电荷增大而收缩至Schwarzschild值以下。

Conclusion: 本文构造了Zipoy-Voorhees-dilaton时空这一新的Kaluza-Klein精确解，系统展示了其基本物理性质，特别是测地线结构和可观测特征（如阴影大小、红移等）随形变参数k与电荷参数α的变化规律，为研究非球对称带电引力系统提供了解析框架。

Abstract: We derive a new exact solution of four-dimensional Kaluza-Klein theory by applying the uplift-boost-reduction procedure to the Zipoy-Voorhees vacuum seed. The resulting Zipoy-Voorhees-dilaton spacetime is a static, axisymmetric, asymptotically flat configuration parametrised by a seed length scale $M$, the Zipoy-Voorhees deformation parameter $k$, and a boost parameter $α$ that controls the electric charge. For $k=1$ it admits a regular black-hole interpretation; for $k \neq 1$ it inherits the naked curvature singularity of the seed at $r=2M$. We extract the ADM mass, electric charge, and dilaton charge, finding that the dilaton charge obeys an algebraic constraint independent of the quadrupole deformation. The equatorial geodesics of neutral test particles and photons are studied in detail. A compact algebraic identity locates the exterior-photon-ring threshold at $k=1/2$ for all $α$, generalising the known threshold of the vacuum Zipoy-Voorhees case. The innermost stable circular orbit is mapped over the $(k,α)$ plane, and the comparison with Schwarzschild is shown to depend qualitatively on whether seed-mass or ADM-mass units are used. We further compute the gravitational redshift, which diverges on the $r=2M$ surface and renders the near-singularity orbits effectively invisible, and the critical impact parameter setting the characteristic shadow size, which in ADM-mass units shrinks below the Schwarzschild value as the charge grows.

### [107] [Cosmological initial data without periodic boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21308)
*Károly Csukás*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用爱因斯坦约束方程（Einstein constraint equations）的抛物-双曲（parabolic-hyperbolic）形式，生成带有局域各向异性完美流体扰动的宇宙学初始数据，避免了传统椭圆方法对边界条件和多重解问题的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准椭圆求解器（elliptic solvers）在求解爱因斯坦约束方程时，需要施加边界条件（如周期性边界），这可能引入系统性偏差（systematic biases），且在存在多个解时可能失效。本文旨在发展一种无需边界条件、且总能得到唯一解的新方法。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦约束方程的抛物-双曲形式，从原点处的正则数据向外演化和推进约束方程，从而生成宇宙学初始数据。自由指定的几何数据对应平坦弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker, FLRW）背景，物质部分则包含局域化的各向异性完美流体（perfect fluid）扰动。

Result: 该方法无需施加任何边界条件，因为约束方程是从原点正则数据向外演化的。与标准椭圆方法相比，该方法总能得到唯一解；本文通过数值实现成功生成了带有局域各向异性完美流体扰动的宇宙学初始数据。

Conclusion: 该抛物-双曲方法是一种可行且更优的宇宙学初始数据生成方案，特别适用于研究常用边界条件（如周期性边界）可能引入的系统性偏差，并且避免了椭圆求解器的多重解问题。

Abstract: We apply the parabolic-hyperbolic formulation of the Einstein constraint equations to generate cosmological initial data. The freely specifiable geometric data correspond to flat Friedmann--Lemaître--Robertson--Walker background, while the matter sector contains localized anisotropic perturbations of a perfect fluid. Unlike the standard approach, our method evolves the constraints outward from regular data at the origin and therefore requires no boundary conditions. This makes our method well suited as a starting point in investigating systematic biases introduced by commonly adopted boundary conditions, such as periodic boundaries. A second advantage concerns uniqueness: standard elliptic solvers may fail when multiple solutions exist, whereas solving the constraints as a well-posed evolutionary system always yields a unique solution. To demonstrate our method, we implement it numerically and generate cosmological initial data with localized anisotropic perfect fluid perturbations.

### [108] [Octupole moments and the non-universality of free-fall in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21314)
*Abraham I. Harte,Paul Ramond*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究广义相对论中八极矩（octupole moment）对自由落体非普适性（non-universality of free-fall）的贡献。在任意真空时空中，仅有八极矩的无迹（trace-free）分量影响物体运动，至少40个分量中的16个与运动定律解耦。通过两种分解（基于类时间架向量和零标架），作者分析了牛顿时空和Petrov D型完全相对论性真空时空（如Kerr）中的运动，发现八极矩可以产生四极矩无法实现的力矩，从而产生定性不同的效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论中，扩展体不一定沿测地线（geodesic）下落，加速度依赖于物体的角动量（angular momentum）以及多极矩（multipole moments）。不同物体的多极矩演化不同，导致自由落体非普适性。此前研究多聚焦于四极矩（quadrupole moment），本文旨在探究八极矩对此非普适性的具体贡献及其与四极矩的定性差异。

Method: 首先证明在任意真空时空中，只有八极矩的无迹分量影响物体运动，从而识别出40个八极矩分量中至少16个与运动定律解耦。随后获得无迹八极矩的两种分解：一种基于类时间架向量（timelike frame vector），另一种基于零标架（null tetrad）。将这些分解应用于牛顿时空和Petrov D型完全相对论性真空时空中的运动分析。

Result: 在牛顿时空中，质量矩（mass moments）产生通常的牛顿效应，而动量矩（momentum moments）决定物体的隐藏动量（hidden momentum），即动量与速度之间的不对准。在Petrov D型时空（如Kerr）中，八极矩能够产生四极矩无法实现的力矩，表明八极矩具有定性不同的效应。

Conclusion: 八极矩对广义相对论中自由落体的非普适性有独特贡献，其无迹分量是影响物体运动的关键部分。八极矩效应在定性上不同于四极矩，尤其在Petrov D型时空中可产生新类型的力矩。这深化了对扩展体在广义相对论中运动行为的理解。

Abstract: Extended bodies in general relativity do not necessarily fall along geodesics, but can be accelerated. These accelerations depend on an object's angular momentum, as well as on its quadrupole, octupole, and higher-order moments. However, these multipole moments can evolve differently from one body to another. Different bodies can thus fall differently, even with identical initial data. This paper examines how octupole moments contribute to the non-universality of free-fall in general relativity. We begin by showing that in arbitrary vacuum spacetimes, only the trace-free component of an octupole moment can affect an object's motion. It follows that at least 16 out of 40 octupole components decouple from the laws of motion. Then, we obtain two decompositions for trace-free octupole moments, one in terms of a timelike frame vector and the other in terms of a null tetrad. These decompositions are applied to motion both in generic Newtonian spacetimes and in fully-relativistic vacuum spacetimes that are of Petrov type D. In Newtonian spacetimes, the mass moments are shown to have their ordinary Newtonian effects, while the momentum moments determine a body's hidden momentum---the misalignment between its momentum and its velocity. In Petrov type D spacetimes (such as Kerr), we show that some torques that are impossible with quadrupole moments are possible with octupole moments. Octupole moments can thus have qualitatively-different effects from quadrupole moments.

</details>


### [109] [A story about a tipsy kangaroo: Reversible jump MCMC for model selection in the analysis of gravitational-wave signals from the coalescence of compact objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21484)
*Anna Puecher,Tim Dietrich,Hauke Koehn,Jonathan Gair,Gregory Ashton,Luca Negri,Anuradha Samajdar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍t-roo，一个基于可逆跳转马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（reversible jump Markov chain Monte Carlo）的采样器，能够对引力波信号中的致密双星并合事件进行跨模型推断，在一次分析中同时提供模型胜率（odds ratio）和参数后验分布，从而在比较多个模型时获得显著的计算优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波数据分析中常用的贝叶斯模型比较方法需要对每个模型分别进行分析并比较贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence），计算成本高昂。本文旨在开发一种能够直接在模型空间中进行采样的方法，以提高模型比较的效率。

Method: 本文提出t-roo采样器，基于可逆跳转马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（reversible jump Markov chain Monte Carlo, RJMCMC）方法，构建于已有的采样器eryn之上。该工具能够在一次运行中同时提供模型胜率（odds ratio）和参数后验分布（parameter posteriors），适用于比较不同类型的致密双星并合源，包括双黑洞（binary black hole）、双中子星（binary neutron star）和中子星-黑洞（neutron star-black hole）系统，以及同一类源的不同模型。

Result: 在注入测试（injection）中，t-roo的结果与巢式采样器（nested sampler）dynesty一致。通过对真实引力波事件GW190425和GW230529的分析，t-roo提供了关于中子星组分存在性的额外信息。

Conclusion: t-roo可适用于任何模型比较场景，尤其对下一代探测器（next-generation detectors）而言，在计算资源需求日益增长的背景下，该工具具有重要价值。

Abstract: Bayesian inference is commonly employed in the analysis of gravitational-wave signals not only to estimate the source parameters, but also for model selection. The latter provides insight into the physics of the source and has the potential to inform the direction for future model development. Although model comparison is usually performed by analyzing the data separately with different models and comparing the obtained Bayesian evidences, an alternative approach consists in sampling directly over the model itself. Here, we present t-roo, a reversible jump Markov chain Monte Carlo sampler capable of performing transdimensional inference on gravitational-wave signals from compact binary coalescences. Employing t-roo, a single analysis provides simultaneously the model odds ratio and the parameter posteriors for the favored models, hence yielding a potentially substantial computational advantage, particularly when comparing many models or analyzing highly informative data. t-roo is built on the sampler eryn and is specifically designed to compare models describing different kinds of sources, i.e., binary black hole, binary neutron star, or neutron star-black hole systems, as well as multiple models for the same source class. We validate the sampler on a set of injections, finding agreement with the results obtained with the nested sampler dynesty. We then use t-roo to analyze the real events GW190425 and GW230529, for which the system's parameters alone do not provide conclusive evidence of the presence of a neutron star component. t-roo can be adapted to any model-comparison scenario, thus providing a valuable tool in particular for next-generation detectors, where analyzing data separately with competing models becomes computationally even more demanding.

</details>

### [110] [Entanglement asymmetry and quantum Mpemba effect for Kramers-Wannier duality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21226)
*Milo Vescovo,Pasquale Calabrese,Filiberto Ares*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文引入Kramers-Wannier纠缠不对称性（entanglement asymmetry）作为量子信息度量，研究横场伊辛链中非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetry）的平衡与非平衡行为，在量子淬火中发现了量子Mpemba效应，即在特定条件下远离平衡的态反而更快恢复Kramers-Wannier对称性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kramers-Wannier对偶性（duality）是非可逆对称性的典型代表，但人们对其在远离临界点和非平衡态下的性质所知甚少。本文旨在引入一种量子信息度量来量化这种对称性的破缺，并研究其平衡与非平衡动力学行为。

Method: 作者定义了Kramers-Wannier纠缠不对称性，用于量化横场伊辛链（transverse-field Ising chain）中非可逆对称性的破缺程度。在平衡态下，分析该量在有序相与无序相之间的交叉行为；在非平衡态下，研究从两个有能隙相（gapped phases）向临界点淬火（quantum quench）后的动力学演化，并结合解析与数值证据揭示量子Mpemba效应。

Result: 平衡态下，Kramers-Wannier纠缠不对称性在有序相与无序相之间表现出显著交叉，在临界点处出现尖锐下降，且随着子体系（subsystem）尺寸增大该下降愈发明显。淬火动力学中，该不对称性衰减至零，表明非可逆对称性在动力学上得以恢复。在特定条件下观察到了量子Mpemba效应（quantum Mpemba effect），即初始态远离平衡的系统反而更快地恢复对称性。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了纠缠不对称性作为非平衡态下非可逆对称性的有效探测工具，为量子多体系统中对偶性（duality）的动力学研究开辟了新视角。

Abstract: The Kramers-Wannier duality is the prototypical example of a non-invertible symmetry, yet little is known about its fate away from criticality and out of equilibrium. We introduce the Kramers-Wannier entanglement asymmetry, a quantum-information measure that quantifies the breaking of this non-invertible symmetry in the transverse-field Ising chain. We first investigate its equilibrium properties, showing that it exhibits a striking crossover between the ordered and disordered phases together with a pronounced dip at the critical point that becomes increasingly sharp with subsystem size. We then study quantum quenches from both gapped phases to criticality and show that the Kramers-Wannier entanglement asymmetry decays to zero, signaling the dynamical restoration of the non-invertible symmetry. Remarkably, we uncover the emergence of a quantum Mpemba effect: under suitable conditions, states initially farther from equilibrium restore the Kramers-Wannier symmetry faster than states prepared closer to it. We provide both analytical and numerical evidence for this phenomenon and identify the mechanism responsible for its occurrence. Our work establishes entanglement asymmetry as a powerful probe of non-invertible symmetries beyond equilibrium and opens new perspectives on the dynamics of dualities in quantum many-body systems.

</details>


### [111] [Thermal pseudo-transitions in a frustrated spin-pseudospin sawtooth chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21359)
*Onofre Rojas,Jozef Strečka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对包含铜离子三种价态的自旋-赝自旋X锯齿链进行了精确分析，作为一维铜氧化物的最小模型。通过转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix method）导出了自由能的精确表达式及伪临界线（pseudo-critical line）的解析条件。基态分析揭示了一个反铁磁相和三个具有不同残余熵（residual entropy）的阻挫相，有限温度下这些相边界演化为窄熵脊（entropy ridges），表现出伪转变（pseudo-transition）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在构建并精确求解一个包含自旋（spin）和电荷（charge）自由度竞争的最小模型，以理解一维铜氧化物中锯齿几何结构诱导的阻挫（frustration）和伪转变行为。

Method: 采用转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix method）对自旋-赝自旋（spin–pseudospin）X锯齿链模型进行精确分析，推导自由能的精确表达式及伪临界线的解析条件，并通过局域关联函数（local correlation functions）刻画不同关联机制的协同重排。

Result: 基态分析发现一个反铁磁相和三个具有不同残余熵的阻挫相；有限温度下相边界演化为窄熵脊，比热和避免交叉标度（avoided-crossing scale）在伪临界温度处呈现尖锐但连续的峰值，物理关联长度（physical correlation length）可能由不同的次主导本征值控制。

Conclusion: 锯齿几何结构促进了阻挫和短程相干性，导致显著的伪转变行为；局域关联函数揭示了从电荷主导到磁关联主导的协同重排过程。

Abstract: We present an exact analysis of a spin--pseudospin X sawtooth chain that incorporates three distinct valence states of copper ions and serves as a minimal model for one-dimensional cuprates composed of corner-sharing copper triangles. The model includes magnetic exchange and electrostatic coupling constants both along the base sites and between base and apex sites capturing the competition between spin and charge degrees of freedom. Using the transfer-matrix method, we derive exact expressions for the free energy and obtain an analytical condition defining the pseudo-critical line associated with pronounced thermodynamic anomalies. The ground-state analysis reveals, besides an antiferromagnetic phase, three frustrated phases characterized by distinct residual entropies. At finite temperatures, these zero-temperature phase boundaries evolve into narrow entropy ridges signaling pseudo-transitions between the corresponding quasi-phases. The specific heat and the avoided-crossing scale exhibit sharp but continuous peaks at the pseudo-critical temperature, whereas the physical correlation length may be controlled by a different subleading eigenvalue. Local correlation functions uncover a cooperative rearrangement from charge-dominated to magnetically correlated regimes. Our results demonstrate that the sawtooth geometry promotes frustration and short-range coherence leading to pronounced pseudo-transition behavior.

</details>


### [112] [Free-volume origin of diverging direct correlations in hard crystals: insights from an exact one-dimensional model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21379)
*Alessandro Simon,Martin Oettel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文通过一维硬杆Percus泛函的精确解，揭示了三维硬球晶体中二阶直接关联函数（second-order direct correlation function）的大振幅和特定空间形式的自由体积起源，指出其$1/n_{\mathrm{vac}}$依赖性是空位主导极限，而空间结构源于硬杆权重函数对排除区间与自由体积区域的几何选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维硬球晶体中的二阶直接关联函数展现出比液态对应物大得多的振幅（量级为$1/n_{\mathrm{vac}}$，$n_{\mathrm{vac}}$为空位浓度）和更短程、更强烈的空间结构形态。论文旨在分离并解释这两个问题——相关性为何如此之大，以及为何具有这种特定形式。

Method: 利用一维硬杆Percus泛函（one-dimensional Percus functional）的精确解进行分析。周期性类晶体密度由高斯峰表示，占据概率$q=1-n_{\mathrm{vac}}$。通过局部插入自由体积$A(x)$的最小值$A_{\mathrm{min}}$表达热力学量，进而推导一阶和二阶直接关联函数中的奇异依赖关系$c^{(1)}\sim\ln A_{\mathrm{min}}$和$c^{(2)}\sim-1/A_{\mathrm{min}}$。并求解非均匀Ornstein–Zernike方程（inhomogeneous Ornstein–Zernike equation）以数值验证。

Result: 一阶和二阶直接关联函数分别包含$c^{(1)}\sim\ln A_{\mathrm{min}}$和$c^{(2)}\sim-1/A_{\mathrm{min}}$的奇异依赖。观测到的$1/n_{\mathrm{vac}}$依赖是空位主导极限$n_{\mathrm{vac}}\ggΔ_{αa}$的结果，而非最一般情形。$c^{(2)}$的空间形式具有独立的几何起源：硬杆权重函数选择那些排除区间及其边界与小区间自由体积区域相交的构型，由此产生与底层周期性密度相关的平台、边缘和局域脊状结构。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一个最小自由体积解释，同时涵盖了晶体直接关联函数的振幅大小和晶格特定空间形式。数值求解非均匀Ornstein–Zernike方程进一步展示了这些奇异直接关联如何重新分布在总关联函数和对关联函数中。

Abstract: Second order direct correlation functions in three-dimensional hard-sphere crystals have much larger amplitudes (of the order of $1/n_{\mathrm{vac}}$ where $n_{\mathrm{vac}}$ is the vacancy concentration) and a more strongly structured spatial form of apparent shorter range than their liquid-state counterparts. We separate the two underlying questions---why the correlations are large and why they have the form they do---using the exact one-dimensional Percus functional for hard rods. A periodic crystal-like density is represented by Gaussian peaks with occupation probability $q=1-n_{\mathrm{vac}}$. The relevant thermodynamic quantity is the local insertion free volume $A(x)$. Its minimum can be written as $A_{\mathrm{min}} =Δ_{αa}+(1-Δ_{αa})n_{\mathrm{vac}}$, where $Δ_{αa}$ is the residual free volume at full occupation caused by finite localization (characterized by a width parameter $α$) and lattice spacing $a$. The first and second direct correlations therefore contain the singular dependences $c^{(1)}\sim\ln A_{\mathrm{min}} $ and $c^{(2)} \sim-1/A_{\mathrm{min}} $. The observed $1/n_{\mathrm{vac}}$ dependence is the vacancy-dominated limit $n_{\mathrm{vac}}\ggΔ_{αa}$, rather than the most general result. The spatial form of $c^{(2)}$ has a separate geometrical origin: the hard-rod weight functions select configurations in which exclusion intervals and their boundaries intersect regions of small free volume. This produces plateaus, edges, and localized ridges tied to the underlying periodic density. A numerical solution of the inhomogeneous Ornstein--Zernike equation shows how these singular direct correlations are redistributed in the total and pair correlations. The model provides a minimal free-volume explanation for both the magnitude and the lattice-specific form of crystalline direct correlation functions.

</details>


### [113] [Optimal feedback control under stepwise equilibration and partial observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21523)
*Francesco Mottes,Michael P. Brenner*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究将部分可观测的反馈控制问题简化为哈密顿量更新的贝尔曼递归，并通过解析求解谐波陷阱平移问题，揭示最优协议平衡信息利用与目标推进，证明测量记录的热力学成本始终超过信息提取收益，导致最优周期数有限且净功非负。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多微观机器依赖噪声信号驱动非平衡（nonequilibrium）变换，并在时间尺度分离的机制下运行；现有控制方法在处理部分可观测控制问题时面临挑战，亟需建立精确简化的理论框架。

Method: 研究考虑系统在快速、测量条件化的能量景观变化之间达到平衡的反馈协议；在该极限下，部分可观测控制问题被精确简化为一个有限时域的哈密顿量更新贝尔曼递归（finite-horizon Bellman recursion over Hamiltonian updates）；针对噪声位置测量下谐波陷阱（harmonic trap）向指定目标平移的情形，求解该递归的解析解。

Result: 最优协议在响应估计涨落与推进目标之间取得平衡，早期利用信息而接近截止期限时强制执行端点；最小功分解为正的热力学长度输运成本（thermodynamic-length transport cost）和负的信息驱动提取项，后者由测量所解析的平衡涨落分数决定；当固定干预成本超过每周期渐近提取量时，最优周期数为有限值；在谐波平移情形下，创建与重置测量记录的最小热力学成本始终超过该阈值，因此任何测量信道下的最优周期数均为有限，净功非负。

Conclusion: 该研究为部分可观测反馈控制提供了精确求解框架，揭示了信息获取与热力学成本之间的基本权衡，证明了测量记录本身的成本限制了控制性能，确保净功不为负值。

Abstract: Many microscopic machines rely on noisy signals to direct nonequilibrium transformations and operate in a timescale-separated regime. We consider feedback protocols in which a system equilibrates between rapid, measurement-conditioned changes of its energy landscape. In this limit, the partially observable control problem reduces exactly to a finite-horizon Bellman recursion over Hamiltonian updates. For a harmonic trap translated to a prescribed target under noisy position measurements, we solve this recursion analytically. The optimal protocol balances its response to the estimated fluctuation against progress toward the target, exploiting information early while enforcing the endpoint near the deadline. The minimum work decomposes into a positive thermodynamic-length transport cost and a negative information-enabled extraction term set by the fraction of equilibrium fluctuations resolved by the measurement. When a fixed intervention cost exceeds the asymptotic extraction per cycle, it selects a finite optimal number of cycles. We show that, in this translated harmonic case, the minimum thermodynamic cost of creating and resetting the measurement record always exceeds this threshold, making the optimal cycle count finite and the net work non-negative for any measurement channel.

</details>

### [114] [Lax pairs and $r$-matrices for some two-dimensional isotropic oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20983)
*Govind S. Krishnaswami,Garima Rajpoot,Srividya N. Vaidya*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维圆对称谐振子、Fock-Darwin型谐振子及四次非简谐振子的Lax对（Lax pair）构造，发现了具有谱参数（spectral parameter）的4×4和2×2块状Lax对，并推广到包含转动能的各向同性振子及Rajeev-Ranken模型，同时给出了相应的动力学期望r矩阵（dynamical r-matrix）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维各向同性谐振子虽然是双哈密顿（bi-Hamiltonian）系统，但其递归算子（recursion operator）无法导出Lax对，且从简谐Calogero模型取极限也无法获得此类对。因此，需要寻找该超可积（superintegrable）系统及其他相关非简谐振子系统本身的Lax对构造方法。

Method: 针对二维圆对称谐振子，构造了4×4块状Lax对（含谱参数），给出两个对易的守恒模能量及对应的动力学期望r矩阵；进一步发现2×2 Lax对，其所有三个独立守恒量满足非阿贝尔泊松代数（nonabelian Poisson algebra）。对于四次非简谐振子，构造了su(2) Lax对及r矩阵族，并推广至带转动能的各向同性振子（即含四次势的Fock-Darwin振子）。通过变量变换，这些构造也适用于Rajeev-Ranken模型。

Result: 获得了超可积简谐振子的4×4和2×2 Lax对，其中2×2 Lax对的守恒量并非全部对易，提供了一个反例。成功构造了二次+四次各向同性非简谐振子的su(2) Lax对及r矩阵，并扩展到含转动能的Fock-Darwin振子。Rajeev-Ranken模型虽然具有非正则泊松结构（noncanonical Poisson structure），但通过变量变换也可适用相同的Lax对和r矩阵。

Conclusion: 二维圆对称谐振子存在形式不同的Lax对，其守恒量的代数结构（对易或非对易）取决于Lax对的维数选择。所构造的Lax对和r矩阵家族能够统一描述谐振子、四次非简谐振子、Fock-Darwin振子及Rajeev-Ranken模型，展示了这些系统之间深层的可积结构关联。

Abstract: This paper concerns Lax pairs for circularly symmetric harmonic, Fock-Darwin-type and quartic anharmonic oscillators in two dimensions. Although the 2d isotropic harmonic oscillator is bi-Hamiltonian, its recursion operator does not lead to a Lax pair, nor do we obtain such a pair by taking a limit of the harmonic Calogero model. On the other hand, we show that this superintegrable harmonic oscillator admits a $4 \times 4$ block-form Lax pair with spectral parameter giving two conserved mode energies in involution and a corresponding dynamical $r$-matrix. Interestingly, we also find $2 \times 2$ Lax pairs with spectral parameter that give all three independent conserved quantities satisfying a nonabelian Poisson algebra, thereby providing a simple example of a Lax pair whose conserved quantities are not all in involution. Next, we construct a family of $su(2)$ Lax pairs and $r$-matrices for the quadratic+quartic isotropic anharmonic oscillator. This is then extended to an isotropic oscillator with a rotational energy, which may be viewed as the Fock-Darwin oscillator with a quartic potential. With a change of variables, these Lax pairs and $r$-matrices also apply to the Rajeev-Ranken model, although its noncanonical Poisson structure is distinct from that of the anharmonic oscillator.

</details>

### [115] [Monte Carlo Studies of Twisted Bilayer Graphene: Strain and Thermal Fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20619)
*Johannes S. Hofmann,Patrick Ledwith,Ashvin Vishwanath,Jong Yeon Lee,Erez Berg*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文利用无符号问题量子蒙特卡罗（sign-problem-free quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，系统研究了中性点处扭转双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）随扭转角、单轴异质应变和温度变化的相图。发现在零温零应变下，随扭转角减小系统从狄拉克半金属连续相变为Kramers谷间相干（KIVC）相。有限应变下，KIVC相在更小扭转角处进一步转变为各向异性半金属。在KIVC区域内，熵随温度急剧上升并在中等温度范围内达到类似Mott绝缘体的平台值。谱函数随扭转角连续演化，低温下能隙从K点移至Γ点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解中性点处扭转双层石墨烯在扭转角、应变和温度共同作用下的完整相图，揭示连续相变、熵行为以及谱函数演化的机制，特别是KIVC相的熵平台与拓扑阻碍局部紧束缚描述之间的矛盾。

Method: 采用无符号问题量子蒙特卡罗（sign-problem-free quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，系统地扫描扭转角θ、单轴异质应变ε和温度T三个参数空间，研究中性点（charge neutrality）处的物相行为。

Result: 在T=0、零应变下，随θ减小发生从狄拉克半金属（Dirac semimetal）到有能隙的Kramers谷间相干（KIVC）相的连续相变。有限应变下，在更小θ处KIVC相进一步连续转变为Γ点附近有能隙激发各向异性半金属。KIVC区域内熵在15K至40K区间达到接近Mott类局域电子的平台值。低温下谱函数能隙从K点移至Γ点；中等温度下谱函数从狄拉克半金属光谱连续演化为近魔角处无能隙Γ中心准粒子光谱。

Conclusion: 明确了扭转双层石墨烯在中性点处的丰富相图，包括两种连续相变和KIVC相中违反常规紧束缚描述的熵平台行为。提出各向异性半金属与Mott半金属的实验区分方法，为后续实验验证提供理论依据。

Abstract: We study the phase diagram of twisted bilayer graphene at charge neutrality as a function of twist angle $θ$, uniaxial heterostrain $\varepsilon$, and temperature $T$ using sign-problem-free quantum Monte Carlo simulations. At $T=0$ and zero strain, we find a continuous transition from a Dirac semimetal to a gapped Kramers inter-valley coherent (KIVC) phase as $θ$ decreases toward the magic angle. With finite strain, the KIVC phase undergoes a further continuous transition at smaller $θ$ into an anisotropic semimetal with gapless excitations near the center of the moiré Brillouin zone. In the KIVC regime, the entropy rises sharply with temperature and plateaus at $15\,\text{K} \lesssim T \lesssim 40\,\text{K}$ near the value expected from a Mott-like regime of localized electrons with nearly uncorrelated spin, valley, and orbital degrees of freedom, despite the topological obstruction preventing a localized tight-binding description of the active bands. The spectral function evolves continuously with $θ$: at low $T$, a gap opens at the $K$ points and the minimal gap shifts to $Γ$ as $θ$ decreases; at intermediate $T$, the spectral function smoothly interpolates between a Dirac semimetal spectrum with coherent $K$-point quasiparticles and a spectrum with gapless $Γ$-centered quasiparticles near the magic angle. The later can be a anisotropic or a Mott semimetal and we discuss how to distiguish them in experiment.

</details>


### [116] [Colloquium: Semi-Dirac Fermions in Quantum Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20627)
*Bruno Uchoa,Mohamed M. Elsayed,Valeri N. Kotov,Yinming Shao,Dmitri N. Basov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半狄拉克费米子作为一类新奇准粒子，具有方向依赖的色散关系，位于拓扑 Lifshitz 相变边界，其基础性质和多体相互作用尚未被充分理解。作者旨在系统梳理该领域的最新理论和实验进展，为后续研究提供全面参考。

Method: 本文为综述性研究，通过整理与分析人工晶格和量子材料中的实验证据，结合理论视角对半狄拉克费米子的多体问题（many-body problem）进行探讨，重点关注与实验可观测物理量（physical observables）相关的理论预测。

Result: 半狄拉克费米子同时具备二次型色散（quadratic dispersion）（类伽利略不变粒子）和线性色散（linear dispersion）（类无质量相对论粒子）两种特征，取决于运动方向；这些粒子存在于费米面连通性连续变化所导致的拓扑 Lifshitz 相变（topological Lifshitz transitions）相界处；已有来自人工晶格和量子材料的实验证据支持其存在。

Conclusion: 半狄拉克费米子的研究已取得显著进展，实验表明其在人工晶格和量子材料中均存在；理论上的多体问题仍需进一步研究，特别是与实验相关的物理可观测量（physical observables）有待深入探索。

Abstract: This article reviews the recent progress on the subject of semi-Dirac fermions, two dimensional quasiparticles that disperse quadratically, as Galilean invariant particles, or linearly, as massless relativistic particles, depending on their direction of motion. These particles exist at a phase boundary set by the continuous change in the connectivity of Fermi surfaces, known as topological Lifshitz transitions. The basic properties and the current experimental evidence of the existence of these particles in both synthetic lattices and quantum materials are presented. The many-body problem of semi-Dirac fermions is discussed from a theoretical perspective with an eye to physical observables of relevance to experiments.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 结合解析推导（手性玻色子场论）与数值计算（基于矩阵乘积态（matrix product state）的方法和精确对角化（exact diagonalization））对模型进行系统研究。

Result: 相变点包含一个不寻常的Lifshitz相变（Lifshitz transition），动力学临界指数（dynamical critical exponent）z=3；手性相为部分自旋极化相（partially spin-polarized phase），自发破缺SU(2)对称性；该相同时存在二次色散的铁磁“磁振子”（magnon）模式和Luttinger液体（Luttinger liquid）特有的幂律奇异性与线性色散激发。

Abstract: We study the zero-temperature properties of a spin-$1/2$ Heisenberg chain with an additional three-site chiral term of strength $g$. The model is known to be integrable and previous work using Bethe ansatz has identified a phase transition from the usual critical state for $g< g_c = 2/π$ to a chiral phase for $g>g_c$. Here we combine analytical and computational approaches to demonstrate that the transition point comprises an unusual Lifshitz transition with dynamical critical exponent $z=3$, and the chiral phase is a partially spin-polarized phase which spontaneously breaks SU(2) symmetry. We derive a strongly interacting chiral boson field theory for the critical point, and show that even its small-momentum, low-energy response is non-trivial. We also determine the universal properties of the chiral phase, and specifically show that it has a simultaneous quadratically dispersing ferromagnetic "magnon" mode coexisting with the power-law singularities and linearly dispersing excitations typical of a Luttinger liquid. Our conclusions are validated using numerics based on matrix product state methods and exact diagonalization.

### [120] [Gaplessness indicator by topologically trivial twisting operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20944)
*Yuan Yao,Linhao Li,Feng-Feng Song*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了U(1)对称一维量子多体系统存在能隙（gapped）的若干普适必要条件，并证明了在热力学极限下拓扑平凡的扭曲算子的基态期望值必须以特定有限尺寸标度趋近于1，违反该条件可指示系统无能隙（gaplessness）。通过静态结构因子（static structure factor）可导出任意高阶的无能隙指标，且对拓扑平凡扭曲算子的运用克服了先前拓扑非平凡方法在实验可观测性上的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前利用拓扑非平凡（topologically nontrivial）扭曲算子判断能隙的方法在实验可观测性上存在局限，无法通过静态结构因子导出高阶无能隙指标。本文旨在提出拓扑平凡（topologically trivial）的扭曲算子作为替代方案，从而获得实验上更易检验且信息更丰富的判据。

Method: 通过理论推导建立U(1)对称一维系统存在能隙的必要条件：拓扑平凡扭曲算子的基态期望值在热力学极限下需以特定有限尺寸标度趋近于1。利用该算子的拓扑平凡性，从静态结构因子出发导出无穷多个任意高阶的无能隙指标。同时结合解析计算与数值计算检验所得结果的有效性与一致性。

Result: 拓扑平凡扭曲算子的期望值趋近1的有限尺寸标度可作为能隙的判据；其违反可指示U(1)对称哈密顿量的无能隙性。由此可构造无穷多个基于静态结构因子的高阶无能隙指标，这些指标在真实实验中可观测，弥补了此前拓扑非平凡方法无法做到的实验可操作性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于拓扑平凡扭曲算子的能隙必要条件为U(1)对称一维量子多体系统提供了实验上可行的普适判据，解析与数值结果验证了该方法的有效性与自洽性。

Abstract: We propose several general necessary conditions for quantum many-body system in one dimension respecting U(1) symmetry to be gapped. We show that the ground-state expectation value of topologically trivial twisting operators must approach unity in the thermodynamic limit with a certain finite-size scaling. Equivalently, its violation can indicate gaplessness of U(1)-symmetric Hamiltonians. The topological triviality of such a twisting operator enables us to derive infinitely many other gaplessness indicators by static structure factor to any order in real experiments, which are impossible to obtain by earlier topologically nontrivial twisting operators. We also apply analytic and numerical calculations to test the efficiency and consistency of our results.

Abstract: A considerable phonon thermal Hall effect was recently discovered across a diverse collection of materials.
