### [122] [Long-wavelength density response and momentum resolution in strange-metal charge spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21206)
*Ilmo Sung*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过将动量分辨的电子能量损失谱（EELS）与光学谱学衔接，利用 Ward 恒等式证明，在长波长极限下，任意均匀 U(1) 守恒金属的密度响应必须满足 χ''(q,ω) ∝ q² 渐近行为；进一步给出一个定理，指出任何具有自相似 q 缩放轮廓且二阶矩有界的归一化动量分辨核（momentum-resolution kernel）仅改变该行为的前因子而不改变 q² 标度律。这一结果对奇异金属 Bi-2212 中近局域有限 q 连续谱构成约束，需通过合适的电动力学转换后才能应用于屏蔽损失函数和表面 EELS 观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇异金属 Bi₂Sr₂CaCu₂O₈₊ₓ（Bi-2212）的动量分辨 EELS 实验观察到一种几乎动量无关的宽电荷连续谱（broad charge continuum），而光学谱学则给出金属性局域电导率。这两种观测之间看似矛盾，本文旨在建立连接这两个能区（无限长波长与有限动量）的长波长响应函数——即均匀体电荷密度极化率（proper homogeneous bulk charge-density polarization），并揭示其物理约束。

Method: 从 Ward 恒等式（Ward identity）出发，推导出均匀 U(1) 守恒金属中密度响应虚部 χ''_{ρρ}(q,ω) 与纵电导率实部 Re σ_L(q,ω) 之间的关系：χ''(q,ω) = q² Re σ_L(q,ω)/ω。随后证明一个一般性定理：任何非负、归一化、具有自相似 q 缩放轮廓（self-similar q-scaled profile）、均匀有界二阶矩且二阶矩尾部收敛的动量分辨核，在保持该关系的前提下仅改变前因子（prefactor），不改变 q² 渐近行为。

Result: 该定理表明，若 Bi-2212 中近局域有限 q 连续谱（nearly local finite-q continuum）能连续连接到同一体响应的正则金属性光学极限（regular metallic optical limit），则该连续谱自然由交叉面（crossover surface）q_*(ω,T) 描述。任何不满足该 q² 渐近行为的实现都将违背 Ward 恒等式或核的正则性假设。

Conclusion: 本文建立的定理是对均匀体密度响应或其正 q 缩放卷积的约束；对于屏蔽损失函数（screened loss functions）和表面 EELS 观测量，需要在应用该约束之前进行相应的电动力学转换（electrodynamic conversion）。该工作为理解奇异金属中电荷动力学从光学到有限动量区域的连续性提供了严格的理论框架。

Abstract: Momentum-resolved electron energy-loss spectroscopy (EELS) on strange-metal Bi$_2$Sr$_2$CaCu$_2$O$_{8+x}$ (Bi-2212) observes a broad charge continuum that is nearly momentum independent over an extended finite-momentum regime, whereas optical spectroscopy determines a metallic local conductivity. We analyze the long-wavelength response function that connects these regimes: the proper homogeneous bulk charge-density polarization. For any homogeneous $U(1)$-conserving metal whose longitudinal matter conductivity remains finite in the $q\to0$ limit at fixed nonzero frequency, the Ward identity gives $χ''_{ρρ}({\bf q},ω)=q^2\operatorname{Re}σ_L({\bf q},ω)/ω$. We then prove that any nonnegative normalized momentum-resolution kernel with a self-similar $q$-scaled profile, uniformly bounded second moment, and tight second-moment tails preserves this $q^2$ asymptotic behavior, changing only the prefactor. Consequently, a nearly local finite-$q$ continuum in Bi-2212, if continuously connected to a regular metallic optical limit of the same proper bulk response, is naturally described by a crossover surface $q_\ast(ω,T)$. The theorem is a constraint on the proper bulk density response, or on a positive $q$-scaled convolution of it; screened loss functions and surface EELS observables require the corresponding electrodynamic conversion before the constraint is applied.

### [123] [Shiba duality and $η$-altermagnetism: Pairing and charge orders in bipartite attractive Hubbard models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21430)
*Yu-Ping Lin*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出η-交错磁（η-altermagnetism, η-ALM）概念，通过Shiba对偶将交错磁（altermagnetism）原理从自旋空间映射到η-赝自旋空间，将其定义为Bogoliubov-de Gennes（BdG）框架下配对与电荷序中的交错磁对应物。研究证明，在二分格点上的半填充纯净Hubbard模型中，该对偶将排斥驱动的反铁磁（AFM）与吸引驱动的η-反铁磁（η-AFM）联系起来，并通过各向异性次近邻跳跃破缺Kramers简并，产生具有奇偶宇称区分和p/d/f波分裂结构的η-ALM。最后讨论了可能的推广与实验探测途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将交错磁（altermagnetism）的概念从自旋空间扩展到Bogoliubov-de Gennes（BdG）框架下的配对与电荷序中，建立一种新的交错磁形式——η-交错磁（η-altermagnetism, η-ALM）。

Method: 利用Shiba对偶将动量依赖的能带分裂从自旋映射到η-赝自旋；通过各向异性次近邻跳跃破缺由$\mathcal{\tilde{P}}\mathcal{\tilde{T}}$对称性保护的Kramers简并；在棋盘格和蜂窝格点上进行Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov数值计算。

Result: η-ALM分为奇宇称（奇宇称η-赝自旋分裂）与偶宇称（自旋-η锁定分裂）两类；数值计算在棋盘格和蜂窝格点上发现了p波、d波和f波分裂结构的η-ALM。

Conclusion: Shiba对偶为在配对和电荷序中实现交错磁提供了一个统一的理论框架；η-ALM具有丰富的对称性和能带分裂结构，可能通过实验探测加以验证与推广。

Abstract: We show that Shiba duality maps the altermagnetic principle of momentum-dependent band splitting from spin to $η$-pseudospin, defining $η$-altermagnetism ($η$-ALM) as a Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) counterpart of ALM in pairing and charge orders. In half-filled pure Hubbard models on bipartite lattices, the duality relates repulsion-driven antiferromagnetism (AFM) to attraction-driven $η$-AFM with uniform singlet pairing and staggered charge-density modulation. In the BdG bands, the Shiba-dual parity-time-reversal $\mathcal{\tilde{P}}\mathcal{\tilde{T}}$ symmetry protects a Kramers degeneracy of $η$-pseudospin. Anisotropic second-neighbor hopping breaks this degeneracy and generates $η$-ALM. Odd-parity $η$-ALM shows $η$-pseudospin splitting, whereas even-parity $η$-ALM has spin-$η$-locked splitting. Hartree-Fock-Bogoliubov computations on checkerboard and honeycomb lattices find $η$-ALMs with $p$-, $d$-, and $f$-wave splitting structures. Possible generalizations and experimental probes are discussed.

</details>


### [124] [Interlayer interactions reshape charge-density wave through electronic elasticity in 4H$_{\mathrm{b}}$-TaS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21470)
*Carolina A. Marques,Martha Rösler,Berk Zengin,Aleš Cahlík,Edoardo Martino,Konstantin Semeniuk,Helmuth Berger,László Forró,Ana Akrap,Fabian D. Natterer*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过4H_b-TaS₂异质结模型，利用扫描隧道显微镜（STM）与准粒子干涉分析，发现非公度电荷密度波（incommensurate CDW）因层间堆垛配准而呈现离散的压缩（-2.3%）与拉伸（+3.2%）弹性态，并通过能带偏移揭示电子弹性（electronic elasticity）是层间弱相互作用调控低能电子结构的内在机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状量子材料中非公度电荷密度波（incommensurate charge-density waves, CDWs）的序波矢在名义相同的样品中也存在显著变化，这掩盖了其本征电子性质。本文旨在揭示该变异的内在起源。

Method: 以4H_b-TaS₂为模型异质结（由1T层上的公度CDW与1H层上的非公度CDW交替构成），采用低温扫描隧道显微镜（low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy），结合傅里叶分析（Fourier analysis）与准粒子干涉分析（quasiparticle-interference analysis），利用晶格钉扎的1T CDW作为内部参考。

Result: 发现相邻1H CDW因层间堆垛配准（interlayer registry）而呈现离散的压缩态（-2.3%）与拉伸态（+3.2%）弹性状态；对应平带（flat band）产生数个meV的偏移，表明弱层间相互作用通过非公度CDW的本征弹性重塑低能电子结构。

Conclusion: 电子弹性（electronic elasticity）是层间弱相互作用控制范德华异质结（van der Waals heterostructures）中关联电子态的一种机制。

Abstract: Incommensurate charge-density waves (CDWs) in layered quantum materials frequently exhibit widely varying ordering wave vectors, even among nominally identical samples, obscuring their intrinsic electronic properties. Here we identify an inherent origin of this variability through the electronic elasticity of an incommensurate CDW using the model heterostructure 4H$_{\mathrm{b}}$-TaS$_2$, composed of alternating commensurate CDW on 1T and incommensurate CDW on 1H layers. Low-temperature scanning tunneling microscopy, combined with Fourier and quasiparticle-interference analysis, exploits the lattice-pinned 1T CDW as an internal reference to resolve discrete compressive ($-2.3\%$) and tensile ($+3.2\%$) elastic states of the neighboring 1H CDW selected by the interlayer registry of the adjacent layers. Corresponding few-meV shifts of a flat band demonstrate that weak interlayer interactions reshape the low-energy electronic structure through the intrinsic elasticity of the incommensurate CDW. These findings establish electronic elasticity as a mechanism by which subtle interlayer interactions control correlated electronic states in van der Waals heterostructures.

</details>


### [125] [Pseudogap formation in the moderate correlated layered attractive Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21478)
*A. V. Belov,A. N. Rubtsov,B. Krippa*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文采用涨落局域场方法（fluctuating local field method）在有效相互作用为零的近似下，研究四分之一填充的层状吸引性哈伯德模型（layered attractive Hubbard model）。结果表明，团簇系统中会形成赝能隙（pseudogap），且对涨落场的积分等价于临界温度以上零模式梯形图（zero-mode ladder diagrams）的求和。对于大层状系统，通过将层间耦合处理为静态$U(1)$对称性破缺场的团簇方案，也能获得态密度中的赝能隙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究中等相互作用强度下四分之一填充的层状吸引性哈伯德模型，旨在理解强关联电子系统中赝能隙（pseudogap）的形成机制，尤其是在有限尺寸团簇和大层状系统中的表现。

Method: 采用涨落局域场方法（fluctuating local field method），在有效相互作用为零的近似下计算较大团簇的格林函数（Green's function）、自能（self-energy）和态密度（density of states）。对于大层状系统，采用将层间耦合处理为静态$U(1)$对称性破缺场的团簇方案。

Result: 在团簇系统中观察到赝能隙（pseudogap）的出现，并证明对涨落场的积分在临界温度以上等价于零模式梯形图（zero-mode ladder diagrams）的求和。在大层状系统的态密度中也获得了赝能隙。

Conclusion: 涨落局域场方法能够有效描述层状吸引性哈伯德模型中的赝能隙现象，并且层间耦合的静态对称性破缺处理为理解赝能隙提供了可行途径。

Abstract: We consider the layered attractive Hubbard model with a moderate interaction strength at quarter filling. The Green's function, self-energy, and density of states are calculated for relatively large clusters using the fluctuating local field method within the approximation of vanishing effective interaction. The emergence of a pseudogap is demonstrated for the cluster system, and it is shown that integration over the fluctuating field is equivalent to the summation of zero-mode ladder diagrams above critical temperature. For the large layered system, a pseudogap in the density of states is obtained within a cluster scheme that treats the coupling between layers as a static $U(1)$ symmetry-breaking field.

### [126] [Strong correlations and local self-energies from on-site ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21490)
*Alberto Carta,Hugo U. R. Strand,Michael Schüler,Nicola Marzari*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“局域退相系综近似（on-site dephased ensemble, DE）”的新方法，用于描述顺磁性莫特绝缘体（paramagnetic Mott insulator）的多体电子结构问题。该方法通过热系综（thermal ensemble）包含所有局域静态解来刻画局域电子结构，能够复现动力学平均场理论（DMFT）的关键特征（如自能的强频率依赖性和局域磁矩的存在），同时无需昂贵的量子蒙特卡洛求解器或大型超胞计算，为第一性原理处理强关联顺磁性莫特系统提供了高效途径，并揭示了强关联物理与无序物理之间的深层联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体电子结构问题是现代凝聚态物理的核心目标，而顺磁性莫特绝缘体对密度泛函理论（DFT）等标准方法构成了长期挑战。传统的处理方式要么依赖动力学平均场理论（DMFT）考虑多体动力学，要么采用包含静态对称性破缺图案的大型超胞描述。本文旨在提出一种更高效且能揭示强关联与无序之间联系的新近似方法。

Method: 受DMFT和超胞方法启发，本文引入了局域退相系综近似（DE近似）。该近似将局域电子结构问题描述为所有可访问的局域静态解的热系综，由此产生局域电子自能（self-energy）的强频率依赖特性，类似于DMFT或无序合金中的相干势近似（coherent-potential approximation）。

Result: DE近似成功恢复了强关联莫特系统的标志性特征，包括自能的频率依赖性以及局域磁矩在时间上的持续存在，且与DMFT结果定量一致。该方法避免了昂贵的量子蒙特卡洛求解器或大型超胞计算。

Conclusion: 该工作为在第一性原理（first-principles）框架下高效处理顺磁性莫特系统提供了新途径，并揭示了强关联物理与无序物理之间更深层次的理论联系。

Abstract: Addressing the many-body electronic-structure problem is a central goal of modern condensed-matter physics. Paramagnetic Mott insulators, in particular, have long represented a challenge for standard approaches, such as density-functional theory. Historically, these systems have been tackled either by considering many-body dynamics, as in the case of dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT), or, more recently, by invoking a polymorphous description consisting of large supercells populated with static symmetry-broken motifs whose spatial average restores the paramagnetic state. Inspired by these viewpoints, we introduce the on-site dephased ensemble (DE) approximation, in which the local electronic-structure problem is described by a thermal ensemble of all accessible local static solutions; this gives rise to a strong frequency dependence of the local electronic self-energy, as seen in DMFT or in the coherent-potential approximation of disordered alloys. We show that the DE successfully recovers defining hallmarks of strongly correlated Mott systems, both in terms of the self-energy as well as the persistence of local moments in time, in quantitative agreement with DMFT. By bypassing expensive quantum Monte Carlo solvers or large supercell calculations, this approach offers efficient routes to treating paramagnetic Mott systems in a first-principles setting, and highlights a deeper connection between the physics of strong correlations and that of disorder.

</details>


### [127] [Symmetry and Quantum Geometry in Bloch Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21581)
*Ziwei Wang,Charlie Raca,Steven H. Simon*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明了若紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）满足特定空间对称性，则最小化贝里曲率方差（variance of Berry curvature）或量子度量张量迹积分（integral of the trace of the quantum metric tensor）的实空间几何（real space geometry）必须遵从所有这些空间对称性；该结论也适用于具有磁平移对称性（magnetic translation symmetries）及其他复合对称性的系统，对Hofstadter模型的量子几何具有意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子几何量（quantum geometric quantities）在量子系统性质研究中被广泛讨论，但它们依赖于紧束缚模型的实空间几何（即“轨道嵌入”，orbital embedding），而非仅取决于模型参数。因此，寻找一种明确与几何无关的量——即所有可能实空间几何中量子几何量的最小值——成为必要。

Method: 本文采用理论分析方法，研究在给定紧束缚模型满足特定空间对称性的条件下，如何通过对称性约束推导出最小化贝里曲率方差或量子度量张量迹积分的实空间几何必须遵从这些对称性；并进一步将该论证推广到磁平移对称性和复合对称性系统。

Result: 如果紧束缚模型与某些空间对称性相容，那么最小化贝里曲率方差或量子度量张量迹积分的实空间几何必然遵守所有这些空间对称性。该结论同样适用于具有磁平移对称性及其他复合对称性的系统。

Conclusion: 本研究为量子几何量的几何无关性（geometry-independent）量提供了对称性约束条件，并指出了在Hofstadter模型等系统中该结论的应用前景。

Abstract: Quantum geometric quantities have featured heavily in the discussion of the properties of quantum systems in recent years. Among quantities most commonly discussed is the variance of Berry curvature and the integral of the trace of the quantum metric tensor. Despite their usefulness, it is known that they suffer from one significant complication: for a tight-binding model, the quantum geometric quantities depend not only on the parameters of the tight-binding model itself, but also the real space geometry of the tight-binding model, the so-called "orbital embedding". One explicitly geometry-independent quantity is therefore the minimal value of the quantum geometric quantity out of all possible real space geometries. In this work, we demonstrate that, if the tight-binding model is compatible with certain spatial symmetries, then the real space geometry that minimizes the variance of the Berry curvature or the integral of the trace of the quantum metric tensor must obey all those spatial symmetries. We further show that the statement is applicable to systems with magnetic translation symmetries and other composite symmetries, with implications for the quantum geometry of the Hofstadter model.

</details>

### [128] [Dark Matter Weather: Probing Sub-GeV Interactions with Earth-Shielding Modulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20620)
*Tetiana Kozynets,Rebecca Leane,Juri Smirnov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用地球屏蔽（Earth shielding）导致的每日调制（daily modulation）效应，探测亚GeV暗物质（dark matter, DM）与电子和原子核的双重耦合，并基于氩/氙液体惰性气体探测器建立统计框架，通过调制形状和电离谱区分不同相互作用类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚GeV暗物质的直接探测面临信号微弱、相互作用类型难以区分的挑战。已有的低阈值实验主要依赖电离信号，但难以单独区分暗物质-电子与暗物质-原子核的相互作用。

Method: 构建暗物质同时耦合电子和原子核的双相互作用框架，针对氩（argon）和氙（xenon）靶材料建模；引入基于地球穿越轨迹（Earth-crossing trajectory）和探测器位置依赖的调制形状统计分析方法，并结合电离能谱进行联合分析。

Result: 以美国SURF、意大利LNGS和澳大利亚SUPL三个地下实验站点为例验证了该方法，并将统计框架应用于DarkSide-50实验数据。结果表明地球散射调制（Earth-scattering modulation）有助于解耦电子和原子核的暗物质相互作用。

Conclusion: 地球散射调制效应可作为低阈值液体惰性气体探测器（liquid-noble detector）验证暗物质信号的有效工具，有助于区分暗物质与电子及原子核的相互作用类型。

Abstract: Daily modulation from Earth shielding provides a powerful search handle for sub-GeV dark matter (DM) in low-threshold experiments. We use this effect as a probe of interaction structure in scenarios where DM couples to both electrons and nuclei. Nuclear scattering in the Earth alters the incident DM flux, while electron scattering produces the observable ionization signal, so the total rate and modulation pattern encode different aspects of the underlying interactions. We develop this two-interaction framework for argon and xenon targets and introduce a new statistical analysis that tests the modulation shape, including the location-dependent exposure of underground detectors to different Earth-crossing trajectories, alone and in combination with the ionization spectrum. We demonstrate the method for liquid-noble detectors at underground sites SURF (USA), LNGS (Italy), and SUPL (Australia), and apply it to DarkSide-50 data as a concrete case study. Our results show that Earth-scattering modulation can help disentangle electron and nuclear DM interactions and provide a validation handle for low-threshold liquid-noble searches.

Method: 采用希格斯门户标量粒子模型，引入有限温度效应对衰变宽度进行修正，并将FCC-hh对撞机的LLP位移衰变探测灵敏度映射到标量粒子质量m_φ与再加热温度T_rh的参数平面上。

Abstract: We study a GeV-scale Higgs-portal scalar $φ$ that can dominate the early Universe and later decay into Standard Model states, ending an early matter-dominated era. Ordinary cosmic reheating is the minimal example of this scenario. The small Higgs mixing makes $φ$ a long-lived particle (LLP), linking the reheating temperature $T_\text{rh}$ to displaced-decay signatures at colliders. Including finite-temperature suppression of the decay width, we map FCC-hh LLP sensitivity onto the $[m_φ, T_\text{rh}]$ plane. We find that FCC-hh displaced searches could probe GeV-scale transition temperatures, up to the electroweak scale within the broken-phase Higgs-portal description.

### [130] [Charged Higgs Search at Future Neutrino Telescope and Higgs Factory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20963)
*YiCheng Dai,Wei Liao,Yi-Song Lu,Qi-Shu Yan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在两种具有普适汤川耦合（universal Yukawa couplings）的简化基准模型下，未来轻子对撞机和微中子望远镜对带电希格斯玻色子（charged Higgs boson）的发现潜力。研究发现，未来轻子对撞机在大部分参数空间中具有更优的灵敏度，而大体积微中子望远镜在带电希格斯玻色子的高质量区域可提供竞争性且互补的探测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在两种具有普适汤川耦合的简化基准模型下，分别利用微中子望远镜中的μ子径迹（muon-track）和级联（cascade）事件通过共振微中子散射过程搜索带电希格斯玻色子，并比较不同天体物理微中子通量模型下的灵敏度；同时，在未来轻子对撞机上采用优化的重建策略（reconstruction strategies）研究带电希格斯玻色子在不同运动学区域（kinematic regimes）的信号。

Result: 未来轻子对撞机在大部分参数空间中提供更好的灵敏度；微中子望远镜在带电希格斯玻色子的高质量区域（heavy-mass region），尤其是具有非常大探测器体积时，能够提供竞争性且互补的灵敏度。

Conclusion: 未来轻子对撞机与微中子望远镜在带电希格斯玻色子的探测上各具优势，两者在参数空间的不同区域可实现互补，其中大体积微中子望远镜在高质量区域的表现尤为突出。

Abstract: We investigate the discovery potential of the charged Higgs boson at future lepton colliders and neutrino telescopes within two simplified benchmark scenarios with universal Yukawa couplings. We demonstrate that both the muon-track and cascade events at neutrino telescopes can be exploited to search for or constrain the charged Higgs boson through resonant neutrino scattering process, and we compare the sensitivities obtained under different astrophysical neutrino flux models. We study the effect of the detector volume of neutrino telescopes on the discovery potential of the charged Higgs boson. We study the signal of charged Higgs boson at future lepton colliders over different kinematic regimes using optimized reconstruction strategies. We compare the discovery potential of the two experimental approaches over the relevant parameter space and find that future lepton colliders generally provide better sensitivity in most of the parameter space, while neutrino telescopes with very large detector volume can offer competitive and complementary sensitivity in the heavy-mass region of the charged Higgs boson.

### [131] [Advanced Statistical Analysis of Linear and Nonlinear Regge Trajectories for Light Non-strange Mesons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21035)
*S. S. Afonin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于严格统计方法分析轻非奇异介子的Regge轨迹，发现非线性修正（含类Dirac-Coulomb项）能有效描述S波共振区的谱形畸变，并支持库仑型简并关系 m²(n,l) ∝ n+l 的统计稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对介子Regge轨迹（Regge trajectory）的分析多采用线性近似，但实验数据中S波共振区存在系统性偏离，且多数研究未充分考虑实验不确定性与理论模型选择偏差。

Method: 基于非线性χ²最小化（nonlinear χ² minimization）框架，通过自洽条件 χ²/dof = 1 确定模型内禀不确定度；采用Akaike信息准则（Akaike information criterion）与贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian information criterion）进行模型选择，并辅以补充统计检验。

Result: 线性模型的偏离主要集中于S波共振区；仅有含非线性修正的Model 3能成功拟合该畸变，并揭示出近似的库仑型简并关系 m²(n,l) ∝ n+l；该非线性修正与库仑问题中领头阶相对论校正（leading-order relativistic correction）一致。

Conclusion: 轻非奇异介子Regge谱的统计证据支持非线性类库仑修正的存在，且该修正与相对论量子力学中的预期形式相符，为介子谱的非线性特征提供了定量约束。

Abstract: A rigorous statistical analysis of Regge-type trajectories for light non-strange meson mass spectra is carried out, which explicitly accounts for experimental uncertainties. We test three scenarios: a linear model with distinct radial ($n$) and orbital ($l$) slopes (Model 1), a linear model with a universal slope (Model 2), and a nonlinear model featuring a universal slope and a Dirac-Coulomb-type term $\propto (l+1)^{-1}$ (Model 3). Optimization is performed using a nonlinear $χ^2$ minimization framework, where the intrinsic theoretical model uncertainty is determined self-consistently by enforcing $χ^2/\text{dof} = 1$. To ensure robust model selection, we employ the Akaike and Bayesian information criteria alongside complementary statistical tests. Our analysis demonstrates that moderate deviations from linearity in the Regge spectrum are predominantly localized within the $S$-wave resonance sector. These distortions are successfully accommodated by the nonlinear correction in Model 3, from which an approximate Coulomb-type degeneracy, $m^2(n,l) \propto n+l$, emerges as a statistically robust feature. Furthermore, we show that the $l$-dependent correction to the principal quantum number in light non-strange mesons is consistent with the leading-order relativistic correction to the Coulomb problem.

</details>


### [132] [MeV Electrophilic Axion-like Particles from Sun](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21168)
*Shao-Feng Ge,Sk Jeesun,Tao Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用太阳核聚变产生的5.5MeV单色光子，通过康普顿类散射产生MeV尺度的亲电轴子粒子（ALPs），并利用现有暗物质直接探测实验（LZ、PandaX-4T、Borexino）的数据来探测此前未被探索的参数空间，在质量窗口0.4 MeV ≲ m_a ≲ 1 MeV区域内获得了新的灵敏度上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索MeV尺度亲电轴子粒子（axion-like particles, ALPs）的产生机制与探测方法，利用太阳核聚变产生的5.5MeV单色光子通过康普顿类散射（Compton-like scattering）与环境电子相互作用产生可观通量的MeV ALPs，从而为暗物质（dark matter, DM）直接探测实验开辟此前未被探索的参数区域。

Method: 利用太阳核聚变过程中产生的5.5MeV单色光子在太阳物质中与环境电子发生类康普顿散射，产生MeV尺度的亲电ALPs；到达地球后，这些ALPs通过相同的电子耦合被暗物质直接探测实验所探测。

Result: 现有LZ、PandaX-4T和Borexino实验数据分别可达到g_ae ≲ 3.7×10^(-6)、g_ae ≲ 3.7×10^(-6)和g_ae ≲ 1.7×10^(-6)的灵敏度（m_a ≲ 1MeV）；PandaX-xT在200吨·年曝光量下，对m_a < 1MeV大部分质量窗口可达g_ae ≲ 1.6×10^(-6)，当m_a接近1MeV时甚至可达g_ae ≲ 1.5×10^(-7)。

Conclusion: 尽管来自不同实验室实验和天体物理观测的约束十分严格，但基于LZ、PandaX-4T和Borexino获得的限制能够在质量窗口0.4 MeV ≲ m_a ≲ 1 MeV内探测到新的参数区域，展示了利用太阳ALPs进行暗物质直接探测的潜力。

Abstract: This work explores the production of an MeV-scale electrophilic axion-like particles (ALPs) by utilizing the monochromatic 5.5MeV photon resulting from the nuclear fusion processes in the Sun. These 5.5MeV photons can undergo the Compton-like scattering with the ambient electrons in the solar matter to produce a substantial flux of MeV ALPs. Upon reaching the Earth, such ALPs can be detected via the same electron coupling, offering a new opportunity for the dark matter (DM) direct detection experiments to probe the previously unexplored parameter regions. We show that the existing data of LZ, PandaX-4T, and Borexino can attain the sensitivities $g_{ae} \lesssim 3.7 \times 10^{-6}$, $g_{ae} \lesssim 3.7 \times 10^{-6}$ and $g_{ae} \lesssim 1.7 \times 10^{-6}$, respectively, for $m_a \lesssim 1$MeV. An optimistic 200 tonne$\times$year exposure by PandaX-xT can reach $g_{ae}\lesssim 1.6 \times 10^{-6}$ for most of the mass window $m_a < 1$MeV and even $g_{ae} \lesssim 1.5 \times 10^{-7}$ with $m_a$ approaching 1MeV. Despite the stringent constraints from different laboratory experiments and astrophysical observations, our obtained limits from LZ, PandaX-4T, and Borexino can probe new parameter regions, specifically in the mass window $0.4\,{\rm MeV} \lesssim m_a \lesssim 1$MeV.

### [133] [Transverse-momentum resummation effects on angular coefficients in Z and W boson hadroproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21395)
*Stefano Camarda,Giancarlo Ferrera,Lorenzo Rossi,Gabriele Francesco Sala*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 论文通过结合微扰QCD的次次领头对数（NNLL）重求和与次领头阶（NLO）固定阶计算，系统分析了强子对撞机上Z和W玻色子产生的角系数，发现重求和效应在中等横动量区域（q_T~20-50 GeV）可适度改善数据描述，在其他情形下则不影响实验与固定阶QCD预言之间的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强子对撞机上电弱规范玻色子（Z/W）的角系数（angular coefficients）是检验量子色动力学（QCD）理论预言的重要观测量，但固定阶QCD计算在小横动量区域存在发散问题，需要引入横动量重求和（transverse-momentum resummation）来获得可靠的预言。本文旨在系统评估重求和效应对角系数的影响，并与多个实验合作组的数据进行对比。

Method: 将次次领头对数（NNLL）精度的对数增强QCD修正重求和与次领头阶（NLO）固定阶计算自洽地结合，从而在全横动量（q_T）范围内获得角系数的理论预言，并与ATLAS、LHCb、CMS（LHC）及CDF（Tevatron）的实验数据进行比较。

Result: 重求和效应的加入使得在中等横动量区间（q_T ~ 20-50 GeV）内多个角系数的数据描述得到适度且系统性的改善；在其余情形下，重求和的引入并不会降低固定阶QCD预言与实验测量之间的一致性。

Conclusion: 横动量重求和是改进Z/W玻色子角系数理论预言的有效工具，尤其在中间q_T区域可带来可观改善，且不会破坏其他区域的预言精度。

Abstract: We present a comprehensive analysis of the angular coefficients of $Z$ and $W$ boson production at hadron colliders in different kinematical ranges, using data from the ATLAS, LHCb, and CMS Collaborations at the LHC, as well as CDF data at the Tevatron. We provide theoretical predictions obtained by consistently combining the resummation of logarithmically enhanced QCD corrections at small transverse momenta $q_T$ up to next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic accuracy (NNLL) with fixed-order calculations at next-to-leading order (NLO), valid at large $q_T$. We quantify the impact of transverse-momentum resummation on the angular coefficients. We find that the inclusion of resummation effects leads to a moderate and systematic improvement in the description of the data in the intermediate $q_T$ region, $q_T \sim 20-50$~GeV, for several angular coefficients, while in the remaining cases it does not degrade the agreement of fixed-order QCD predictions with experimental measurements.

### [134] [Numerical Backreaction and Finite-Time Energy Transfer in Post-Recombination Magnetogenesis from Ultralight Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20793)
*Aviv David,Robert Brandenberger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟研究了后重组时期超轻赝标量暗物质场与电磁场耦合产生规范场的机制，确认了此前解析方法给出的光谱结果，并进一步揭示了不同共振通道下能量转移效率的显著差异。研究发现，在速失稳（tachyonic instability）通道打开的参数区间，反作用（back-reaction）会在远小于哈勃时间（Hubble time）的时标内将约一阶的暗物质能量密度转移给光子；而在仅打开窄共振（narrow resonance）通道的参数区间，这一能量转移可能需要极长时间，直至今天仍可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前解析工作表明，均匀振荡的超轻赝标量暗物质背景可通过速失稳和窄共振两种通道激发规范场模式，但其动力学演化，特别是反作用对共振过程的终止机制以及能量转移效率，尚缺乏数值验证与定量刻画。本文旨在通过数值方法跟踪背景场与规范场的耦合演化，以弥补这一空白。

Method: 在膨胀宇宙背景下，对均匀振荡的赝标量暗物质场与两种螺旋度（helicity）的规范场模式的耦合演化进行数值模拟，并与此前近似解析方法所得结果进行对比验证。

Result: 数值结果确认了此前解析方法给出的规范粒子产生光谱。进一步发现：当速失稳不稳定带打开时，反作用会在远小于哈勃时间的时标内终止共振，并将约一阶（order one）的初始暗物质能量密度转移给光子；当仅窄共振带打开时，能量转移分数最终也能达到一阶，但所需时标随有效耦合常数减小而增加，因此在某些参数下该转移直至当前宇宙时刻仍可忽略。

Conclusion: 后重组时期超轻赝标量暗物质与电磁场的耦合可有效产生规范场，但能量转移效率强烈依赖于共振通道类型：速失稳通道可在短时间内高效转移暗物质能量至光子，而窄共振通道在弱耦合下效率极低。该差异对理解暗物质候选者的观测约束及磁生成（magnetogenesis）机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: We study gauge-field production in a post-recombination magnetogenesis scenario driven by an ultralight pseudoscalar dark matter field $φ$ coupled to electromagnetism. Previous analytical work has shown that a homogeneous oscillating $φ$ background can excite gauge field modes through tachyonic and narrow-band resonance channels. Here we follow the coupled evolution of the homogeneous $φ$ mode and gauge field modes of both helicities in an expanding background. Our numerical work confirms the results for the spectra of produced gauge particles obtained in the previous approximate analytical treatments. In addition, our study allows us to determine when back-reaction shuts off the resonance. We find that for parameter values for which the tachyonic instability band is open, back-reaction does not shut off the resonance until a fraction ${\cal{F}}$ of order one of the initial dark matter energy density has been transferred to photons, and this happens on a time scale which is short compared to the Hubble time. In the parameter range in which only the narrow resonance band is open, ${\cal{F}}$ eventually reaches order one, but the time when this happens increases as the effective coupling constant decreases, and therefore ${\cal{F}}$ may remain negligible until the present time.

*Rodrigo Carmo Terin*

Conclusion: 神经网络方法能够以高精度和稳定性求解耦合DSEs，其误差小于顶点模型不确定性，表明该方法可作为一种可靠的计算工具。同时，该方法保留了对关键物理特征（如紫外跑动和施温格函数符号变化）的预测能力。

Abstract: The coupled ghost and gluon Dyson--Schwinger equations (DSEs) of four-dimensional Landau-gauge Yang--Mills (YM) theory are solved with a neural representation trained only from renormalized equation residuals. The neural and fixed-point solutions agree at the percent level and remain stable under changes of initialization, network size, integration grid, and infrared boundary condition. Variations of the three-gluon vertex model produce substantially larger effects than the neural error. The MiniMOM ultraviolet running and the sign change of the gluon Schwinger function are also reproduced within the limitations of the truncation.

Method: 采用微扰理论（perturbation theory）进行分析，将晶格周期与扭结宽度之比作为展开参数（expansion parameter）。研究对象包括非线性Klein-Gordon链（$φ^4$和sine-Gordon）以及离散串联约瑟夫森传输线（discrete series-connected Josephson transmission line）。

Abstract: We use perturbation theory to study kinks in nonlinear Klein--Gordon ($φ^4$ and sine-Gordon) chains and in a discrete series-connected Josephson transmission line. The next-to-leading-order approximation modifies the kink profiles obtained previously in the leading-order approximation.

### [138] [Geometric Superconducting Diode Effect in an NbN Nanoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20794)
*Tianyu Li,Peiyuan Huang,Jiong Li,Jiyao Shang,Nuo-Zhou Yang,Wuyue Xu,Wen-Cheng Yue,Yang-Yang Lyu,Chong Li,Yihuang Xiong,Xuecou Tu,Tao Tao,Xiaoqing Jia,Qing-Hu Chen,Huabing Wang,Peiheng Wu,Yong-Lei Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在单材料NbN纳米环中实现了几何诱导的超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect），仅通过非对称几何结构打破反演对称性（inversion-symmetry breaking），无需约瑟夫森结或多层异质结等复杂元件，并系统表征了其临界电流非互易性（critical-current nonreciprocity）与温度、磁场的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超导二极管平台通常依赖约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）、多层异质结构、铁磁元件或栅极定义结构，结构复杂且制备成本高；本文旨在探索一种结构更简单、仅依赖几何不对称性实现超导二极管效应的最小化平台。

Method: 作者在单材料NbN薄膜上制备了具有非对称几何形状的纳米环（nanoring），通过结构设计破坏反演对称性；随后在不同温度与外加磁场条件下测量了正反偏置方向的临界电流，分析非互易性与二极管理效率（diode efficiency）的变化规律。

Result: 器件展现出显著且极性可切换的临界电流非互易性。在低磁场条件下，磁场在不显著降低整体超导载流能力的前提下，使临界电流在正反偏置方向间发生不对称再分布。最大非互易性和最大二极管理效率表现出不同的温度依赖性：最大二极管理效率随能隙（energy gap）演化，而最大非互易性更紧密关联于超流密度（superfluid density）。

Conclusion: 非对称超导纳米环为研究非互易超导输运（nonreciprocal superconducting transport）提供了一个最小化几何平台，并为未来超导电子学器件提供了一种简单的设计原则。

Abstract: Superconducting diodes, which exhibit nonreciprocal critical currents, are promising building blocks for low-power cryogenic electronics and superconducting circuits. Existing superconducting diode platforms commonly rely on Josephson junctions, multilayer heterostructures, ferromagnetic elements, gate-difined structures. Here, we demonstrate a geometrically induced superconducting diode effect realized in a structurally minimal, single-materials NbN nanoring, where inversion-symmetry breaking is introduced solely by the asymmetric geometry. The device exhibits pronounced and polarity-switchable critical-current nonreciprocity. Systematic magnetic-field and temperature-dependent measurements reveal that, at low fields, the applied magnetic field redistributes the critical current asymmetrically between opposite bias directions without significantly reducing the overall superconducting current-carrying capability. Moreover, the maximal nonreciprocity and diode efficiency exhibit distinct temperature dependence: the maximal diode efficiency follows the evolution of the energy gap, whereas the maximal nonreciprocity is more closely associated with the superfluid density. These results establish asymmetric superconducting nanorings as a minimal geometric platform for studying nonreciprocal superconducting transport and provide a simple design principle for future superconducting electronics.

</details>


### [139] [Evidence for fully-gapped superconductivity in BCS superconductor NiBi3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20974)
*Atul Gangwar,Kunal Yadav,S. Patnaik,Sandip Chatterjee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过对NiBi3单晶的电阻率、磁化强度和伦敦穿透深度测量，表征其物理特性、正常态和超导性质。结果表明NiBi3是典型的第二类（type-II）超导体，具有s波BCS行为，超导转变温度Tc=4.0 K，无节点超导能隙，为完全有能隙（fully gapped）超导体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究NiBi3单晶的物理特性、正常态和超导性质，明确其超导机制和分类归属。

Method: 对NiBi3单晶进行电阻率（electrical resistivity）、磁化强度（magnetization）和伦敦穿透深度（London penetration depth）测量；通过两种磁场取向（H平行于b和H垂直于b）分析上临界场（upper critical field, Hc2）；基于超流密度（superfluid density）的温度依赖关系检验能隙结构。

Result: 超导转变温度Tc=4.0 K，电阻转变宽度ΔTc=0.20 K，剩余电阻比RRR=18，样品质量高；Hc2显著低于Pauli极限，表明超导态中轨道对破坏（orbital pair breaking）占主导；相干长度ξ(0)=26.78 nm，电子-声子耦合常数λ(e-p)=0.81，穿透深度λ0=181.8 nm，表明为第二类超导；λ(T)符合s波BCS模型，无线性或二次温度依赖；超流密度证实完全有能隙超导，超导能隙=4.07。

Conclusion: NiBi3是典型的第二类、BCS类、中等强度耦合、完全有能隙的超导体，且处于脏极限（dirty limit）。

Abstract: We investigate the physical characteristics, normal state and superconducting properties of NiBi3 single crystals. Measurements of electrical resistivity, magnetization, and London penetration depth demonstrate a superconducting transition temperature, Tc=4.0 K, with a sharp transition in resistivity (Tc = 0.20 K) and RRR = 18, reflecting the high quality of NiBi3 single crystals. With both orientations H perpendicular b and H parallel b of NiBi3 single crystals, we estimated the upper critical field, Hc2, from the magnetization data. In both orientations, Hc2 is significantly smaller than the Pauli limit, suggesting the orbital pair breaking in superconducting state. The coherence length, xi(0) = 26.78 nm, electron-phonon coupling constant, lambda(e-p) = 0.81, and penetration depth, lambda0 = 181.8 nm, suggest type-II superconductivity in NiBi3. In the superconducting state, lambda(T) is best described by an s-wave BCS model and does not have linear or quadratic dependency with T, which is in line with the expectation for a node-less superconducting order parameter. The temperature evolution of the superfluid density, obtained from lambda(T), reveals a fully gapped superconductivity in NiBi3, with a superconducting gap = 4.07. All the results from the present study indicate that NiBi3 is a typical type-II, BCS-like, moderately strong coupled, and fully gapped superconductor in the dirty limit.

</details>


### [140] [Magnetically memorable inductance in superconducting multilayer resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21147)
*R. Tyumenev,D. S. Kalashnikov,B. V. Fradkin,A. A. Neilo,A. G. Shishkin,N. V. Klenov,I. I. Soloviev,A. A. Golubov,M. Yu. Kupriyanov,I. A. Golovchanskiy,V. S. Stolyarov,A. S. Sidorenko,S. V. Bakurskiy*

TL;DR: 本文报道了基于Nb/Co/Nb/Co/Nb/Al自旋触发多层膜（spin-trigger multilayers）的开口环谐振器（split-ring resonators）的制备与微波表征，展示了其在零磁场下具有非易失性自旋阀效应（non-volatile spin-valve effect），谐振频率平移最高达4 MHz，且通过邻近化铝覆盖层（proximitized aluminum overlayer）将动能电感对比度（kinetic inductance contrast）提升约三倍，实验结果与基于Usadel方程的微观模型定量吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 具有可调动能电感（tunable kinetic inductance）的超导体-铁磁体混合结构（superconductor-ferromagnet hybrid structures）是神经形态计算（neuromorphic computing）和量子计算电路（quantum computing circuits）的理想元件，因此需要探索能实现非易失性可调电感的新型材料体系。

Method: 制备基于Nb/Co/Nb/Co/Nb/Al自旋触发多层膜的开口环谐振器，通过微波表征（microwave characterization）测量其谐振特性，在不同钴层相对磁化取向（relative magnetization orientation）下记录谐振频率变化，并引入邻近化铝覆盖层以增强电感对比度。

Result: 零磁场下，反转钴层的相对磁化方向可产生最高4 MHz的可重复谐振频率平移，对应结构动能电感的改变；铝覆盖层将平行与反平行磁态之间的电感对比度增强约三倍；实验结果与基于Usadel方程的微观模型定量一致。

Conclusion: 本文在零场下演示了谐振频率的磁性记忆效应（magnetic memory），证明自旋触发多层膜可作为可行的场可编程电感元件（field-programmable inductive elements），应用于超导数字电路（superconducting digital circuits）和神经形态电路（neuromorphic circuits）。

Abstract: Superconductor-ferromagnet hybrid structures with tunable kinetic inductance are promising elements for neuromorphic and quantum computing circuits. We report the fabrication and microwave characterization of split-ring resonators based on Nb/Co/Nb/Co/Nb/Al spin-trigger multilayers and demonstrate a non-volatile spin-valve effect on their resonant properties. Reversal of the relative magnetization orientation of the cobalt layers produces a reproducible shift of the resonant frequency up to 4 MHz at zero applied magnetic field, corresponding to a change in the kinetic inductance of the structure. The incorporation of a proximitized aluminum overlayer is shown to enhance the inductance contrast between the parallel and antiparallel magnetic states by a factor of approximately three relative to structures without this layer. The experimental results are in quantitative agreement with a microscopic model based on the Usadel equations. The demonstrated magnetic memory of the resonant frequency at zero field establishes spin-trigger multilayers as viable field-programmable inductive elements for superconducting digital and neuromorphic circuits.

### [141] [Puzzling superconductivity in strontium ruthenate: then and now](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21194)
*James F. Annett,Karol I. Wysokiński*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了Sr₂RuO₄超导体的研究进展，指出其序参量对称性仍不明确；基于最新实验表明其更可能是自旋单态（spin singlet）超导体，作者计算了手性d波E_g配对态的Kerr效应，发现霍尔电导非零，与先前手性p波E_u序参量的结果定性相似，并与Berry曲率及f求和规则相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sr₂RuO₄虽然经过三十多年的深入研究，其超导序参量（order parameter）的精确对称性仍未确定；早期认为它是自旋三重态奇宇称手性p波超导体，但近期实验结果对这一理解提出了挑战，需要重新评估其配对对称性。

Method: 作者对关键实验进展（尤其是质疑原有认识的新实验）进行了简要综述；基于Sr₂RuO₄很可能为自旋单态超导体的最新判断，选择了一个候选d波配对态（E_g），并计算了该配对态下的Kerr效应（Kerr effect）与霍尔电导（Hall conductance）。

Result: 对于手性d波E_g配对态，计算得到的霍尔电导非零，且与先前在手性p波E_u序参量假设下得到的霍尔电导结果定性相似；进一步将霍尔电导与两个求和规则（sum rules）——Bogoliubov准粒子态的Berry曲率（Berry curvature）相关的求和规则以及指示存在轨道间配对（inter-orbital pairing）的f求和规则——联系起来进行了表征。

Conclusion: 综述表明Sr₂RuO₄最可能为自旋单态超导体，而非原有的手性p波图像；针对候选d波E_g态的计算验证了该配对态下可以产生非零霍尔电导，其行为与早期手性p波情形定性一致，为理解该超导体的配对机制提供了新的理论线索。

Abstract: Strontium ruthenate is a very interesting low temperature superconductor with relatively simple normal state and very puzzling superconducting state properties. Despite over thirty years of intensive research, even the precise symmetry of the order parameter is not known. In this paper we briefly review some of the key developments, focussing on some of the newer experiments, especially those which challenged the previous understanding that it is a spin triplet odd parity chiral p-wave superconductor. Since Sr$_2$RuO$_4$ now appears most probably a spin singlet superconductor we have calculated the Kerr effect for one candidate $d$-wave pairing state. We find that for the chiral $d$-wave $E_g$ pairing state the calculated Hall conductance is non-zero and qualitatively similar to that found earlier under the assumption of a chiral p-wave $E_u$ order parameter. We characterize the Hall conductance in relation to two sum rules, one related to Berry curvatures in the Bogoliubov quasiparticle states, and the other $f$-sum rule indicating the presence of inter-orbital pairing.

### [142] [Supercurrent effect in a charge density wave intertwined superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21507)

Method: 采用扫描隧道显微谱学成像（scanning tunneling spectroscopic imaging）技术，在施加平面内磁场条件下观测超导NbSe₂中电荷密度波调制的变化，并结合模型计算对选择性多普勒频移引起的E-k色散重构进行分析。

Abstract: The energy-momentum (E-k) dispersion of quasiparticles constitutes a fundamental concept in condensed matter systems. The ability to modify the E-k dispersion, exemplified by supercurrent-induced Doppler shifts of Bogoliubov quasiparticle spectra in superconductors, enables manipulation of various emergent quantum properties. However, investigations into the supercurrent effect on superconductors intertwined with charge orders remain scarce. Here, we report that the Meissner current, generated by the diamagnetic response to an applied in-plane magnetic field, can tailor Bogoliubov quasiparticle excitations at the precursor charge density wave (CDW) vectors. Our scanning tunneling spectroscopic imaging reveals a field-driven symmetry breaking of CDW modulations, specifically a C3v-to-Cs transition, in superconducting NbSe2. Model calculations suggest that the observed anisotropy originates from a selective Doppler-shift-induced E-k dispersion reconstruction. Furthermore, altering the field direction enables on-demand tuning of anisotropic CDW modulations and visualization of their momentum-space distribution. These results highlight a novel mechanism for controlling emergent electronic phases through momentum-space engineering.

### [143] [Sequential Topological Superconductivity in a Square Lattice with Chiral Charge Density Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21525)
*Zhong-Xian Jin,Junkang Huang,Yu-Xuan Li,Tao Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文理论研究了同时包含实部键调制（电荷键序）和虚部跳变调制（手性通量相）的复合电荷密度波与方格超导体共存系统，发现实虚两种键调制的协同作用可诱导出陈数为C=±2的两类拓扑非平庸超导相，其低温热霍尔电导率呈现与陈数成正比的量子化平台，为实验检测提供了清晰指纹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电荷序与超导性之间的相互作用为涌现量子相提供了丰富的研究空间，本文旨在探索具有复合电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）的方格超导体中能否产生拓扑非平庸的超导相。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，在方格点阵上构建同时存在实部键调制（charge bond order, CBO）和虚部跳变调制（chiral flux phase, CFP）的复合CDW与超导共存模型，通过计算陈数（Chern number）和低温热霍尔电导率（thermal Hall conductivity κxy）来表征体系的拓扑性质。

Result: 单独的CFP无法在方格点阵中诱导拓扑性质，但CFP与CBO共存可使体系进入两个拓扑非平庸的超导相，其陈数分别为C=+2和C=-2；低温热霍尔电导率κxy呈现与陈数成正比的量子化平台。

Conclusion: 方格点阵通过实部和虚部键调制的协同作用，为工程化实现拓扑超导（topological superconductivity）提供了一个纯净的平台。

Abstract: The interplay between charge order and superconductivity offers a fertile ground for emergent quantum phases. Here we theoretically investigate a square-lattice superconductor coexisting with a composite charge density wave (CDW) consisting of a real bond modulation (charge bond order, CBO) and an imaginary hopping modulation (chiral flux phase, CFP) that breaks time-reversal symmetry. We uncover that, while CFP alone does not induce topology in square lattices, its coexistence with CBO drives the system into two topologically nontrivial superconducting phases with Chern numbers $C=+2$ and $C=-2$. The low-temperature thermal Hall conductivity $κ_{xy}$ exhibits quantized plateaus proportional to the Chern number, providing a clear experimental fingerprint. Our results establish the square lattice as a pristine platform for engineering topological superconductivity through the synergy of real and imaginary bond modulations.

### [144] [A Mixed Discrete Cosserat Rod Formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21164)
*Tianxiang Dai,Marco Herrmann,Jonas Breuling,Remco I. Leine,Simon R. Eugster*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出一种离散Cosserat杆公式，将细长弹性杆表示为刚体链，通过节点间的弹性力和力矩耦合；该公式严格源于混合Petrov–Galerkin有限元格式，兼具无锁死性和两节点耦合结构，通过三个数值算例验证了其精度与收敛性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有应变参数化降阶模型在软体机器人应用中存在密集耦合（dense coupling）问题，计算效率与结构清晰度不足；同时希望弥合计算机图形学中离散杆模型与严格力学有限元方法之间的理论鸿沟。

Method: 将弹性杆离散为刚体节点链，节点间由弹性力和力矩耦合；基于混合Petrov–Galerkin (mixed Petrov–Galerkin) Cosserat杆有限元公式，线性运动学插值阶下，内虚功用中点积分法（midpoint rule）计算，外力和惯性项用梯形法则（trapezoidal rule）积分，导出离散膨胀、剪切、扭转和曲率应变度量（strain measures）以及柔度形式（compliance form）的本构关系。

Result: 所提公式继承了混合有限元方法的鲁棒性和无锁死性（locking-free），同时呈现与计算机图形学离散杆模型一致的两节点耦合结构，克服了软体机器人中常用应变参数化降阶模型的密集耦合问题。三个数值算例（分段变截面、肌腱驱动在不同空间离散下的响应、纵向-扭转耦合动力学）验证了方法的精度、鲁棒性和收敛行为。

Conclusion: 该离散Cosserat杆公式在严格有限元框架下实现了简洁的两节点耦合结构，为细长弹性杆的力学模拟提供了兼具理论严谨性与计算高效性的新方案，尤其适用于软体机器人等需要复杂变形模拟的应用场景。

Abstract: In this communication we propose a discrete Cosserat rod formulation in which a slender elastic rod is represented as a chain of rigid bodies (nodes) coupled by compliant elastic forces and moments acting between adjacent node pairs. Discrete dilatation, shear, torsion and curvature strain measures are evaluated from the relative kinematics of each node pair, while the constitutive behavior is expressed in compliance form through independent stress degrees of freedom. We show that the resulting model arises rigorously from a mixed Petrov--Galerkin Cosserat rod finite element formulation (FEM) at linear kinematic interpolation order when the internal virtual work is integrated by the midpoint rule and the external and inertial contributions by the trapezoidal rule. The proposed formulation inherits the robustness and the absence of locking from the underlying mixed FEM while simultaneously exposing a two-node coupling structure that mirrors discrete rod models from the computer graphics community. This is in sharp contrast to the dense coupling of strain-parameterized reduced-order models often used in soft robotic applications. Three numerical examples involving piecewise-varying cross sections, tendon-driven actuation under different spatial discretizations, and coupled longitudinal-torsional dynamics confirm the accuracy, robustness, and convergence behavior of the presented approach.

Abstract: Resolving steep damage gradients across diffuse cracks in the phase-field modeling of fracture favors the use of high-order finite elements, for which matrix-free methods can provide superior performance and scalability. Here, we implement the Peric & Dettmer constitutive framework for visco-elastoplastic materials in an open source solid mechanics library supporting matrix-free operators for high-order finite elements with p-multigrid preconditioning on GPUs. We introduce a rheological fracture element assembled in series so that inelastic and fracture properties can appear to affect each other only at homogenization length scales. Numerical simulations of tensile and compressive tests are conducted for synthetic particle-matrix microstructures on an El Capitan high performance computing prototype. ### [146] [The silent dark sector: a field-theory approach to unified dark fluids with vanishing speed of sound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.19494)
*Javier de Cruz Pérez,Darío Jaramillo-Garrido,Antonio L. Maroto,Prado Martín-Moruno*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类全新的场论模型，将暗区（dark sector）统一描述为一种声速为零的单一完美流体。该框架基于横向微分同胚（transverse diffeomorphisms）不变的标量场，自然实现了类似拟射模型（mimetic models）的约束，并以标准ΛCDM模型为特例。通过一个具体例子，该模型可再现DESI最佳拟合的CPL暗能量演化，且自由参数数量相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有暗物质与暗能量的描述通常是分离的，缺乏统一的理论框架；同时，需要避免幽灵行为（phantom behavior）等理论病态。本文旨在构建一种能够将暗区作为一个整体进行统一描述、同时规避上述问题的新模型。

Method: 引入一类新的场论模型，利用一个在横向微分同胚变换下保持不变的标量场（scalar field）来构建暗区。该框架自然纳入了拟射模型中的约束条件，使得暗区表现为一种声速为零的单一完美流体（perfect fluid），并可解释为冷暗物质与真空能量（vacuum energy）的相互作用系统。

Result: 该模型在特定简单示例下，能够在不增加自由参数数量的前提下，再现DESI（暗能量光谱巡天，Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument）最佳拟合的CPL（Chevallier-Polarski-Linder）参数化暗能量演化行为。

Conclusion: 本文提出的场论模型为暗区的统一描述提供了新的理论途径，兼具理论自洽性（无幽灵行为、包含ΛCDM为特例）与观测拟合能力，为暗能量和暗物质的相互作用研究提供了新的框架。

Abstract: We introduce a novel class of field-theory models that provide a unified description of the dark sector as a single perfect fluid with vanishing sound speed. These models also admit the interpretation of cold dark matter interacting with vacuum energy while avoiding any phantom behavior and including standard $Λ$CDM as a particular case. Built upon a single scalar field invariant under transverse diffeomorphisms, the framework naturally implements the constraints imposed in the so called mimetic models. We analyze a particular simple example exhibiting an effectively evolving dark energy and find that it can reproduce the DESI best-fit CPL evolution with the same number of free parameters.

</details>


### [147] [Isotropic deceleration and near-zero baseline acceleration in Pantheon+ supernovae: new arguments in the dark energy debate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20570)
*Saibal Ray,Maxim Khlopov,Aritra Sanyal,Rikpratik Sengupta,Maxim Krasnov*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用Pantheon+星表中的1564颗Ia型超新星（SNe Ia），通过红移bin、天空半球、寄主星系质量和超新星颜色四种独立分解方式分析减速参数q₀。未经过任何前身年龄校正时，全样本得到的qₘ = -0.062，远低于ΛCDM模型预期的-0.55，挑战了标准宇宙学图像。天空半球检验显示减速在CMB偶极子（dipole）半球（qₘ = +1.45）和反偶极子（anti-dipole）半球（+1.55）同样强，直接反驳了SRS26各向异性论证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Pantheon+星表中1564颗Ia型超新星数据，对减速参数q₀进行四种独立分解：按红移bin（redshift bin）、天空半球（sky hemisphere）、寄主星系质量（host galaxy mass）和超新星颜色（supernova colour）分组测量。未对超新星前身年龄（progenitor age）做任何校正。

Result: 全样本未校正前得到qₘ = -0.062，显著低于ΛCDM模型预期的-0.55。天空半球检验中，CMB偶极子（dipole）半球qₘ = +1.45，反偶极子（anti-dipole）半球qₘ = +1.55，两者数值接近，未显示各向异性差异。

Conclusion: 标准宇宙学图像在未做前身年龄校正时受到挑战；天空半球检验结果直接反驳了SRS26各向异性论证，表明当前对q₀的解释可能存在问题。

Abstract: We perform four independent decompositions of the deceleration parameter $q_0$ using 1564 Type Ia supernovae (SNe Ia) from the Pantheon+ catalogue: by redshift bin, sky hemisphere, host galaxy mass, and supernova colour. Without any progenitor age correction, the full sample yields $q_m$ = - 0.062 -- far below the $Λ$CDM expectation of - 0.55 -- challenging the standard picture before any correction. Crucially, the sky hemisphere test shows the deceleration is equally strong in the CMB dipole ($q_m$ = + 1.45) and anti-dipole hemispheres (+ 1.55), directly contradicting the SRS26 anisotropy argument. Our results challenge both current interpretations.

### [148] [Hubble tension: the shape wall](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21244)
*Miguel A. Sabogal,Luis A. Escamilla,Davide Pedrotti,Edvig Selimaj,Sunny Vagnozzi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文指出，晚期宇宙（late-time）解决哈勃常数（Hubble constant, H₀）紧张问题（Hubble tension）的方案不仅面临已知的“归一化壁垒”（normalization wall），更面临由膨胀历史形状（expansion history shape）所施加的“形状壁垒”（shape wall）。通过对径距离积分（dimensionless distance integral, I）与H₀之间关系的量化分析，利用高斯过程（Gaussian Processes）对无锚定Ia型超新星（SNeIa）和重子声学振荡（BAO）数据进行非参数重建，发现H₀的最大增长仅为~2%，远低于解决该紧张所需的~8%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对哈勃常数紧张问题的“不可行定理”（no-go theorem）主要局限于BAO归一化约束（product H₀r_d），但晚期宇宙解不仅受归一化限制，还受膨胀历史形状（dimensionless expansion rate E(z)）的约束。本文旨在系统量化这一“形状壁垒”对H₀增长的约束上限。

Method: 推导了当声学视界（sound horizon, r_d）和声学角尺度（acoustic angular scale, θ_s）固定时，H₀分数变化与无量纲径距离积分I分数变化之间的近似等式：δH₀/H₀ ≃ δI/I。利用高斯过程（Gaussian Processes）对PantheonPlus SNeIa和DESI DR2 BAO数据进行非参数重建（nonparametric reconstruction），重构E(z)并约束I的变化。

Result: 在最保守的分析（使用PantheonPlus SNeIa和DESI DR2 BAO数据）中，H₀的最大分数增长仅为≤ 2%，远小于解决哈勃常数紧张所需的≥ 8%。该形状壁垒在引入早期宇宙新物理（early-time new physics）时仍然存在。

Conclusion: 晚期宇宙对膨胀历史E(z)的修改，无论单独使用还是与早期宇宙新物理结合，都不仅面临已知的归一化壁垒，还面临一个严格的百分量级形状壁垒，这严重限制了通过晚期方案缓解哈勃常数紧张的可能空间。

Abstract: The standard "no-go theorem" against late-time solutions to the Hubble tension is essentially a normalization wall, since Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) measurements constrain the product $H_0r_d$, with $r_d$ the sound horizon at baryon drag. However, late-time solutions (which keep $r_d$ fixed) are tightly constrained not only by the BAO normalization $H_0r_d$, but also by the shape of the expansion history, i.e. the dimensionless expansion rate $E(z) \equiv H(z)/H_0$. We show that, if $r_d$ and the acoustic angular scale $θ_s$ are fixed, an increase in $H_0$ needs to be matched by an equal fractional increase in the dimensionless distance integral $I \equiv \int dz/E(z)$: $δH_0/H_0 \simeq δI/I$. We use this to quantify the "shape wall" set by relative distance constraints on $E(z)$, which we reconstruct nonparametrically, using Gaussian Processes and the latest unanchored Type Ia Supernovae (SNeIa) and BAO data. In our most conservative analysis using PantheonPlus SNeIa and DESI DR2 BAO data, we find a maximum fractional increase in $H_0$ of $\lesssim 2\%$, falling well short of the $\gtrsim 8\%$ required to solve the tension. This shape wall holds even in the presence of early-time new physics, and limits the maximum increase in $H_0$ which can be contributed by late-time modifications to $E(z)$ at fixed $θ_s$. Therefore, late-time modifications, whether invoked alone or alongside early-time new physics, face not only the well-known normalization wall, but also a stringent percent-level shape wall.

</details>


### [149] [Hubble tension: a short review of theoretical explanations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21497)
*Jia-Qi Wang,Zong-Kuan Guo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文综述了为解决哈勃常数（Hubble constant）在宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）测量与局域距离阶梯（local distance ladder）测定之间的不一致（即“哈勃张力”），针对修改引力（modified gravity）及其他早期与晚期宇宙学机制的理论方案。当前方案虽能降低名义张力，但常导致CMB谱、标准尺距离、引力透镜、结构增长等观测量的关联偏移，未来需依赖统一似然函数（unified likelihoods）与多探针检验（multiprobe tests）来整合关键观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Λ冷暗物质（Λ cold dark matter, ΛCDM）模型虽成功描述广泛宇宙学观测，但哈勃常数（Hubble constant）在CMB框架下的推断值与局域距离阶梯（local distance ladder）测定值之间存在持续且显著的差异（即“哈勃张力”）。该不一致性表明现有模型可能存在系统性问题，需从理论层面探索其根源。

Method: 本文以短评（short review）形式，系统审视从引力场方程（gravitational field equations）到复合前声波视界（pre-recombination sound horizon）及晚期距离-红移关系（late-time distance-redshift relation）的整个宇宙学推断链条。研究重点聚焦于修改引力（modified gravity），并简要讨论可通过改变声学标尺（acoustic ruler）、距离测度、结构增长或引力响应来缓解张力的早期与晚期机制。

Result: 当前提出的各类理论方案可在名义上降低哈勃张力，但通常以引起宇宙微波背景谱（CMB spectra）、标准尺距离（standard-ruler distances）、引力透镜（lensing）、结构增长（structure growth）或校准器信息（calibrator information）中的关联偏移为代价。

Conclusion: 进一步推进该领域需要构建统一似然函数（unified likelihoods）与多探针检验（multiprobe tests），将所有关键观测数据置于相同的模型假设下进行联合约束。

Abstract: The $Λ$ cold dark matter model successfully describes a wide range of cosmological observations. However, the persistent discrepancy between the value of the Hubble constant inferred from cosmic microwave background measurements within this model and that obtained from local distance-ladder determinations points to a significant inconsistency. This short review examines theoretical responses across the cosmological inference chain, from the gravitational field equations to the pre-recombination sound horizon and the late-time distance-redshift relation. We focus primarily on modified gravity, and briefly discuss early- and late-time mechanisms that can alter the acoustic ruler, distance measures, structure growth, or gravitational response. Current proposals can reduce the nominal tension, but often at the cost of correlated shifts in cosmic microwave background spectra, standard-ruler distances, lensing, structure growth, or calibrator information. Further progress requires unified likelihoods and multiprobe tests linking all key observables under the same model assumptions.

</details>

### [150] [Exploring Physics beyond the Standard Model from kHz-Gravitational-Wave Signals of Core-Collapse Supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20921)
*Kei Kotake,Takami Kuroda*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文综述了核心坍缩超新星（CCSNe）多维建模的最新进展及其产生的高频引力波（GW）信号，包括标准的中微子星（PNS）本征振荡机制以及由黑洞形成、量子色动力学（QCD）相变和标量-张量引力等奇异物理过程引发的高频GW特征，指出下一代探测器的联合分析可揭示超越标准模型和新引力理论的关键多信使信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核心坍缩超新星（CCSNe）的多维建模已能预测高频引力波（GW）信号，这些信号有望成为探测极端物质与引力的新探针。现有模拟揭示了多种超出传统机制的GW辐射过程，但需要系统性整合以识别超越标准模型和广义相对论的“确凿证据（smoking-gun signatures）”。

Method: 基于最先进的CCSNe多维模拟，分析中微子星（PNS）的特征振荡模式（如g模式和f模式）产生的准连续GW频谱，并结合完全广义相对论（GR）模拟探索高丰度前身星吸积致密化、一阶QCD相变以及标量-张量引力自发标量化的极端物理场景。

Result: PNS的g模式和f模式主导GW频谱，其频率在激波反弹后随PNS致密化从数百赫兹升至千赫兹（kHz）范围。高丰度前身星中快速吸积导致PNS迅速收缩并早期形成黑洞（BH），产生突然终止的kHz GW发射。强一阶QCD相变可诱发次级坍缩与回弹，产生超过2 kHz的毫秒级GW爆发。标量-张量引力中的自发标量化可触发多次PNS坍缩，产生类似的高频宽带GW信号。

Conclusion: 通过结合下一代GW探测器对这些信号的探测与综合分析，可为识别超越标准CCSN GW机制和广义相对论的新物理提供多信道路径。

Abstract: Recent advances in multidimensional modeling of core-collapse supernovae (CCSNe) have enabled detailed predictions of high-frequency gravitational-wave (GW) signals, offering a new probe of extreme matter and gravity. A proto-neutron star (PNS) emits quasi-continuous GWs through the excitation of its characteristic oscillation modes. State-of-the-art CCSN simulations show that these oscillations, in particular $g$- and $f$-modes, dominate the GW spectrum, with frequencies rising from a few hundred hertz to the kilohertz (kHz) range as the PNS compactness increases in the post-bounce phase. Therefore, the temporal evolution of these GW frequencies, if detected, would provide a direct and quantitative tracer of the PNS internal structure and the surrounding explosive dynamics. In addition to such standard GW emission mechanism, fully general relativistic (GR) simulations have revealed additional GW sources linked to more exotic physical processes. In highly massive progenitors, continuous mass accretion drives rapid PNS contraction and early black-hole (BH) formation, producing strong kHz GW emission that abruptly ceases when the PNS core is swallowed by the BH horizon. Similarly, a strong first-order quantum chromodynamics (QCD) phase transition can induce a secondary collapse and rebound of the nascent quark core, generating powerful, millisecond-duration GW bursts with frequencies exceeding $\sim$2 kHz. Alternative theories of gravity, such as scalar-tensor frameworks, predict spontaneous scalarization that can trigger multiple collapses of the PNS, yielding analogous high-frequency and broadband GW signals. The combined analysis of these GW signals, together with their detection by next-generation GW detectors, offers a promising multi-messenger pathway to identify smoking-gun signatures of new physics beyond the standard model of the CCSN GW mechanism and general relativity.

</details>


### [151] [Ultra-High-Energy Particle Production in Binary Mergers Endowed with Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21385)
*Carlos H. Coimbra-Araujo,Rita C. Anjos,Jonas P. Pereira,Jaziel G. Coelho*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA探测的双星系统并合前阶段中，通过Bañados–Silk–West (BSW)机制产生超高能粒子的过程。在磁化Kerr时空（magnetized Kerr spacetime）中求解带电粒子的测地线方程，发现视界附近的碰撞可实现质心系能量（center-of-mass energy）$E_{\mathrm{cm}} \sim 10^{18}$–$10^{20}$ eV，达到超高能宇宙射线（UHECR）范围。分析揭示了三种加速区间，并针对34个高自旋引力波事件计算了最大可达能量，确立了磁化双星并合系统作为UHECR有前景的来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索双星并合系统在并合前阶段能否通过BSW机制产生超高能粒子，从而为超高能宇宙射线（UHECR）的来源提供理论解释，并将引力波观测与粒子加速效率定量关联起来。

Method: 在磁化Kerr时空中求解带电粒子的测地线方程（geodesic equations），系统扫描并合残余体的参数空间，包括黑洞质量（$M \sim 20$–$150\,M_\odot$）、无量纲自旋（$\chi_f \sim 0.7$–$0.9$）、磁场强度（$B \sim 10^{12}$–$10^{14}$ G）及粒子角动量，并对34个高自旋（$\chi_f > 0.7$）引力波事件计算最大可达能量。

Result: 发现三种加速区间：引力主导区间（$B < 10^{12}$ G，磁增强可忽略）、过渡区间（$10^{12}~\text{G} \lesssim B \lesssim 10^{13}$ G，引力与磁效应竞争）和磁主导区间（$B > 10^{13}$ G，碰撞能量提升近一个数量级）。自旋 $\chi_f \gtrsim 0.85$ 且质量 $M \gtrsim 100\,M_\odot$ 的系统最大能量可达 $E_{\mathrm{max}} \sim 10^{20}$ eV。

Conclusion: 磁化双星并合系统，特别是黑洞–中子星系统以及双中子星并合形成的黑洞残余体，是超高能宇宙射线的有前景来源；研究提供了将引力波可观测物理量与粒子加速效率联系起来的定量预测。

Abstract: We study the production of ultra-high-energy particles via the Bañados--Silk--West (BSW) mechanism in the pre-merger phase of binary systems detected by LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA. By solving the geodesic equations for charged particles in magnetized Kerr spacetime with fields of $B \sim 10^{12}$--$10^{14}$~G, we demonstrate that collisions near the horizon can achieve center-of-mass energies $E_{\mathrm{cm}} \sim 10^{18}$-- $10^{20}$~eV, placing them firmly in the ultra-high-energy cosmic-ray (UHECR) range. We systematically explore the parameter space of merger remnants, varying black hole mass ($M \sim 20$--$150\,M_\odot$, characteristic of the binary black hole population), dimensionless spin ($χ_f \sim 0.7$--$0.9$), magnetic field strength, and particle angular momenta. Our analysis reveals three distinct acceleration regimes: a gravity-dominated regime ($B < 10^{12}$~G) with negligible magnetic enhancement; a transition regime ($10^{12}~\text{G} \lesssim B \lesssim 10^{13}~\text{G}$) where gravitational and magnetic effects compete; and a magnetic-dominated regime ($B > 10^{13}$~G) where fields amplify collision energies by nearly an order of magnitude. For the 34 gravitational-wave events with high remnant spins ($χ_f > 0.7$), we compute the maximum achievable energies, finding that systems with $χ_f \gtrsim 0.85$ and $M \gtrsim 100\,M_\odot$ can reach $E_{\mathrm{max}} \sim 10^{20}$~eV. Our results establish magnetized binary mergers, particularly black hole--neutron star systems and postmerger black hole remnants formed in binary neutron star coalescences, as promising sources of UHECRs and provide quantitative predictions linking gravitational-wave observables to particle acceleration efficiency.

</details>

### [152] [Driven criticality links universal computation and optimal representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21232)
*Adrián Roig,Miguel A. Muñoz,Guillermo B. Morales*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文在储备池计算（reservoir computing）框架下，通过引入有限分辨率邻域可分离性指标和输入条件最大李雅普诺夫指数（input-conditioned maximal Lyapunov exponent），展示了邻域可分离性、混沌时间序列预测和平滑高维表示几何在边际驱动稳定性（marginal driven stability）的狭窄窗口内同时达到最优，并将边缘不稳定性计算、普适性、读出性能和最优表示几何统一在一个动力学框架中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近临界动力学（near-critical dynamics）常被认为与增强的计算能力相关，但其潜在机制尚不清楚。本文旨在储备池计算这一具体框架中阐明该问题。

Method: 将固定储备池普适性结果推广到离散时间输入驱动储备池，建立其关键几何条件——邻域可分离性（neighborhood separation）——与动力学之间的联系。为此引入有限分辨率邻域可分离性指标（finite-resolution neighborhood separability index）和输入条件最大李雅普诺夫指数。

Result: 邻域可分离性、混沌时间序列预测和平滑高维表示几何在边际驱动稳定性的同一狭窄窗口内同时达到最优。在该区域中，协方差谱（covariance spectrum）趋近于近最优平滑表示所预期的幂律标度（power-law scaling）。

Conclusion: 本文将边缘不稳定性计算（edge-of-instability computation）、普适性（universality）、读出性能（readout performance）和最优表示几何（optimal representation geometry）统一在一个共同的动力学框架中。

Abstract: Near-critical dynamics are often linked to enhanced computation, but the underlying mechanism remains unclear. We address this question in reservoir computing, where a fixed recurrent network maps input sequences into high-dimensional states and only a simple readout is trained. We extend fixed-reservoir universality results to discrete-time input-driven reservoirs and connect their key geometric condition, neighborhood separation, to dynamics. To this end, we introduce a finite-resolution neighborhood separability index and an input-conditioned maximal Lyapunov exponent. We find that neighborhood separability, chaotic time-series prediction, and smooth high-dimensional representation geometry are optimized in the same narrow window of marginal driven stability. In this regime, the covariance spectrum approaches the power-law scaling expected for near-optimal smooth representations. Our results link edge-of-instability computation, universality, readout performance, and optimal representation geometry within a common dynamical framework.

### [153] [Scalable Low-Cost Laboratory Automation: A Digital Twin-Integrated Robotic Platform for Autonomous Liquid Handling (RAINBOTTM)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20662)
*Mohamed Rami Ayeche,Souhil Sid,Ahyen Mostofa,Rehaan Hussain,Ali Shayesteh,Fadwa El Mellouhi*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文介绍RAINBOT\textsuperscript{TM}，一种基于消费级3D打印机改造的低成本、开放可复现的液体处理机器人，其配备浏览器数字孪生实现远程监控，并集成CEID\textsuperscript{TM}逆设计框架，以低于1300美元的成本实现了接近商业系统的实验自动化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验室自动化虽能加速科学发现，但商业液体处理系统（liquid-handling system）成本高昂、设计专有且远程可监督性有限，限制了其广泛采用。

Method: 将消费级笛卡尔3D打印机（Elegoo Neptune 4 Max）的挤出机替换为精密单通道移液器（single-channel pipette），通过打印机原有的G代码驱动的X-Y-Z龙门架驱动；吸头弹出和柱塞运动由两个紧凑型线性致动器（linear actuator）在Python控制下完成。同时实现基于浏览器的数字孪生（digital twin），与物理平台双向同步，实时反映运动学和移液状态，支持远程监控、干预和紧急停止。

Result: 作为概念验证，RAINBOT\textsuperscript{TM}完成了不同颜色水溶液的序贯交换实验，集成颜色传感器定量测量混合结果；红、黄、蓝（RYB）响应与预期混合行为的平均绝对误差（mean absolute error）在两个百分点以内。完整硬件成本低于1300美元，约为入门级商业系统的十分之一。

Conclusion: RAINBOT\textsuperscript{TM}建立了一个低成本、可访问的物理-虚拟框架（physical–virtual framework），支持自驱动实验室自动化（self-driving laboratory automation），并通过集成CEID\textsuperscript{TM}框架将实验从迭代手动猜测转变为目标导向的逆设计搜索（inverse-design search），同时保持人机协同。

Abstract: Laboratory automation accelerates discovery, yet its adoption is constrained by the high cost, proprietary design, and limited remote supervisability of commercial liquid-handling systems. This work presents RAINBOT\textsuperscript{TM}, a low-cost, openly reproducible liquid-handling robot built by converting a consumer-grade Cartesian 3D printer (Elegoo Neptune 4 Max). The printer extruder is replaced by a precision single-channel pipette actuated through the printer's own G-code-driven X--Y--Z gantry, with plunger and tip-eject motions effected by two compact linear actuators under Python control. To make experiments transparent and remotely supervisable, a browser-based digital twin is implemented to synchronise bidirectionally with the physical platform, mirroring kinematics and pipetting states in real time and exposing remote monitoring, intervention, and an emergency stop from any web browser. As a proof of concept, RAINBOT\textsuperscript{TM} performed sequential exchanges of differently coloured aqueous solutions while an integrated colour sensor quantified the resulting mixtures; measured red, yellow, and blue (RYB) responses agreed with expected mixing behaviour to within a mean absolute error of two percentage points, validating correct execution and real-time tracking. Closing the loop, the platform is coupled to the CEID\textsuperscript{TM} (Cooperative Explorer for Inverse Design) framework, which recasts experimentation from iterative manual guessing into a goal-directed inverse-design search while keeping a human in the loop. The complete hardware costs under US\$1300, which is roughly an order of magnitude below entry-level commercial handlers, thereby establishing an accessible physical--virtual framework for self-driving laboratory automation.

</details>

### [154] [Doubling for chronological diamonds in Lorentzian geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21423)
*Mauricio Che,Sebastian Gieger,Clemens Sämann*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文定义了以时间顺序菱形（chronological diamonds）为基础的测度洛伦兹长度空间（measured Lorentzian length spaces）的加倍条件（doubling conditions），证明了这种条件可由适当的类时曲率界（timelike curvature bounds）推出，首次在洛伦兹几何中将加倍与曲率界联系起来，并由此得到了洛伦兹广义锥（Lorentzian generalized cones）在Mondino--Sämann提出的洛伦兹Gromov--Hausdorff收敛下的紧致性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者在测度洛伦兹长度空间中引入基于时间顺序菱形的加倍条件，并通过理论推导证明该条件可由类时曲率界（timelike curvature bounds）推出。

Result: 首次建立了洛伦兹几何中加倍条件与曲率界之间的蕴含关系，并基于此获得了洛伦兹广义锥在洛伦兹Gromov--Hausdorff收敛意义下的紧致性结果。

Conclusion: 测度洛伦兹长度空间中的加倍条件可以从合适的类时曲率界导出，这为研究洛伦兹几何中的紧致性问题提供了新的工具，并推广了相关收敛理论的应用范围。

Abstract: We define doubling conditions for measured Lorentzian length spaces in terms of chronological diamonds, and prove that such conditions are implied by suitable timelike curvature bounds. In particular, for the first time, we relate doubling to curvature bounds in Lorentzian geometry. As a consequence, we obtain compactness results for Lorentzian generalized cones with respect to the Lorentzian Gromov--Hausdorff convergence introduced by Mondino--Sämann.

Conclusion: 本研究扩展了彭罗斯猜想的适用范围，表明在适当的能量条件和曲率条件下，该猜想对于具有外在曲率的初始数据集仍然成立，深化了对黑洞质量与视界面积之间关系的理解。

Abstract: Let $(M^3, g, \mathbf{k})$ be a smooth, connected, asymptotically flat initial data set with outermost past apparent horizon. We prove the Penrose conjecture for each connected component of the boundary, assuming the dominant energy condition and the $2$-convexity condition that the sum of the two smallest eigenvalues of $\mathbf{k}$ is nonnegative. The main tool is the $σ$-inverse mean curvature flow and a monotonicity formula developed in \cite{Dong26SigmaIMCF}.

### [156] [Perturbatively Stable Self-Correcting Classical Memory from Gauge Averaging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20605)

Abstract: We show that the self-correcting memory in 3d Wegner gauge theory is stable to arbitrary small enough perturbations of the Hamiltonian. Our proof relies on a new method we dub ``gauge averaging'', which gives conditions under which explicitly broken gauge symmetries are effectively restored by fluctuations. These conditions show that the self-correcting memory phase is fluctuation stabilized, with its robustness to perturbations increasing with increasing temperature, up to some $T_c > 0$.

### [157] [A solution to 2-copy distillability of Werner states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21367)
*Jinshi Fu,Li Gao,Sang-Jun Park*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文通过理论证明的方法，系统分析了任意维度下Werner态的2-拷贝蒸馏条件，并将其与1-拷贝蒸馏条件进行了等价性论证。

Result: 证明了任意维度的Werner态是2-拷贝可蒸馏的当且仅当它是1-拷贝可蒸馏的。这一结果回应了关于Werner态2-拷贝可蒸馏性的长期公开问题。

Conclusion: 该结果为最终确定是否所有NPT态均可蒸馏提供了重要进展，但该核心问题仍未完全解决。

Abstract: Entanglement distillation is a fundamental task in quantum information theory. In this work, we prove that Werner states in arbitrary dimension are 2-copy distillable if and only if they are 1-copy distillable. This answers the longstanding open question of the 2-copy distillability of Werner states. This is an important step on determining whether every non-positive partial transpose (NPT) state is distillable, which remains one of the central open problems in the field of entanglement distillation.

### [158] [Unitary $k$-designs without Hamiltonian quenches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20640)
*Pratik Nandy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无需多次哈密顿量淬火（Hamiltonian quench）即可生成近似酉设计（unitary $k$-designs）的双泡利冲击（2PK）协议：在固定混沌哈密顿量的演化中插入两次泡利算符，即可使时间系综收敛至Haar值，并在高斯随机矩阵、SYK模型及简化自旋SYK模型中验证，还建立了有限温帧势（finite-temperature frame potential）的规范定义及全息对偶解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 酉设计（unitary designs）能在无需指数资源的情况下模拟Haar随机性，但现有方法即使采用时间系综（temporal ensembles）也需多次独立哈密顿量淬火。本研究试图证明单个混沌哈密顿量即足以生成近似酉设计，从而简化资源需求。

Method: 提出双泡利冲击（2PK）协议：在固定混沌哈密顿量的幺正演化中插入两次泡利算符（Pauli operator insertions）作为“冲击”（kicks）。通过计算帧势（frame potential）评估系综与Haar值的收敛性，并对高斯随机矩阵系综、Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型及简化自旋（玻色子）SYK模型进行验证。

Result: 该协议生成的系综帧势收敛至Haar值，表明近似酉设计（approximate unitary designs）的出现。此外，该协议可给出有限温帧势（finite-temperature frame potentials）的规范定义，并建立了与配分函数（partition function）的关系。

Conclusion: 单一混沌哈密顿量结合两次泡利冲击即可生成近似酉设计，无需多次淬火；该协议还具有有限温推广及全息对偶（holographic interpretation）的潜在解释。

Abstract: Unitary designs provide an efficient means of emulating Haar randomness without the requirement of exponential resources. Hamiltonian quench protocols have recently been shown to generate such designs, but achieving this typically requires multiple independent Hamiltonian quenches, even via temporal ensembles. Here, we show that no Hamiltonian quenches are required: a single chaotic Hamiltonian is sufficient to generate approximate unitary $k$-designs. We introduce a two-Pauli-kick (2PK) protocol, where unitary evolution under a fixed Hamiltonian is interspersed with two Pauli operator insertions (kicks). By evaluating the frame potential, we demonstrate that the resulting ensemble converges to the Haar value, indicating the emergence of approximate unitary designs. We verify this protocol for Gaussian random matrix ensembles, the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model, and simplified spin (bosonic) SYK models. Furthermore, our protocol admits a canonical definition of finite-temperature frame potentials and establishes the relation with the partition function. We outline a plausible holographic interpretation of our protocol from the dual gravity picture.
