### [159] [Detecting Hidden Nonlinear High Frequency Modes Beyond Fundamental Minimal Temporal Resolution Using Weak Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20647)
*Igor Prlina*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非线性量子力学效应若仅以高频模式存在，是否能通过强测量避免被探测。通过定义时间不可区分性公设并构建非线性玩具模型，发现即使在这种理想设置下，桌面级弱后选择测量仍能探测到非线性行为，并对超出基本时间分辨率的非线性高频演化模式施加约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验一种假设：量子力学中的非线性效应（nonlinear effects）如果仅以高频模式（high frequency modes）存在，能否通过强测量（strong measurements）避免被实验探测。这一问题关乎非线性量子力学理论的可检验性及其与标准量子力学的区分边界。

Method: 首先定义了一个时间不可区分性公设（temporal indistinguishability postulate），用以描述在基本不可区分的时间尺度上进行振幅级时间平均（amplitude level time averaging）的过程。随后手工构建了一个特别适合规避探测的非线性玩具模型（nonlinear toy model），并在此理想化框架下分析弱后选择测量（weak postselected measurements）的探测能力。

Result: 即使在最有利于隐藏非线性效应的理想设置下，桌面级弱后选择测量仍然能够探测到非线性行为。该探测能力可以对非线性高频演化模式施加约束（put constraints），即使这些模式的频率超出了基本的最小时间分辨率（fundamental minimal temporal resolution）。

Conclusion: 非线性量子力学效应即使以超出基本时间分辨率的高频模式存在，也无法完全逃避弱后选择测量的探测。这表明对非线性量子理论的实验约束可以扩展到极高频率区域，从而压缩了非线性效应可能隐藏的参数空间。

Abstract: In this work we study whether nonlinear models of quantum mechanics can avoid detection by strong measurements, if the nonlinear effects only exist as high frequency modes. A potential physical process which could hide such modes would be amplitude level time averaging over fundamentally indistinguishable times. To that end, we have defined a temporal indistinguishability postulate which describes the averaging process, and handcrafted a nonlinear toy model well suited to avoid detection. We have demonstrated that even in such an ideal setup, tabletop weak postselected measurements can still detect nonlinear behavior and put constraints on nonlinear high frequency modes of evolution, even at frequencies beyond fundamental minimal temporal resolution.

</details>


### [160] [Large deviations in quantum dynamics and complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20959)
*Xiangyu Cao,Jorge Kurchan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了多体量子动力学中大偏差（large deviation）的三种定义，揭示了它们在达到长时间极限时的时间尺度存在巨大差异——从O(1)到exp(e^N)——并指出演化前沿的移动可作为量子复杂性的度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在系统性地理解多体量子动力学中大偏差行为的长时间极限收敛时间，并探索如何通过大偏差前沿的演化来刻画量子复杂性（quantum complexity）。

Method: 研究比较了三种大偏差定义：(i) 基于可观测量的全分布（full distribution）；(ii) 基于对可观测量连续监测（continuous monitoring）所得测量结果在时间区间 t ≤ t_max 内的分布；(iii) 基于 t ≤ t_max 内期望值（expectation values）的分布。分析对象为无守恒律（conservation laws）的通用系统。

Result: 定义(i)在t ~ O(1)时达到长时间极限，与系统大小N无关。定义(ii)和(iii)分别需t ~ e^N和t ~ exp(e^N)才能达到长时间极限。在达到极限之前，已探索与未探索结果/期望值之间存在尖锐边界（sharp frontier），其分布为长时间极限在该边界处的截断版本。

Conclusion: 这些边界值随t_max的漂移提供了量子复杂性的一种度量方式，揭示了不同大偏差定义下量子动力学复杂度的巨大差异。

Abstract: We study three definitions of large deviation in many-body quantum dynamics: (i) via the full distribution of an extensive observable, (ii) via the distribution of measurement outcomes (from a continuous monitoring of the observable) over a time interval $t \le t_{\max}$, and (iii) via the distribution of expectation values over $t \le t_{\max}$. In generic systems without conservation laws, the large deviation function (i) reaches its longtime limit at $t \sim \mathcal{O}(1)$, independently of system size $N$. (ii) and (iii) reach their longtime limit at $t \sim e^{ N}$ and $t \sim \exp(e^{N})$, respectively. Before that, there is a {\it sharp} frontier between the explored and unexplored outcomes/expectation values; their distribution equals the longtime limit truncated at values that drift with $t_{\max}$. We propose that the evolution of these values with $t_{\max}$ provides a measure of quantum complexity.

</details>


### [161] [Beyond Calabrese-Cardy Scaling: Exceptional-Point Sensitivity from the de Sitter RT Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21536)
*Kuang-Hung Chou*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现，在非厄米（non-Hermitian）临界链中，当系统靠近例外点（exceptional point）时，双正交熵（biorthogonal entropy）中会出现一个与子系统大小无关的残余项 \(S_{\rm res}=\log(\Delta L)\)，这一行为在厄米（Hermitian）临界系统中不存在。该结果可通过非酉多尺度纠缠重整化（non-unitary continuous multiscale entanglement renormalization）所生成的德西特（de Sitter, dS）几何加以解释：残余熵源自红外（IR）端点的长程纠缠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的一维临界系统中的纠缠熵遵循Calabrese-Cardy标度律。然而，在非厄米临界链中，例外点附近的行为尚不明确，尤其是亚有限尺寸能隙（sub-finite-size gap）对纠缠熵的影响机制有待揭示。

Method: 本文通过解析计算有限尺寸非厄米临界链的双正交熵，分析其对小能隙 \(\Delta\) 的依赖关系；并利用非酉连续多尺度纠缠重整化（cMERA）生成的德西特几何，从红外端点的贡献出发对残余熵进行理论解释。

Result: 在通常的Calabrese-Cardy项之上，双正交熵中出现一个与子系统大小无关的残余项 \(S_{\rm res}=\log(\Delta L)\)，表现为垂直偏移（vertical offset），即使对单比特子系统也可检测。该行为在厄米临界链中不存在——亚有限尺寸能隙对酉临界链的纠缠熵无效，而非厄米系统中纠缠熵仍能通过 \(\Delta L\) 依赖关系分辨该能隙。

Conclusion: 非厄米临界链中的残余熵源于红外端点的贡献：有限环上的正则电路（regular circuit）无法终止于单比特乘积态，而是留下一个纠缠的双比特红外态。计算该红外态的纠缠可恢复相同的 \(\log(\Delta L)\) 项，从而将这种额外的长程纠缠识别为有限深度退纠缠（finite-depth disentangling）后残留的残余熵。

Abstract: Entanglement entropy at one-dimensional criticality typically follows the Calabrese-Cardy scaling. In non-Hermitian critical chains near exceptional points, however, we show that the biorthogonal entropy of a finite system retains an additional sensitivity to a small energy gap \(Δ\) even when \(Δ< 1/L\). On top of the usual Calabrese-Cardy term, we find an interval-independent contribution \(S_{\rm res}=\log(ΔL)\), visible as a vertical offset and detectable even for a one-site subsystem. This behavior has no Hermitian analogue: a sub-finite-size gap is effectively invisible to entanglement in unitary critical chains, whereas here the entropy continues to resolve such a gap through its dependence on \(ΔL\). We interpret the result within the de Sitter geometry generated by non-unitary continuous multiscale entanglement renormalization: because the dS extremal surface reaches the IR endpoint, entanglement necessarily retains the endpoint contribution. On a finite ring, a regular circuit cannot terminate at a one-site product state and instead leaves an entangled two-site IR state. Computing the entanglement of the IR state recovers the same \(\log(ΔL)\) term, identifying this additional long-range entanglement as the residual entropy left after finite-depth disentangling.

</details>


### [162] [General Concurrence Percolation on Quantum Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2501.11004)
*Deep Nath,Soumen Roy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对量子网络中非最大纠缠态难以直接用于远距离量子通信的问题，提出了一种基于键渗流（bond percolation）的通用并发渗流（GCP）协议，用于在二维晶格量子网络中构造最大纠缠态网络。研究表明，GCP协议的渗流阈值低于现有协议，且与现有协议同属一个渗流普适类（percolation universality class）。作者还引入并解析求解了一个最小模型，以解释GCP阈值更低的内在机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子网络中，最大纠缠态（maximally entangled state）比非最大纠缠态（nonmaximally entangled state）能够更有效地实现远距离量子通信，但实验上难以直接产生和维持最大纠缠态；非最大纠缠态则更为常见。因此，需要利用非最大纠缠态构成的网络结构，通过特定协议在远距离节点间建立最大纠缠。

Method: 将二维晶格视为量子网络（quantum network），边（edge）表示非最大纠缠纯态（pure state）。提出一种基于键渗流（bond percolation）的通用协议——通用并发渗流（general concurrence percolation, GCP），用于将非最大纠缠态网络转化为最大纠缠态网络。通过有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis）在二维晶格上确定渗流临界值，并引入一个可解析求解的最小模型（minimal model）。

Result: GCP的渗流阈值（percolation threshold）小于现有协议的渗流阈值。与现有协议类似，GCP也属于渗流普适类（percolation universality class）。通过最小模型的解析求解，揭示了GCP实现更低渗流阈值的根本原因。

Conclusion: GCP协议能够在二维晶格量子网络上以低于现有协议的渗流阈值构造最大纠缠态网络，从而有望实现更高效的远距离量子通信。该协议与现有协议同属一个渗流普适类，最小模型为理解其性能优势提供了理论依据。

Abstract: A quantum network is a network of entangled states, which can be used to transmit quantum information. Nonmaximally entangled states are not really effective in establishing quantum communication across vast distances. Creating and maintaining a maximally entangled state over which quantum information can be transferred more effectively is difficult in experiments, as nonmaximally entangled states are typically produced there. Therefore, we usually construct a network of nonmaximally entangled states and use the underlying network structure to establish maximal entanglement between distant nodes. Various protocols leveraging interesting aspects of quantum and statistical physics are designed to achieve long-range maximally entangled states. Here, we consider two-dimensional lattices as quantum networks where edges represent nonmaximally entangled pure states. We introduce a general protocol based on bond percolation -- general concurrence percolation (GCP) -- to create a network of maximally entangled states. The associated network obtained through GCP ought to enable the achievement of long-range quantum communication. Our observations indicate that, similar to other existing protocols, GCP falls within the percolation universality class, as determined through finite-size scaling analysis performed on two-dimensional lattices. We find that the associated percolation threshold value is smaller than that of the existing protocols. We introduce and analytically solve a minimal model that renders insight into the origin of the fundamentally lower percolation threshold achieved by GCP.

</details>


### [163] [Autonomization of Quantum Systems and the Emergence of the Work Operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20602)
*Carlo Cepollaro,Danial Chughtai,Alberto Spalvieri,Marcus Huber,Alberto Rolandi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过将受控量子系统嵌入到更大系统的能量守恒演化中，提出了一种量子功（quantum work）的新定义——功算符（work operator），解决了量子热力学中功是否可作为量子可观测量（quantum observable）的长期争议，并推导了量子涨落定理（quantum fluctuation theorem），将框架扩展至开放量子系统后得到了算符形式的热力学第一定律（first law）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子功估算方法假定系统受经典控制（classical control），但控制本身的能量成本常被忽略，其量级可能远超系统能标，导致功的数值缺乏操作性意义（operational significance）。作者旨在通过自主化（autonomizing）受控能量转移，消除对外部经典控制的依赖，从而为量子功提供一致且可操作的定义。

Method: 将受驱动动力学（driven dynamics）嵌入到一个更大量子系统的能量守恒演化（energy-conserving evolution）中，使能量转移发生在两个系统之间，从而将功唯一地定义为系统间转移的能量，并由此导出作用于受驱系统上的唯一可观测量——功算符（work operator）。

Result: 推导出量子涨落定理，在经典极限下恢复Jarzynski等式（Jarzynski equality）；表明量子功算符规避了相关的不可行定理（no-go theorem）；考虑了不完美控制（imperfect control）并修正了功统计量（work statistics）；在开放量子系统（open quantum systems）中，获得了算符形式的第一定律，其中功、热（heat）与内能变化（internal-energy change）由约化系统上的不同算符表示。

Conclusion: 当控制系统被纳入描述而非视作外部因素时，功确实是一个量子可观测量。该框架解决了功在量子热力学中的可观测量地位这一长期争议。

Abstract: Estimation of work at the quantum scale remains a central challenge in quantum thermodynamics. Canonical approaches have a fundamental drawback: they assume classical control of the quantum system, as implicit in a time-dependent Hamiltonian. Yet the energetic cost of implementing this control is omitted and can exceed the system's energy scale by orders of magnitude, calling into question the operational significance of work values. We address this by autonomizing the controlled energy transfer, embedding the driven dynamics into an energy-conserving evolution on a larger quantum system. Work is then unambiguously identified with the energy transferred between the two systems, singling out a unique observable on the driven system: the work operator. We show that the quantum work operator evades a no-go theorem by deriving a quantum fluctuation theorem that recovers the Jarzynski equality in classical scenarios. We incorporate imperfect control and quantify corrections to work statistics. Extending the framework to open quantum systems, we obtain an operatorial first law in which work, heat, and internal-energy changes are represented by distinct operators on the reduced system. Together, these results settle the long-standing debate over whether work is a quantum observable: it is, once the controlling system is included in the description rather than treated as external.

</details>


### [164] [Learning the closest Slater determinant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20623)
*Nisarga Paul,Haimeng Zhao,David D. Dai*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究如何从任意费米子多体态（fermionic many-body state）中学习具有最大保真度（fidelity）的斯莱特行列式（Slater determinant），提供了经典与量子算法并证明其复杂度最优性，同时揭示了优化景观（optimization landscape）在保真度2/3处的相变（transition point）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统的紧凑、可解释描述是量子科学的重要任务。本文受Hartree-Fock方法与不可知层析成像（agnostic tomography）启发，研究从任意费米子多体态中学习最优斯莱特行列式的问题。

Method: 给出经典与量子算法，在时间$m^{\text{poly}(n,1/\varepsilon)}$内返回保真度在$\varepsilon$以内的斯莱特行列式。量子算法在拥有量子副本（quantum copies）时仅需$\text{poly}(m,n,1/\varepsilon)$个副本。同时利用复杂度理论假设证明下界（hardness lower bounds），并分析优化景观。

Result: 证明保真度高于2/3时任何驻点（stationary point）均为唯一全局最大值，低于2/3时优化景观（optimization landscape）会产生虚假驻点（spurious stationary points），从而2/3为该问题的相变点。在Fermi-Hubbard模型上将算法应用于神经量子态（neural quantum state）解，提取最近的斯莱特行列式。

Conclusion: 为经典或量子模拟中理解费米子多体系统提供了具有可证明保证（provable guarantees）的算法工具。

Abstract: Learning compact, interpretable descriptions of quantum many-body states is an important task in quantum science. We study the task of learning the Slater determinant with maximum fidelity to an arbitrary fermionic many-body state, with motivation from both Hartree-Fock methods and agnostic tomography. Given an $n$-fermion wavefunction built from $m$ fermionic modes, we provide classical and quantum algorithms returning a Slater determinant with fidelity within $\varepsilon$ of maximal in time $m^{\text{poly}(n,1/\varepsilon)}$. We prove matching hardness lower bounds, assuming standard complexity conjectures, along some parameter axes. Given access to quantum copies, we prove this can be accomplished with $\text{poly}(m,n,1/\varepsilon)$ copies of $ρ$. We also show that above a fidelity of $2/3$ any stationary point is the unique global maximum while below $2/3$ the optimization landscape can have spurious stationary points, and hence $2/3$ marks a transition point in the optimization landscape for this problem. We apply the algorithm to the Fermi-Hubbard model, extracting the closest Slater determinant from neural quantum state solutions. Together, our results provide algorithmic tools with provable guarantees in understanding fermionic many-body systems with classical or quantum simulation.

</details>


### [165] [Fermionic Genuine Multiparty Entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.20707)
*James Allen,Liuke Lyu,William Witczak-Krempa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种可通过半定规划高效计算的费米子体系中的真正多体纠缠度量——费米子真正多体负性（fGMN），证明其是纠缠单调且为费米子负性（fermionic negativity）的自然多体推广。研究发现，许多态（包括大规模费米子稳定子态）具有fGMN但无非费米子真正多体纠缠（GME），并且fGMN在分离性和温度参数上展现出与双费米子负性不同的有限突然死亡点等新现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双体费米子纠缠度量已有成熟框架，但费米子系统中的真正多体纠缠（GME）尚缺乏深入理解。因此，需要建立一种高效可计算且具有物理意义的费米子GME度量，以填补该领域空白。

Method: 通过半定规划（semi-definite programming）定义了一种可高效计算的费米子真正多体负性（fGMN），并将其构造为费米子负性（fermionic negativity）的自然多体推广。同时证明了该度量满足纠缠单调（entanglement monotone）性质。

Result: 发现许多量子态（包括大类的费米子稳定子态（fermionic stabilizer states））具有fGMN但无非费米子的GME。fGMN在分离性（separation）和温度（temperature）参数下展现出有限突然死亡点（finite sudden death points），这与双体费米子负性存在显著的现象学差异。

Conclusion: fGMN为费米子体系中真正多体纠缠的刻画提供了高效且物理意义明确的工具，揭示了费米子多体纠缠与玻色子或自旋体系之间根本不同的行为特质，尤其是在多体纠缠的存在性与相变特征方面。

Abstract: Entanglement can show fundamentally different behavior in fermionic systems. However, while bipartite measures of fermionic entanglement have been established, genuine multiparty entanglement (GME) in fermionic systems is much less understood. We introduce an efficiently computable measure (via semi-definite programming) of fermionic GME, fermion genuine multiparty negativity (fGMN), and show that it is an entanglement monotone and a natural multipartite extension of the fermionic negativity. Using this measure, we find many states which have fGMN but no non-fermionic GME, including large classes of fermionic stabilizer states. The fGMN also displays some major phenomenological differences to the bipartite fermionic negativity, such as finite sudden death points over separation and temperature.

</details>

Conclusion: 该实验代表了向长距离自由空间量子通信（long-distance free-space quantum communication）以及在未来高需求场景（如基于卫星的量子网络（satellite-based quantum networks））中实现时间关联纠缠态（time-correlated entangled states）的重要基准。

Abstract: Time-evolving entangled states describe quantum particles whose correlations evolve in time according to a well-defined dynamics. Such states can be generated in a variety of physical systems and are promising resources for several quantum technologies, ranging from quantum clock synchronization to quantum communication. However, their full potential is currently limited by the fact that the entanglement dynamics often occur on timescales comparable to the achievable synchronization precision, especially in experiments aimed at distributing entanglement through noisy urban channels. In this context, accurate timing is not merely a technical detail, but a fundamental requirement for faithfully observing and exploiting the underlying quantum correlations. Here, we demonstrate the faithful distribution of a fast-evolving entangled state over a 270 m free-space channel connecting two buildings in the center of Rome. The developed system incorporates a synchronization device capable of achieving sub-50 ps timing accuracy between the two ends of the link while simultaneously supporting channel stabilization. Our results demonstrate that time-evolving entanglement can be reliably transmitted through a noisy urban free-space channel, representing an important benchmark toward long-distance free-space quantum communication and the future implementation of time-correlated entangled states in demanding scenarios such as satellite-based quantum networks.

### [167] [Rack-integrated quantum dot-based source of single and entangled photons at telecom C-band](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21454)
*Michal Vyvlecka,Raphael Joos,Benjamin Breiholz,Emma Marmasse,Anna Friederike Köhler,Ponraj Vijayan,Tobias Huber-Loyola,Sven Höfling,Michael Jetter,Simone Luca Portalupi,Peter Michler*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: For quantum light sources in everyday telecommunication networks, quantum science needs to be fully transformed into quantum technology. This can be provided using epitaxial quantum dots as deterministic sources of quantum light. Particularly intriguing is that emitters operating at telecom wavelengths are rapidly catching up with their short wavelength counterparts in terms of performances. Here, we make a decisive step forward in the development of quantum communication networks: a state-of-the-art source of quantum light, a semiconductor quantum dot (QD), with record coincidence rate for entangled photon emission in the telecom C-band, is operated inside an optimized rack-based setup. ### [168] [Flow of local sensitivity in a spin chain coupled to a bosonic bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21501)
*Marcin Płodzień*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究自旋链与耦合玻色子浴（bosonic bath）构成的完整多体量子系统中，量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）的流动，揭示耦合对称性如何决定相位敏感性的去向，以及浴谱对灵敏度是否返回自旋链的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越Lindbladian近似（Lindbladian approximation），将浴视为完整的多体量子系统，探究局部编码参数（encoded parameter）的量子Fisher信息如何在自旋链、玻色子浴及它们之间的量子关联中流动。

Method: 直接在哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）层次上分析耦合对称性（coupling symmetry）如何决定灵敏度去向；对比两种耦合类型：保持总激发数守恒的Jaynes–Cummings耦合（Jaynes–Cummings coupling）和保持自旋激发数守恒的Holstein耦合（Holstein coupling）。

Result: Holstein耦合使浴不携带关于相位（phase）的一阶信息，丢失的灵敏度全部存储在自旋–浴关联中；Jaynes–Cummings耦合则将灵敏度传递给浴，单激发下完全转移。灵敏度是否返回自旋取决于浴谱：当耦合系统的频率有公周期时完全周期性恢复，频率分散时则在不同浴模之间退相（dephase）且永不返回。

Conclusion: 转移的计量寄存器（metrological register）丢失的灵敏度超过其到达保真度（arrival fidelity）所暗示的程度。

Abstract: We study how local sensitivity to an encoded parameter, captured by the quantum Fisher information, flows between a spin chain, a coupled bosonic bath, and their quantum correlations, where we treat the bath as a full many-body quantum system beyond the Lindbladian approximation. We analyze how the coupling symmetry determines the destination of the departed sensitivity directly at the level of the Hamiltonian. We consider an excitation-exchanging Jaynes--Cummings coupling, which preserves the total number of excitations, and a spin-excitation-conserving Holstein coupling. We find that the Holstein coupling leaves the bath with no first-order information about the phase and stores the lost sensitivity entirely in spin--bath correlations, whereas the Jaynes--Cummings coupling passes this sensitivity to the bath, in full for a single excitation. The bath spectrum then governs whether the sensitivity ever returns to the spins. It revives fully and periodically when the coupled-system frequencies share a common period, but when those frequencies disperse the departed share dephases across the bath modes and never returns. We note that a transported metrological register loses more sensitivity than its arrival fidelity implies.

</details>

### [169] [A One-Dimensional Integral Equation for a Porous Horizontal Disc under Water Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.21102)
*Luiz Fernando de Moraes Campos Filho,Leandro Farina,Juliana Sartori Ziebell*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究了深水中薄型多孔圆形平板（thin, porous circular plate）对波浪的散射问题，通过转化为第二类超奇异Fredholm积分方程（hypersingular Fredholm integral equation）并利用边界元法（Boundary Element Method）数值求解，分析了孔隙参数G对水动力系数（附加质量和阻尼系数）的影响规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立并求解深水中薄型多孔圆形平板的波浪散射问题，量化孔隙参数对水动力性能的影响，以填补相关理论解析与数值研究的空白。

Method: 将问题表述为单位圆盘上的第二类超奇异Fredholm积分方程（hypersingular Fredholm integral equation of the second kind），并采用边界元法（Boundary Element Method）进行数值求解。

Result: 孔隙参数G为实数（低孔隙率）时，附加质量（added mass）与水动力增大；G为虚数（高孔隙率）时，上述效应减弱，但阻尼系数（damping coefficient）增大。

Conclusion: 所提出的数值公式得到了验证，与已有文献结果高度一致，表明该方法可有效分析多孔板的波浪散射与流体动力特性。

Abstract: Wave scattering by a thin, porous circular plate submerged in deep water is investigated. The problem is formulated as a second-kind hypersingular Fredholm integral equation over the unit disk, solved numerically using the Boundary Element Method. The analysis focuses on calculating hydrodynamic forces, specifically added mass (real part) and damping coefficient (imaginary part). Results demonstrate the influence of the porosity parameter G: less porous plates (G real) increase added mass and hydrodynamic force, while more porous plates (G imaginary) reduce these effects but increase the damping coefficient. The proposed formulation is validated, showing excellent agreement with established literature.

</details>

### [170] [Event-sparse stack denoising for 4D-STEM applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.10555)

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对四维扫描透射电子显微镜（4D-STEM）数据的去噪方法——事件稀疏堆栈去噪（event-sparse stack denoising），通过在数据采集时增加额外时间维度，形成局域时间分辨STEM（LTR-STEM）五维数据集，并采用DBSCAN结合多步持久化阈值或稀疏主成分分析（sparse PCA）结合单步阈值两种稀疏去噪流水线，显著降低了所需曝光时间（约16%）并提高了缺陷检测灵敏度（4.1倍）。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四维扫描透射电子显微镜（4D-STEM）数据采集常面临电子事件稀疏（electron event-sparse）导致的信噪比不足问题，传统方法难以在保持图像质量的同时有效降低电子剂量。为此，本文引入局部时间分辨策略与稀疏去噪流水线，以解决低曝光条件下的数据去噪与材料表征性能提升问题。

Method: 该方法在采集时记录多个电子事件稀疏的衍射图案，构建局域时间分辨STEM（LTR-STEM）五维数据集。每个扫描位置的衍射数据堆栈通过两条稀疏去噪流水线之一处理：1）基于密度的带噪声空间聚类算法（DBSCAN）结合多步持久化阈值；2）稀疏主成分分析（sparse PCA）结合单步阈值。

Result: 模拟峰值信噪比（PSNR）曲线显示，稀疏去噪后的4D-STEM数据在约16%的曝光时间下即可达到原始数据的PSNR水平。在缺陷检测任务中，去噪数据对相对径向圆盘偏移的灵敏度提升了4.1倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出的LTR-STEM技术可用于通过跟踪衍射圆盘强度变化来检查材料退化，支持临界剂量估计（critical dose estimation）和曝光选择性成像（exposure-selective imaging），为低剂量条件下的高分辨电子显微表征提供了有效方案。

Abstract: We introduce a denoising method for four-dimensional scanning transmission electron microscopy (4D-STEM) that relies on processing local, scan position-independent electron event-sparse data stacks, called event-sparse stack denoising. This method adds an extra time dimension during data collection by recording multiple electron event-sparse diffraction patterns. The resulting datasets are effectively five-dimensional, referred to as locally time-resolved STEM (LTR-STEM). Diffraction data stacks at each scan position are processed using one of two sparsity denoising pipelines: 1) the density-based spatial clustering of applications with noise (DBSCAN) algorithm followed by multi-step persistence thresholding, or 2) sparse principal component analysis (sparse PCA), followed by single-step thresholding. Both methods perform well for diffraction data denoising, as shown by simulated peak signal-to-noise ratio (PSNR) curves, denoised experimental data for virtual imaging, and application-specific denoising for defect detection. PSNR analysis indicates that sparsity-denoised 4D-STEM data reaches the same PSNR as raw data at approximately 16% of the exposure time, demonstrating comparable image quality with a lower dose. In defect detection, a 4.1x increase in sensitivity to relative radial disk shift is observed in the denoised data. Moreover, the LTR-STEM technique may be used to inspect material degradation by tracking changes in diffraction disk intensity, allowing for critical dose estimation and exposure-selective imaging.

</details>
